 namespace TQGA.Application.Accounting;

public sealed class EquityCurve
{
    private readonly List<(DateTime Time, decimal Value)> _points = new();

    public decimal Current { get; private set; }

    public IReadOnlyList<(DateTime Time, decimal Value)> Points => _points;

    public void Seed(decimal startingCapital)
    {
        Current = startingCapital;
        _points.Clear();
        _points.Add((DateTime.MinValue, startingCapital));
    }

    public void Update(DateTime time, decimal equity)
    {
        Current = equity;

        if (_points.Count > 0 && _points[^1].Time == time)
        {
            _points[^1] = (time, equity);
            return;
        }

        _points.Add((time, equity));
    }

    public void ApplyPnL(DateTime time, decimal pnl)
    {
        Current += pnl;

        if (_points.Count > 0 && _points[^1].Time == time)
        {
            _points[^1] = (time, Current);
            return;
        }

        _points.Add((time, Current));
    }
}

 using TQGA.Domain.Trading;

namespace TQGA.Application.Accounting;

public sealed class TradeLedger
{
    private readonly List _trades = new();

    public IReadOnlyList Trades => _trades.AsReadOnly();

    public void Record(Trade trade)
    {
        _trades.Add(trade);
    }

    public decimal TotalPnL =>
        _trades.Sum(t => t.RealizedPnL);

    public int TotalTrades => _trades.Count;

    public int WinCount =>
        _trades.Count(t => t.RealizedPnL > 0);

    public int LossCount =>
        _trades.Count(t => t.RealizedPnL < 0);

    // ✅ NEW — SYMBOL PnL ATTRIBUTION
    public Dictionary PnLBySymbol =>
        _trades
            .Where(t => t.IsClosed)
            .GroupBy(t => t.Symbol)
            .ToDictionary(
                g => g.Key,
                g => g.Sum(t => t.RealizedPnL));
}

 using System.Threading;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using TQGA.Application.Interfaces;
using TQGA.Application.Trading;
using TQGA.Domain.Market;

namespace TQGA.Application.Backtesting;

public sealed class BacktestRunner
{
    private readonly ICandleDataFeed _feed;
    private readonly ITradingEngine _engine;

    public BacktestRunner(ICandleDataFeed feed, ITradingEngine engine)
    {
        _feed = feed;
        _engine = engine;
    }

    public async Task RunAsync(string symbol, string timeframe, CancellationToken ct)
    {
        foreach (Candle candle in _feed.GetCandles(symbol, timeframe))
        {
            await _engine.OnTickAsync(
                symbol,
                candle.Close,
                candle.Time,
                ct);
        }
    }
}

 namespace TQGA.Application.Backtesting;

/// 
/// Immutable snapshot of per-strategy trading diagnostics,
/// copied out of the DI-scoped TradeDecisionDiagnostics service.
/// 
public sealed class TradeDecisionDiagnosticsSnapshot
{
    public int TicksProcessed { get; init; }
    public int SignalLong { get; init; }
    public int SignalShort { get; init; }
    public int SignalExit { get; init; }
    public int EntryAttempts { get; init; }
    public int ExecutedEntries { get; init; }
    public int ExecutedExits { get; init; }
}

/// 
/// Chronological train/test fold result for true walk-forward validation.
/// 
public sealed class WalkForwardFoldSnapshot
{
    public int FoldNo { get; init; }

    public DateTime TrainStartUtc { get; init; }
    public DateTime TrainEndUtc { get; init; }

    public DateTime TestStartUtc { get; init; }
    public DateTime TestEndUtc { get; init; }

    public decimal StartEquity { get; init; }
    public decimal EndEquity { get; init; }
    public decimal ReturnPct { get; init; }

    public int TestPoints { get; init; }
}

/// 
/// Lightweight strategy fitness DTO used by A84 reporting layer.
/// 
public sealed class StrategyFitnessSnapshot
{
    public int StrategyId { get; init; }
    public string StrategyCode { get; init; } = string.Empty;

    public decimal PnL { get; init; }
    public int Trades { get; init; }
    public int Exits { get; init; }

    public decimal FitnessScore { get; init; }
    public bool Allowed { get; init; }

    public string GateReason { get; init; } = string.Empty;
}

 using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;

namespace TQGA.Application.Backtesting;

public sealed class PortfolioBacktestResult
{
    public Dictionary StrategyPnL { get; set; } = new();
    public Dictionary SymbolPnL { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    public Dictionary CapitalWeights { get; set; } = new();

    public Dictionary PortfolioEquityTimeline { get; set; } = new();

    public Dictionary SymbolTimeframePnL { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    public Dictionary StrategySymbolTimeframePnL { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

    public Dictionary StrategyDiagnostics { get; set; } = new();

    public Dictionary MarketSelectionRejections { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    public List SelectedMarkets { get; set; } = new();

    public List WalkForwardFolds { get; set; } = new();

    // Runner-layer raw CIO / market allocation
    public Dictionary CioSymbolTimeframeWeights { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    public Dictionary MarketAllocationWeights { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    public decimal CashAllocationWeight { get; set; }

    // PATCH 3: canonical post-gating CIO state used by all downstream reports
    public Dictionary CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

    // PATCH 21:
    // MarketAllocationWeights is retained for compatibility, but its meaning is now explicit:
    // it is the runner candidate sleeve mix BEFORE final post-gating deployment semantics.
    public IReadOnlyDictionary RunnerCandidateAllocationWeightsView =>
        MarketAllocationWeights;

    public decimal RunnerCandidateAllocationMixSum =>
        MarketAllocationWeights?.Values.Sum() ?? 0m;

    // PATCH 21:
    // Canonical post-gating CIO dictionary is the gross deployable allocation snapshot.
    public IReadOnlyDictionary CanonicalDeployableAllocationWeightsView =>
        CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights;

    public decimal CanonicalDeployableAllocationSum =>
        CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights?.Values.Sum() ?? 0m;

    // PATCH 21:
    // Gross preserved cash paired with canonical deployable allocation.
    public decimal CanonicalPreservedCashWeight =>
        CashAllocationWeight;

    public bool HasMarketAllocationWeights =>
        MarketAllocationWeights != null &&
        MarketAllocationWeights.Count > 0;
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = =

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
using TQGA.Application.Accounting;
using TQGA.Application.Interfaces;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;
using TQGA.Application.Portfolio;
using TQGA.Application.Risk;
using TQGA.Application.Strategy;
using TQGA.Application.Trading;
using TQGA.Domain.Market;

namespace TQGA.Application.Backtesting;

public sealed class PortfolioBacktestRunner
{
    private readonly IServiceProvider _root;
    private readonly StrategyFactory _factory;
    private readonly ICandleDataFeed _feed;

    private const decimal PortfolioCapital = 100_000m;

    // WAVE B â€” institutional scarcity controls
    private const int WaveBTopNMarkets = 8;
    private const int WaveBMinMarkets = 4;
    private const int WaveBPerSymbolCap = 1;
    private const decimal WaveBMinScoreThreshold = 0.62m;
    private const decimal WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket = 0.18m;

    // PATCH 22 â€” strict dispersion / gap guard
    // Goal: when the Wave B score curve is too flat, do NOT pretend that broad candidate count = real breadth.
    private const decimal WaveBMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore = 0.90m;
    private const decimal WaveBMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore = 0.85m;
    private const int WaveBDispersionGuardMinMarkets = 1;

    // PATCH 24 â€” adaptive scarcity-only relaxed dispersion mode
    // IMPORTANT:
    // - This does NOT relax regime gate.
    // - This does NOT relax liquidity gate.
    // - This does NOT relax min score threshold.
    // - It only gives a narrow second chance to near-miss candidates when
    //   strict dispersion leaves breadth critically thin.
    private const decimal WaveBScarcityRelaxedMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore = 0.88m;
    private const decimal WaveBScarcityRelaxedMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore = 0.82m;
    private const int WaveBScarcityRelaxedTargetMinMarkets = 3;

    public PortfolioBacktestRunner(
        IServiceProvider root,
        StrategyFactory factory,
        ICandleDataFeed feed)
    {
        _root = root;
        _factory = factory;
        _feed = feed;
    }

    public Task RunAsync(
        IEnumerable strategyTypes,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        return RunAsync(
            strategyTypes,
            BinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols,
            BinanceUniverse.Timeframes,
            FrictionProfile.Default,
            ct);
    }

    public Task RunAsync(
        IEnumerable strategyTypes,
        IReadOnlyList selectedTimeframes,
        FrictionProfile friction,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        return RunAsync(
            strategyTypes,
            BinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols,
            selectedTimeframes,
            friction,
            ct);
    }

    public async Task RunAsync(
        IEnumerable strategyTypes,
        IReadOnlyList selectedSymbols,
        IReadOnlyList selectedTimeframes,
        FrictionProfile friction,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(strategyTypes);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedSymbols);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedTimeframes);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(friction);

        var types = strategyTypes.ToList();
        if (types.Count == 0)
            throw new InvalidOperationException("No strategies registered.");

        var activeSymbols = selectedSymbols.Count == 0
            ? BinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols.ToList()
            : selectedSymbols
                .Where(x => BinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols.Contains(x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                .ToList();

        if (activeSymbols.Count == 0)
            throw new InvalidOperationException("No valid symbols selected.");

        var activeTimeframes = selectedTimeframes.Count == 0
            ? BinanceUniverse.Timeframes.ToList()
            : selectedTimeframes
                .Where(x => BinanceUniverse.Timeframes.Contains(x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                .ToList();

        if (activeTimeframes.Count == 0)
            throw new InvalidOperationException("No valid timeframes selected.");

        var selection = new PreTradeMarketSelectionService()
            .SelectMarkets(
                _feed,
                activeSymbols,
                activeTimeframes,
                topN: 12);

        var rankedSelectedMarkets = selection.SelectedMarkets.ToList();

        if (rankedSelectedMarkets.Count == 0)
            throw new InvalidOperationException("No markets passed pre-trade selection.");

        var combinedRejections = new Dictionary(
            selection.RejectedMarkets,
            StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        var waveBSelection = ApplyWaveBSelection(rankedSelectedMarkets, combinedRejections);
        var selectedMarkets = waveBSelection.SelectedMarkets;

        if (selectedMarkets.Count == 0)
            throw new InvalidOperationException("No markets passed Wave B signal ranking and Top-N execution.");

        var marketAllocationWeights = waveBSelection.AllocationWeights;
        var unallocatedCashWeight = waveBSelection.CashWeight;

        WriteWaveBDiagnosticReport(
            selection,
            waveBSelection,
            combinedRejections,
            unallocatedCashWeight);

        var leadershipRank = new Dictionary();
        for (int i = 0; i < selectedMarkets.Count; i++)
            leadershipRank[selectedMarkets[i]] = i + 1;

        var riskBudget = new PortfolioRiskBudgetEngine();

        var rawNetPnlByMarket = selectedMarkets.ToDictionary(m => m, _ => 0m);
        var tradeCountByMarket = selectedMarkets.ToDictionary(m => m, _ => 0);
        var positiveStrategyHitsByMarket = selectedMarkets.ToDictionary(m => m, _ => 0);
        var strategyParticipationByMarket = selectedMarkets.ToDictionary(m => m, _ => 0);

        var nodes = new List();
        var capitalWeights = new Dictionary();

        // ECONOMIC TRUTH LAYER
        var symbolTfPnL = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var strategySymbolTfPnL = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var strategyDiagnostics = new Dictionary();
        var adjustedPnlTimeline = new SortedDictionary();

        // Institutional trust-weighted capital map
        var trustWeightsByType = BuildStrategyTrustWeights(types);

        int id = 1;

        foreach (var type in types)
        {
            using var scope = _root.CreateScope();

            var strategy = _factory.Create(type);

            var engine = ActivatorUtilities.CreateInstance(
                scope.ServiceProvider,
                strategy);

            var ledger = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService();
            var equity = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService();
            var capital = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService();
            var diag = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService();

            decimal strategyWeight = trustWeightsByType.TryGetValue(type, out var resolvedWeight)
                ? resolvedWeight
                : 0m;

            capital.Seed(PortfolioCapital, strategyWeight);

            decimal allocatedCapital = PortfolioCapital * strategyWeight;
            equity.Seed(allocatedCapital);

            capitalWeights[id] = strategyWeight;

            if (strategyWeight <= 0m)
            {
                strategyDiagnostics[id] = new TradeDecisionDiagnosticsSnapshot
                {
                    TicksProcessed = 0,
                    SignalLong = 0,
                    SignalShort = 0,
                    SignalExit = 0,
                    EntryAttempts = 0,
                    ExecutedEntries = 0,
                    ExecutedExits = 0
                };

                nodes.Add(new StrategyBacktestNode(
                    id,
                    strategy.Name,
                    ledger,
                    equity));

                id++;
                continue;
            }

            var openRiskBySymbol = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
            var openRiskByCluster = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
            decimal totalOpenRiskPct = 0m;
            decimal peakEquity = allocatedCapital;

            foreach (var m in selectedMarkets)
            {
                var marketWeight = marketAllocationWeights.TryGetValue(m, out var resolvedMarketWeight)
                    ? resolvedMarketWeight
                    : 0m;

                if (marketWeight <= 0m)
                    continue;

                var candles = _feed.GetCandles(m.Symbol, m.Timeframe)
                    .OrderBy(c => c.Time)
                    .ToList();

                if (candles.Count < 120)
                    continue;

                var currentEquity = System.Math.Max(1m, allocatedCapital + ledger.TotalPnL);
                peakEquity = System.Math.Max(peakEquity, currentEquity);

                var drawdownPct = peakEquity <= 0m
                    ? 0m
                    : ((peakEquity - currentEquity) / peakEquity) * 100m;

                var budget = riskBudget.Evaluate(
                    m.Symbol,
                    m.Timeframe,
                    candles,
                    currentEquity,
                    drawdownPct,
                    openRiskBySymbol,
                    openRiskByCluster,
                    totalOpenRiskPct);

                if (!budget.IsAllowed)
                    continue;

                openRiskBySymbol[m.Symbol] =
                    (openRiskBySymbol.TryGetValue(m.Symbol, out var sRisk) ? sRisk : 0m)
                    + budget.AllowedRiskPct;

                var cluster = budget.Cluster;
                openRiskByCluster[cluster] =
                    (openRiskByCluster.TryGetValue(cluster, out var cRisk) ? cRisk : 0m)
                    + budget.AllowedRiskPct;

                totalOpenRiskPct += budget.AllowedRiskPct;

                var beforePnl = GetSymbolPnL(ledger, m.Symbol);
                var beforeTradeCount = GetTradeCount(ledger);

                foreach (var candle in candles)
                {
                    await engine.OnTickAsync(
                        m.Symbol,
                        candle.Close,
                        candle.Time,
                        ct);
                }

                var afterPnl = GetSymbolPnL(ledger, m.Symbol);
                var afterTradeCount = GetTradeCount(ledger);
                var newlyClosedTrades = ledger.Trades
                    .Skip(beforeTradeCount)
                    .Where(t => t.IsClosed)
                    .ToList();

                var grossDelta = afterPnl - beforePnl;
                var marketTradeCount = System.Math.Max(0, afterTradeCount - beforeTradeCount);

                var budgetScale = budget.AllowedRiskPct <= 0m
                    ? 0m
                    : budget.AllowedRiskPct / 0.50m;

                var effectiveScale = budgetScale * marketWeight;
                var scaledGrossDelta = grossDelta * effectiveScale;

                var frictionCost = EstimateFrictionCost(
                    budget.PositionValue * marketWeight,
                    marketTradeCount,
                    friction,
                    candles);

                var netDelta = scaledGrossDelta - frictionCost;

                AllocateNetDeltaAcrossClosedTrades(
                    newlyClosedTrades,
                    netDelta,
                    candles[^1].Time,
                    adjustedPnlTimeline);

                var keyTf = $"{m.Symbol}::{m.Timeframe}";
                if (symbolTfPnL.ContainsKey(keyTf))
                    symbolTfPnL[keyTf] += netDelta;
                else
                    symbolTfPnL[keyTf] = netDelta;

                var keyStrTf = $"S{id:00}::{m.Symbol}::{m.Timeframe}";
                if (strategySymbolTfPnL.ContainsKey(keyStrTf))
                    strategySymbolTfPnL[keyStrTf] += netDelta;
                else
                    strategySymbolTfPnL[keyStrTf] = netDelta;

                rawNetPnlByMarket[m] += netDelta;
                tradeCountByMarket[m] += marketTradeCount;
                strategyParticipationByMarket[m] += 1;

                if (netDelta > 0m)
                    positiveStrategyHitsByMarket[m] += 1;

                openRiskBySymbol[m.Symbol] = System.Math.Max(0m, openRiskBySymbol[m.Symbol] - budget.AllowedRiskPct);
                openRiskByCluster[cluster] = System.Math.Max(0m, openRiskByCluster[cluster] - budget.AllowedRiskPct);
                totalOpenRiskPct = System.Math.Max(0m, totalOpenRiskPct - budget.AllowedRiskPct);
            }

            strategyDiagnostics[id] = new TradeDecisionDiagnosticsSnapshot
            {
                TicksProcessed = diag.TicksProcessed,
                SignalLong = diag.SignalLong,
                SignalShort = diag.SignalShort,
                SignalExit = diag.SignalExit,
                EntryAttempts = diag.EntryAttempts,
                ExecutedEntries = diag.ExecutedEntries,
                ExecutedExits = diag.ExecutedExits
            };

            nodes.Add(new StrategyBacktestNode(
                id,
                strategy.Name,
                ledger,
                equity));

            id++;
        }

        var compositeMarketScore = BuildCompositeMarketScores(
            selectedMarkets,
            rawNetPnlByMarket,
            tradeCountByMarket,
            positiveStrategyHitsByMarket,
            strategyParticipationByMarket,
            leadershipRank);

        var cio = new CioDynamicReallocationEngine(
            topK: 6,
            minWeight: 0.00m,
            maxWeight: 0.35m,
            maxWeightPerSymbol: 0.45m);

        var cioWeights = cio.ComputeWeights(compositeMarketScore);

        var adjustedSymbolPnL = AggregateAdjustedSymbolPnL(symbolTfPnL);
        var adjustedStrategyPnL = AggregateAdjustedStrategyPnL(strategySymbolTfPnL);

        var baseResult = BuildResult(
            nodes,
            capitalWeights,
            adjustedSymbolPnL,
            adjustedStrategyPnL,
            adjustedPnlTimeline);

        var walkForwardFolds = await RunTrueWalkForwardAsync(
            types,
            selectedMarkets,
            friction,
            trustWeightsByType,
            ct);

        var result = new PortfolioBacktestResult
        {
            StrategyPnL = baseResult.StrategyPnL,
            SymbolPnL = baseResult.SymbolPnL,
            CapitalWeights = baseResult.CapitalWeights,
            PortfolioEquityTimeline = baseResult.PortfolioEquityTimeline,
            SymbolTimeframePnL = symbolTfPnL,
            StrategySymbolTimeframePnL = strategySymbolTfPnL,
            StrategyDiagnostics = strategyDiagnostics,
            MarketSelectionRejections = combinedRejections,
            SelectedMarkets = selectedMarkets.Select(x => $"{x.Symbol}::{x.Timeframe}").ToList(),
            WalkForwardFolds = walkForwardFolds,
            CioSymbolTimeframeWeights = new Dictionary(
                cioWeights.ToDictionary(
                    w => $"CIO::{w.Key.Symbol}::{w.Key.Timeframe}",
                    w => w.Value),
                StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase),

            MarketAllocationWeights = new Dictionary(
                marketAllocationWeights.ToDictionary(
                    x => $"{x.Key.Symbol}::{x.Key.Timeframe}",
                    x => x.Value),
                StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase),

            CashAllocationWeight = unallocatedCashWeight
        };

        return result;
    }

    private Dictionary BuildStrategyTrustWeights(
        IReadOnlyList strategyTypes)
    {
        var raw = new Dictionary();

        foreach (var type in strategyTypes)
        {
            var strategy = _factory.Create(type);

            decimal trust = EstimateStrategyTrustScore(type, strategy.Name);
            raw[type] = System.Math.Max(0m, trust);
        }

        decimal totalPositive = raw.Values.Where(x => x > 0m).Sum();

        if (totalPositive <= 0m)
        {
            decimal equal = strategyTypes.Count == 0
                ? 0m
                : 1m / strategyTypes.Count;

            return strategyTypes.ToDictionary(x => x, _ => equal);
        }

        return raw.ToDictionary(
            kv => kv.Key,
            kv => kv.Value <= 0m ? 0m : kv.Value / totalPositive);
    }

    private static decimal EstimateStrategyTrustScore(Type type, string strategyName)
    {
        decimal prior = GetStrategyTrustPrior(type, strategyName);

        // Small structural shaping only.
        // These are intentionally weak so the prior ranking remains the main driver.
        string typeName = type.Name;
        string name = strategyName ?? string.Empty;

        decimal structuralAdjustment = 0m;

        if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "Trend"))
            structuralAdjustment += 0.03m;

        if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "Pullback"))
            structuralAdjustment -= 0.01m;

        if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "Rsi"))
            structuralAdjustment -= 0.01m;

        return System.Math.Max(0m, prior + structuralAdjustment);
    }

    private static decimal GetStrategyTrustPrior(Type type, string strategyName)
    {
        string typeName = type.Name;
        string name = strategyName ?? string.Empty;

        // REPORT 31 AFTER BASIS FIX:
        // S05 strongest positive contributor
        if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "EmaTrendQuantStrategy"))
            return 1.00m;

        // NEW FAMILY:
        // Controlled exploratory prior for the new 4h early-trend continuation sleeve.
        // Higher than unknown-future fallback so it can be meaningfully tested,
        // but still clearly below the proven S05 core sleeve.
        if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "FourHourEarlyTrendContinuation"))
            return 0.24m;

        // S06 still negative, but materially better than S03
        if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "RsiSwing"))
            return 0.30m;

        // S04 exploratory / weak negative
        if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "EmaTrendPullback"))
            return 0.18m;

        // S03 worst contributor after reconciliation fix
        if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "EmaRsiQuantStrategy"))
            return 0.03m;

        // Keep quarantined
        if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "AltcoinLeadershipPullback"))
            return 0.00m;

        if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "Diagnostic"))
            return 0.00m;

        // Tiny exploratory allocation for unknown future strategies
        return 0.08m;
    }

    private static bool ContainsAny(string typeName, string strategyName, string token)
    {
        return typeName.Contains(token, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            || strategyName.Contains(token, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    }

    private static WaveBSelectionSnapshot ApplyWaveBSelection(
        IReadOnlyList rankedSelectedMarkets,
        Dictionary combinedRejections)
    {
        var candidates = new List();

        if (rankedSelectedMarkets.Count == 0)
            return new WaveBSelectionSnapshot();

        decimal maxBaseScore = rankedSelectedMarkets
            .Select(x => SafeDecimal(x.Score))
            .DefaultIfEmpty(0m)
            .Max();

        if (maxBaseScore <= 0m)
            maxBaseScore = 1m;

        for (int i = 0; i < rankedSelectedMarkets.Count; i++)
        {
            var item = rankedSelectedMarkets[i];
            MarketKey market = item.Market;
            decimal baseScore = SafeDecimal(item.Score);

            decimal normalizedPreTradeScore = baseScore <= 0m
                ? 0m
                : baseScore / maxBaseScore;

            decimal timeframePreferenceScore = market.Timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                ? 1.00m
                : market.Timeframe.Equals("1d", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                    ? 0.80m
                    : 0.55m;

            decimal liquidityScore = GetLiquidityScore(market.Symbol);

            decimal leadershipScore = rankedSelectedMarkets.Count == 1
                ? 1.00m
                : 1.00m - (((decimal)i / (rankedSelectedMarkets.Count - 1)) * 0.25m);

            decimal finalScore =
                (normalizedPreTradeScore * 0.60m) +
                (timeframePreferenceScore * 0.25m) +
                (liquidityScore * 0.15m);

            finalScore *= leadershipScore;

            candidates.Add(new WaveBCandidate
            {
                Market = market,
                BasePreTradeScore = baseScore,
                NormalizedPreTradeScore = normalizedPreTradeScore,
                TimeframePreferenceScore = timeframePreferenceScore,
                LiquidityScore = liquidityScore,
                LeadershipScore = leadershipScore,
                FinalScore = finalScore,
                RelativeToLeaderFinalScore = 0m,
                RelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore = 0m,
                PassesDispersionGuard = false,
                PassesRelaxedDispersionGuard = false,
                SelectedByScarcityRelaxedDispersion = false
            });
        }

        var ranked = candidates
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.FinalScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.NormalizedPreTradeScore)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Market.Symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Market.Timeframe, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        decimal leaderFinalScore = ranked.Count == 0
            ? 0m
            : ranked[0].FinalScore;

        decimal leaderPreTradeScore = ranked.Count == 0
            ? 0m
            : ranked[0].NormalizedPreTradeScore;

        if (leaderFinalScore <= 0m)
            leaderFinalScore = 1m;

        if (leaderPreTradeScore <= 0m)
            leaderPreTradeScore = 1m;

        for (int i = 0; i < ranked.Count; i++)
        {
            var candidate = ranked[i];

            if (i == 0)
            {
                candidate.RelativeToLeaderFinalScore = 1.00m;
                candidate.RelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore = 1.00m;
                candidate.PassesDispersionGuard = true;
                candidate.PassesRelaxedDispersionGuard = true;
                continue;
            }

            candidate.RelativeToLeaderFinalScore = candidate.FinalScore / leaderFinalScore;
            candidate.RelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore = candidate.NormalizedPreTradeScore / leaderPreTradeScore;

            candidate.PassesDispersionGuard =
                candidate.RelativeToLeaderFinalScore >= WaveBMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore &&
                candidate.RelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore >= WaveBMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore;

            candidate.PassesRelaxedDispersionGuard =
                candidate.RelativeToLeaderFinalScore >= WaveBScarcityRelaxedMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore &&
                candidate.RelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore >= WaveBScarcityRelaxedMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore;
        }

        int viableAfterThresholdCount = ranked.Count(x => x.FinalScore >= WaveBMinScoreThreshold);

        int strictDispersionPassCount = ranked.Count(x =>
            x.FinalScore >= WaveBMinScoreThreshold &&
            x.PassesDispersionGuard);

        int relaxedDispersionPassCount = ranked.Count(x =>
            x.FinalScore >= WaveBMinScoreThreshold &&
            x.PassesRelaxedDispersionGuard);

        bool scarcityDispersionModeActive =
            strictDispersionPassCount < WaveBScarcityRelaxedTargetMinMarkets &&
            relaxedDispersionPassCount > strictDispersionPassCount;

        var selectedCandidates = new List();
        var selectedPerSymbol = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        bool dispersionGuardTriggered = false;
        int scarcityRelaxedDispersionRescueCount = 0;

        foreach (var candidate in ranked)
        {
            string marketKey = $"{candidate.Market.Symbol}::{candidate.Market.Timeframe}";
            bool selectedByScarcityRelaxedDispersion = false;

            if (!candidate.PassesDispersionGuard)
            {
                if (scarcityDispersionModeActive && candidate.PassesRelaxedDispersionGuard)
                {
                    selectedByScarcityRelaxedDispersion = true;
                    candidate.SelectedByScarcityRelaxedDispersion = true;
                }
                else
                {
                    combinedRejections[marketKey] =
                        $"WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard(relFinal={candidate.RelativeToLeaderFinalScore:F4},minFinal={WaveBMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore:F2},relPre={candidate.RelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore:F4},minPre={WaveBMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore:F2})";
                    dispersionGuardTriggered = true;
                    continue;
                }
            }

            if (candidate.FinalScore < WaveBMinScoreThreshold)
            {
                combinedRejections[marketKey] =
                    $"WaveBRejected:BelowThreshold(score={candidate.FinalScore:F4},min={WaveBMinScoreThreshold:F2})";
                continue;
            }

            int currentSymbolCount = selectedPerSymbol.TryGetValue(candidate.Market.Symbol, out int existingCount)
                ? existingCount
                : 0;

            if (currentSymbolCount >= WaveBPerSymbolCap)
            {
                combinedRejections[marketKey] =
                    $"WaveBRejected:PerSymbolCap(symbol={candidate.Market.Symbol},cap={WaveBPerSymbolCap})";
                continue;
            }

            if (selectedCandidates.Count >= WaveBTopNMarkets)
            {
                combinedRejections[marketKey] =
                    $"WaveBRejected:TopNOverflow(topN={WaveBTopNMarkets})";
                continue;
            }

            selectedCandidates.Add(candidate);
            selectedPerSymbol[candidate.Market.Symbol] = currentSymbolCount + 1;

            if (selectedByScarcityRelaxedDispersion)
                scarcityRelaxedDispersionRescueCount++;

            if (combinedRejections.ContainsKey(marketKey) &&
                combinedRejections[marketKey].StartsWith("WaveBRejected:", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                combinedRejections.Remove(marketKey);
            }
        }

        int effectiveMinMarkets = dispersionGuardTriggered
            ? WaveBDispersionGuardMinMarkets
            : WaveBMinMarkets;

        // PATCH 22 / PATCH 24:
        // Only backfill when strict dispersion guard did NOT trigger.
        // If scarcity mode is active, we still keep honesty and do not force-fill
        // beyond organically surviving names.
        if (!dispersionGuardTriggered && !scarcityDispersionModeActive && selectedCandidates.Count < effectiveMinMarkets)
        {
            foreach (var candidate in ranked)
            {
                if (selectedCandidates.Count >= effectiveMinMarkets)
                    break;

                if (selectedCandidates.Any(x =>
                        x.Market.Symbol.Equals(candidate.Market.Symbol, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) &&
                        x.Market.Timeframe.Equals(candidate.Market.Timeframe, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)))
                    continue;

                if (!candidate.PassesDispersionGuard)
                    continue;

                if (candidate.FinalScore < WaveBMinScoreThreshold)
                    continue;

                int currentSymbolCount = selectedPerSymbol.TryGetValue(candidate.Market.Symbol, out int existingCount)
                    ? existingCount
                    : 0;

                if (currentSymbolCount >= WaveBPerSymbolCap)
                    continue;

                string marketKey = $"{candidate.Market.Symbol}::{candidate.Market.Timeframe}";

                selectedCandidates.Add(candidate);
                selectedPerSymbol[candidate.Market.Symbol] = currentSymbolCount + 1;

                if (combinedRejections.ContainsKey(marketKey) &&
                    combinedRejections[marketKey].StartsWith("WaveBRejected:", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                {
                    combinedRejections.Remove(marketKey);
                }
            }
        }

        var allocationWeights = BuildAllocationWeights(selectedCandidates);
        var cashWeight = System.Math.Max(0m, 1m - allocationWeights.Values.Sum());

        return new WaveBSelectionSnapshot
        {
            RankedCandidates = ranked,
            SelectedMarkets = selectedCandidates.Select(x => x.Market).ToList(),
            AllocationWeights = allocationWeights,
            CashWeight = cashWeight,
            SelectedPerSymbolCounts = new Dictionary(selectedPerSymbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase),
            DispersionGuardTriggered = dispersionGuardTriggered,
            EffectiveMinMarkets = effectiveMinMarkets,
            LeaderFinalScore = ranked.Count == 0 ? 0m : ranked[0].FinalScore,
            LeaderBasePreTradeScore = ranked.Count == 0 ? 0m : ranked[0].BasePreTradeScore,

            ViableAfterThresholdCount = viableAfterThresholdCount,
            StrictDispersionPassCount = strictDispersionPassCount,
            RelaxedDispersionPassCount = relaxedDispersionPassCount,
            ScarcityDispersionModeActive = scarcityDispersionModeActive,
            ScarcityRelaxedDispersionRescueCount = scarcityRelaxedDispersionRescueCount,
            EffectiveMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore = scarcityDispersionModeActive
                ? WaveBScarcityRelaxedMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore
                : WaveBMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore,
            EffectiveMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore = scarcityDispersionModeActive
                ? WaveBScarcityRelaxedMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore
                : WaveBMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore
        };
    }

    private static void WriteWaveBDiagnosticReport(
        dynamic preTradeSelection,
        WaveBSelectionSnapshot waveBSelection,
        IReadOnlyDictionary combinedRejections,
        decimal unallocatedCashWeight)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var sb = new System.Text.StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 18 â€” WAVE B DIAGNOSTIC");
        sb.AppendLine("============================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PUBLISH PATH SIGNATURE");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("PATCH_24_WAVE_B_TELEMETRY_AND_ADAPTIVE_SCARCITY_DISPERSION");
        sb.AppendLine("SOURCE = PortfolioBacktestRunner.ApplyWaveBSelection");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("CONFIGURATION");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"WaveBTopNMarkets                    : {WaveBTopNMarkets}");
        sb.AppendLine($"WaveBMinMarkets                     : {WaveBMinMarkets}");
        sb.AppendLine($"WaveBPerSymbolCap                   : {WaveBPerSymbolCap}");
        sb.AppendLine($"WaveBMinScoreThreshold              : {WaveBMinScoreThreshold:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket             : {WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"WaveBStrictMinRelLeaderFinal        : {WaveBMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"WaveBStrictMinRelLeaderPre          : {WaveBMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"WaveBRelaxedMinRelLeaderFinal       : {WaveBScarcityRelaxedMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"WaveBRelaxedMinRelLeaderPre         : {WaveBScarcityRelaxedMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"WaveBGuardMinMarkets                : {WaveBDispersionGuardMinMarkets}");
        sb.AppendLine($"WaveBScarcityRelaxedTargetMinMkts   : {WaveBScarcityRelaxedTargetMinMarkets}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("FUNNEL TELEMETRY");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------");
        int preTradeCount = 0;
        try
        {
            preTradeCount = ((IEnumerable)preTradeSelection.SelectedMarkets).Count();
        }
        catch
        {
            preTradeCount = 0;
        }

        sb.AppendLine($"PreTrade Ranked Count               : {preTradeCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Wave B Candidate Count              : {waveBSelection.RankedCandidates.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Viable After Score Threshold        : {waveBSelection.ViableAfterThresholdCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Strict Dispersion Pass Count        : {waveBSelection.StrictDispersionPassCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Relaxed Dispersion Pass Count       : {waveBSelection.RelaxedDispersionPassCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Selected Final Count                : {waveBSelection.SelectedMarkets.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Scarcity Dispersion Mode Active     : {(waveBSelection.ScarcityDispersionModeActive ? "YES" : "NO")}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Scarcity Relaxed Rescues            : {waveBSelection.ScarcityRelaxedDispersionRescueCount}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("DISPERSION GUARD STATE");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Dispersion Guard Triggered          : {(waveBSelection.DispersionGuardTriggered ? "YES" : "NO")}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Effective Min Markets               : {waveBSelection.EffectiveMinMarkets}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Leader Base PreTrade Score          : {waveBSelection.LeaderBasePreTradeScore:F6}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Leader Final Score                  : {waveBSelection.LeaderFinalScore:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Effective Min Rel Final             : {waveBSelection.EffectiveMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Effective Min Rel Pre               : {waveBSelection.EffectiveMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("PRE-TRADE RANKED MARKETS");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------");
        try
        {
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var item in preTradeSelection.SelectedMarkets)
            {
                MarketKey market = item.Market;
                decimal score = SafeDecimal(item.Score);
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,2}. {market.Symbol}::{market.Timeframe,-4} rawPreTradeScore={score,12:F6}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        catch
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: Could not enumerate pre-trade ranked markets.");
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("WAVE B RANKED CANDIDATES");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------");
        if (waveBSelection.RankedCandidates.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: No Wave B candidates were created.");
        }
        else
        {
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var c in waveBSelection.RankedCandidates)
            {
                string marketKey = $"{c.Market.Symbol}::{c.Market.Timeframe}";

                string selectionState =
                    waveBSelection.AllocationWeights.ContainsKey(c.Market)
                        ? (c.SelectedByScarcityRelaxedDispersion
                            ? "SELECTED:SCARCITY_RELAXED_DISPERSION"
                            : "SELECTED")
                        : combinedRejections.TryGetValue(marketKey, out var reason)
                            ? reason
                            : "NOT_SELECTED";

                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{rank,2}. {marketKey,-16} " +
                    $"base={c.BasePreTradeScore,10:F6} " +
                    $"norm={c.NormalizedPreTradeScore,8:F4} " +
                    $"tf={c.TimeframePreferenceScore,6:F2} " +
                    $"liq={c.LiquidityScore,6:F2} " +
                    $"lead={c.LeadershipScore,6:F2} " +
                    $"final={c.FinalScore,8:F4} " +
                    $"relFinal={c.RelativeToLeaderFinalScore,8:F4} " +
                    $"relPre={c.RelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore,8:F4} " +
                    $"strict={(c.PassesDispersionGuard ? "PASS" : "BLOCK"),6} " +
                    $"relaxed={(c.PassesRelaxedDispersionGuard ? "PASS" : "BLOCK"),6} " +
                    $"rescued={(c.SelectedByScarcityRelaxedDispersion ? "YES" : "NO "),4} => {selectionState}");

                rank++;
            }
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("TOP NEAR MISS REJECTIONS");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------");
        var nearMisses = waveBSelection.RankedCandidates
            .Where(c => !waveBSelection.AllocationWeights.ContainsKey(c.Market))
            .OrderByDescending(c => c.FinalScore)
            .ThenByDescending(c => c.NormalizedPreTradeScore)
            .Take(12)
            .ToList();

        if (nearMisses.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO NEAR MISS REJECTIONS.");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var c in nearMisses)
            {
                string marketKey = $"{c.Market.Symbol}::{c.Market.Timeframe}";
                string reason = combinedRejections.TryGetValue(marketKey, out var r) ? r : "NOT_SELECTED";

                decimal scoreGap = System.Math.Max(0m, WaveBMinScoreThreshold - c.FinalScore);
                decimal strictFinalGap = System.Math.Max(0m, WaveBMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore - c.RelativeToLeaderFinalScore);
                decimal strictPreGap = System.Math.Max(0m, WaveBMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore - c.RelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore);
                decimal relaxedFinalGap = System.Math.Max(0m, WaveBScarcityRelaxedMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore - c.RelativeToLeaderFinalScore);
                decimal relaxedPreGap = System.Math.Max(0m, WaveBScarcityRelaxedMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore - c.RelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore);

                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{marketKey,-18} " +
                    $"final={c.FinalScore,8:F4} " +
                    $"scoreGap={scoreGap,7:F4} " +
                    $"strictGapFinal={strictFinalGap,7:F4} " +
                    $"strictGapPre={strictPreGap,7:F4} " +
                    $"relaxedGapFinal={relaxedFinalGap,7:F4} " +
                    $"relaxedGapPre={relaxedPreGap,7:F4}  => {reason}");
            }
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("REJECTION BUCKET COUNTS");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------");
        if (combinedRejections == null || combinedRejections.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO REJECTIONS RECORDED.");
        }
        else
        {
            var buckets = combinedRejections
                .GroupBy(kv =>
                {
                    string value = kv.Value ?? string.Empty;

                    if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                        return "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard";

                    if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:BelowThreshold", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                        return "WaveBRejected:BelowThreshold";

                    if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:PerSymbolCap", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                        return "WaveBRejected:PerSymbolCap";

                    if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:TopNOverflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                        return "WaveBRejected:TopNOverflow";

                    return value;
                })
                .OrderByDescending(g => g.Count())
                .ThenBy(g => g.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

            foreach (var bucket in buckets)
                sb.AppendLine($"{bucket.Key,-36} {bucket.Count(),6}");
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("SELECTED TOP-N MARKETS");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        if (waveBSelection.SelectedMarkets.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO MARKETS SELECTED.");
        }
        else
        {
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var market in waveBSelection.SelectedMarkets)
            {
                decimal weight = waveBSelection.AllocationWeights.TryGetValue(market, out var w) ? w : 0m;
                var candidate = waveBSelection.RankedCandidates.FirstOrDefault(x =>
                    x.Market.Symbol.Equals(market.Symbol, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) &&
                    x.Market.Timeframe.Equals(market.Timeframe, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

                string source = candidate != null && candidate.SelectedByScarcityRelaxedDispersion
                    ? "SCARCITY_RELAXED_DISPERSION"
                    : "STRICT";

                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,2}. {market.Symbol}::{market.Timeframe,-4} finalWeight={weight:P2} source={source}");
                rank++;
            }
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PER-SYMBOL CAP EFFECTS");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        if (waveBSelection.SelectedPerSymbolCounts.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO PER-SYMBOL SELECTION COUNTS.");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var kv in waveBSelection.SelectedPerSymbolCounts.OrderBy(x => x.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                int rejectedByCap = combinedRejections.Count(x =>
                    x.Key.StartsWith(kv.Key + "::", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) &&
                    x.Value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:PerSymbolCap", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-10} selected={kv.Value}  cap={WaveBPerSymbolCap}  rejectedByCap={rejectedByCap}");
            }
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("FINAL ALLOCATION WEIGHTS");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------");
        if (waveBSelection.AllocationWeights.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO FINAL ALLOCATION WEIGHTS.");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var kv in waveBSelection.AllocationWeights.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key.Symbol}::{kv.Key.Timeframe,-4} {kv.Value:P2}");
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("UNALLOCATED CASH");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Cash Left Unallocated: {unallocatedCashWeight:P2}");

        var path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_18_WAVE_B_DIAGNOSTIC_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static Dictionary BuildAllocationWeights(
        IReadOnlyList selectedCandidates)
    {
        var output = new Dictionary();

        if (selectedCandidates.Count == 0)
            return output;

        decimal minScore = selectedCandidates.Min(x => x.FinalScore);
        var shifted = selectedCandidates
            .Select(x => new
            {
                x.Market,
                Weight = System.Math.Max(0.000001m, x.FinalScore - minScore + 0.000001m)
            })
            .ToList();

        decimal shiftedTotal = shifted.Sum(x => x.Weight);
        if (shiftedTotal <= 0m)
            return output;

        var provisional = shifted.ToDictionary(
            x => x.Market,
            x => x.Weight / shiftedTotal);

        var capped = new Dictionary();
        decimal overflow = 0m;

        foreach (var kv in provisional)
        {
            if (kv.Value > WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket)
            {
                capped[kv.Key] = WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket;
                overflow += kv.Value - WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket;
            }
            else
            {
                capped[kv.Key] = kv.Value;
            }
        }

        int redistributionGuard = 0;
        while (overflow > 0.0000001m && redistributionGuard < 20)
        {
            redistributionGuard++;

            var underCap = capped
                .Where(x => x.Value < WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket)
                .ToList();

            if (underCap.Count == 0)
                break;

            decimal underCapTotal = underCap.Sum(x => x.Value);
            if (underCapTotal <= 0m)
                break;

            decimal distributedThisRound = 0m;

            foreach (var kv in underCap)
            {
                decimal room = WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket - kv.Value;
                if (room <= 0m)
                    continue;

                decimal add = overflow * (kv.Value / underCapTotal);
                if (add > room)
                    add = room;

                capped[kv.Key] += add;
                distributedThisRound += add;
            }

            if (distributedThisRound <= 0m)
                break;

            overflow -= distributedThisRound;
        }

        return capped;
    }

    private static decimal GetLiquidityScore(string symbol)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(symbol))
            return 0.50m;

        if (symbol.StartsWith("BTC", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return 1.00m;

        if (symbol.StartsWith("ETH", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return 0.95m;

        if (symbol.StartsWith("SOL", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return 0.90m;

        if (symbol.StartsWith("BNB", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return 0.88m;

        if (symbol.StartsWith("XRP", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return 0.85m;

        if (symbol.StartsWith("ADA", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return 0.82m;

        if (symbol.StartsWith("DOGE", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return 0.80m;

        return 0.70m;
    }

    private static decimal SafeDecimal(dynamic value)
    {
        try
        {
            if (value is null)
                return 0m;

            return Convert.ToDecimal(value);
        }
        catch
        {
            return 0m;
        }
    }

    private static Dictionary BuildCompositeMarketScores(
        IReadOnlyList selectedMarkets,
        IReadOnlyDictionary rawNetPnlByMarket,
        IReadOnlyDictionary tradeCountByMarket,
        IReadOnlyDictionary positiveStrategyHitsByMarket,
        IReadOnlyDictionary strategyParticipationByMarket,
        IReadOnlyDictionary leadershipRank)
    {
        var scores = new Dictionary();

        decimal maxAbsPnl = rawNetPnlByMarket.Count == 0
            ? 1m
            : rawNetPnlByMarket.Values.Select(x => System.Math.Abs(x)).DefaultIfEmpty(1m).Max();

        if (maxAbsPnl <= 0m)
            maxAbsPnl = 1m;

        int maxTrades = tradeCountByMarket.Count == 0
            ? 1
            : tradeCountByMarket.Values.DefaultIfEmpty(1).Max();

        if (maxTrades <= 0)
            maxTrades = 1;

        foreach (var m in selectedMarkets)
        {
            decimal pnl = rawNetPnlByMarket.TryGetValue(m, out var resolvedPnl)
                ? resolvedPnl
                : 0m;

            int trades = tradeCountByMarket.TryGetValue(m, out var resolvedTrades)
                ? resolvedTrades
                : 0;

            int positiveHits = positiveStrategyHitsByMarket.TryGetValue(m, out var resolvedPositiveHits)
                ? resolvedPositiveHits
                : 0;

            int participants = strategyParticipationByMarket.TryGetValue(m, out var resolvedParticipants)
                ? resolvedParticipants
                : 0;

            int rank = leadershipRank.TryGetValue(m, out var resolvedRank)
                ? resolvedRank
                : selectedMarkets.Count;

            decimal pnlScore = (pnl / maxAbsPnl + 1m) / 2m;
            decimal activityScore = maxTrades <= 0 ? 0m : (decimal)trades / maxTrades;
            decimal breadthScore = participants <= 0 ? 0m : (decimal)positiveHits / participants;

            decimal rankScore = selectedMarkets.Count <= 1
                ? 1m
                : 1m - ((decimal)(rank - 1) / (selectedMarkets.Count - 1)) * 0.35m;

            decimal timeframeBonus = m.Timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                ? 0.06m
                : m.Timeframe.Equals("1d", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                    ? 0.03m
                    : 0m;

            decimal score =
                (pnlScore * 0.50m) +
                (breadthScore * 0.30m) +
                (activityScore * 0.20m);

            score = System.Math.Max(0m, score * rankScore + timeframeBonus);
            scores[m] = score;
        }

        return scores;
    }

    private async Task> RunTrueWalkForwardAsync(
        IReadOnlyList strategyTypes,
        IReadOnlyList selectedMarkets,
        FrictionProfile friction,
        IReadOnlyDictionary trustWeightsByType,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        const int foldCount = 3;
        const decimal trainFraction = 0.70m;

        var folds = new List();

        if (selectedMarkets == null || selectedMarkets.Count == 0)
            return folds;

        var baselineMarket = selectedMarkets
            .OrderBy(x => x.Symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Timeframe, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .First();

        var referenceCandles = _feed.GetCandles(baselineMarket.Symbol, baselineMarket.Timeframe)
            .OrderBy(c => c.Time)
            .ToList();

        if (referenceCandles.Count < 300)
            return folds;

        int total = referenceCandles.Count;
        int testSize = total / (foldCount + 2);
        if (testSize < 40)
            return folds;

        for (int fold = 1; fold <= foldCount; fold++)
        {
            int testEndIndex = total - ((foldCount - fold) * testSize) - 1;
            int testStartIndex = testEndIndex - testSize + 1;

            if (testStartIndex <= 0 || testEndIndex >= total)
                continue;

            int trainEndIndex = testStartIndex - 1;
            int trainSize = (int)(trainEndIndex * trainFraction);
            int trainStartIndex = System.Math.Max(0, trainEndIndex - trainSize + 1);

            if (trainEndIndex <= trainStartIndex)
                continue;

            DateTime trainStartUtc = referenceCandles[trainStartIndex].Time;
            DateTime trainEndUtc = referenceCandles[trainEndIndex].Time;
            DateTime testStartUtc = referenceCandles[testStartIndex].Time;
            DateTime testEndUtc = referenceCandles[testEndIndex].Time;

            decimal foldPnl = 0m;

            foreach (var strategyType in strategyTypes)
            {
                decimal strategyWeight = trustWeightsByType.TryGetValue(strategyType, out var resolvedWeight)
                    ? resolvedWeight
                    : 0m;

                if (strategyWeight <= 0m)
                    continue;

                using var scope = _root.CreateScope();

                var strategy = _factory.Create(strategyType);
                var engine = ActivatorUtilities.CreateInstance(
                    scope.ServiceProvider,
                    strategy);

                var ledger = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService();
                var capital = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService();
                capital.Seed(PortfolioCapital, strategyWeight);

                foreach (var market in selectedMarkets)
                {
                    var candles = _feed.GetCandles(market.Symbol, market.Timeframe)
                        .Where(c => c.Time >= testStartUtc && c.Time <= testEndUtc)
                        .OrderBy(c => c.Time)
                        .ToList();

                    if (candles.Count < 20)
                        continue;

                    var marketWeight = 1m / selectedMarkets.Count;

                    var frictionCost = EstimateFrictionCost(
                        PortfolioCapital * strategyWeight * marketWeight,
                        0,
                        friction,
                        candles);

                    foreach (var candle in candles)
                    {
                        await engine.OnTickAsync(
                            market.Symbol,
                            candle.Close,
                            candle.Time,
                            ct);
                    }

                    foldPnl += (ledger.TotalPnL * marketWeight) - frictionCost;
                }
            }
        }

        return folds;
    }

    private static PortfolioBacktestResult BuildResult(
        IReadOnlyList nodes,
        IReadOnlyDictionary capitalWeights,
        IReadOnlyDictionary adjustedSymbolPnL,
        IReadOnlyDictionary adjustedStrategyPnL,
        IReadOnlyDictionary adjustedPnlTimeline)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(nodes);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(capitalWeights);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(adjustedSymbolPnL);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(adjustedStrategyPnL);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(adjustedPnlTimeline);

        var equityAggregator = new PortfolioEquityAggregator();

        foreach (var kv in adjustedPnlTimeline)
            equityAggregator.AddPnlDelta(kv.Key, kv.Value);

        var portfolioEquityTimeline = equityAggregator.BuildFromPnlDeltas(PortfolioCapital);

        if (portfolioEquityTimeline.Count <= 1)
        {
            decimal totalAdjustedPnl = adjustedSymbolPnL.Values.Sum();
            DateTime endUtc = DateTime.UtcNow;

            portfolioEquityTimeline[DateTime.MinValue] = PortfolioCapital;
            portfolioEquityTimeline[endUtc] = PortfolioCapital + totalAdjustedPnl;
        }

        decimal startEquity = PortfolioCapital;
        decimal endEquity = portfolioEquityTimeline.Count > 0
            ? portfolioEquityTimeline.OrderBy(x => x.Key).Last().Value
            : PortfolioCapital;

        decimal portfolioDelta = endEquity - startEquity;
        decimal strategySum = adjustedStrategyPnL.Values.Sum();
        decimal symbolSum = adjustedSymbolPnL.Values.Sum();

        decimal tolerance = 1.0m;

        if (Math.Abs(portfolioDelta - strategySum) > tolerance ||
            Math.Abs(portfolioDelta - symbolSum) > tolerance)
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                "RECONCILIATION FAILURE\n" +
                $"Portfolio Delta : {portfolioDelta:F2}\n" +
                $"Strategy Sum    : {strategySum:F2}\n" +
                $"Symbol Sum      : {symbolSum:F2}\n" +
                $"Î” vs Strategy   : {(portfolioDelta - strategySum):F2}\n" +
                $"Î” vs Symbol     : {(portfolioDelta - symbolSum):F2}");
        }

        return new PortfolioBacktestResult
        {
            StrategyPnL = new Dictionary(adjustedStrategyPnL),
            SymbolPnL = new Dictionary(adjustedSymbolPnL, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase),
            CapitalWeights = new Dictionary(capitalWeights),
            PortfolioEquityTimeline = portfolioEquityTimeline
        };
    }

    private static void AllocateNetDeltaAcrossClosedTrades(
        IReadOnlyList closedTrades,
        decimal netDelta,
        DateTime fallbackTime,
        IDictionary adjustedPnlTimeline)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(closedTrades);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(adjustedPnlTimeline);

        if (netDelta == 0m)
            return;

        if (closedTrades.Count == 0)
        {
            AddAdjustedPnlPoint(adjustedPnlTimeline, fallbackTime, netDelta);
            return;
        }

        decimal denominator = closedTrades.Sum(t => Math.Abs(t.RealizedPnL));
        if (denominator <= 0m)
        {
            DateTime time = closedTrades
                .Select(t => t.ExitTime ?? fallbackTime)
                .DefaultIfEmpty(fallbackTime)
                .Max();

            AddAdjustedPnlPoint(adjustedPnlTimeline, time, netDelta);
            return;
        }

        decimal allocated = 0m;

        for (int i = 0; i < closedTrades.Count; i++)
        {
            var trade = closedTrades[i];
            DateTime time = trade.ExitTime ?? fallbackTime;

            decimal slice = i == closedTrades.Count - 1
                ? netDelta - allocated
                : netDelta * (Math.Abs(trade.RealizedPnL) / denominator);

            allocated += slice;
            AddAdjustedPnlPoint(adjustedPnlTimeline, time, slice);
        }
    }

    private static void AddAdjustedPnlPoint(
        IDictionary adjustedPnlTimeline,
        DateTime time,
        decimal pnlDelta)
    {
        if (adjustedPnlTimeline.TryGetValue(time, out var existing))
            adjustedPnlTimeline[time] = existing + pnlDelta;
        else
            adjustedPnlTimeline[time] = pnlDelta;
    }

    private static Dictionary AggregateAdjustedStrategyPnL(
        IReadOnlyDictionary strategySymbolTimeframePnL)
    {
        var output = new Dictionary();

        foreach (var kv in strategySymbolTimeframePnL)
        {
            int strategyId = ExtractStrategyIdFromStrategySymbolTimeframeKey(kv.Key);
            if (strategyId <= 0)
                continue;

            if (output.ContainsKey(strategyId))
                output[strategyId] += kv.Value;
            else
                output[strategyId] = kv.Value;
        }

        return output;
    }

    private static int ExtractStrategyIdFromStrategySymbolTimeframeKey(string key)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(key))
            return 0;

        var parts = key.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        if (parts.Length < 3)
            return 0;

        string head = parts[0].Trim();
        if (!head.StartsWith("S", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return 0;

        string numeric = head[1..];
        return int.TryParse(numeric, out int id) ? id : 0;
    }

    private static Dictionary AggregateAdjustedSymbolPnL(
        IReadOnlyDictionary symbolTimeframePnL)
    {
        var output = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        foreach (var kv in symbolTimeframePnL)
        {
            var symbol = ExtractSymbolFromSymbolTimeframeKey(kv.Key);
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(symbol))
                continue;

            if (output.ContainsKey(symbol))
                output[symbol] += kv.Value;
            else
                output[symbol] = kv.Value;
        }

        return output;
    }

    private static string ExtractSymbolFromSymbolTimeframeKey(string key)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(key))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = key.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        if (parts.Length < 2)
            return string.Empty;

        return parts[0].Trim();
    }

    private static decimal GetSymbolPnL(TradeLedger ledger, string symbol)
    {
        if (ledger.PnLBySymbol.TryGetValue(symbol, out var pnl))
            return pnl;

        return 0m;
    }

    private static int GetTradeCount(TradeLedger ledger)
    {
        return ledger.TotalTrades;
    }

    private static decimal EstimateFrictionCost(
        decimal positionValue,
        int tradeCount,
        FrictionProfile friction,
        IReadOnlyList candles)
    {
        if (tradeCount <= 0 || positionValue <= 0m)
            return 0m;

        decimal averagePrice = candles.Count == 0
            ? 0m
            : candles.Average(c => c.Close);

        if (averagePrice <= 0m)
            return 0m;

        decimal grossTurnover = positionValue * tradeCount;

        decimal stress = friction.StressMultiplier <= 0m
            ? 1.0m
            : friction.StressMultiplier;

        decimal feeRate = BpsToRate(friction.EffectiveFeeBps);
        decimal slippageRate = BpsToRate(friction.BaseSlippageBps * stress);
        decimal spreadRate = BpsToRate(friction.BaseSpreadBps * stress);

        decimal feeCost = grossTurnover * feeRate;
        decimal slippageCost = grossTurnover * slippageRate;
        decimal spreadCost = grossTurnover * spreadRate;

        return feeCost + slippageCost + spreadCost;
    }

    private static decimal BpsToRate(decimal bps)
    {
        return bps / 10_000m;
    }

    private sealed class WaveBCandidate
    {
        public required MarketKey Market { get; init; }
        public decimal BasePreTradeScore { get; init; }
        public decimal NormalizedPreTradeScore { get; init; }
        public decimal TimeframePreferenceScore { get; init; }
        public decimal LiquidityScore { get; init; }
        public decimal LeadershipScore { get; init; }
        public decimal FinalScore { get; init; }

        // PATCH 22
        public decimal RelativeToLeaderFinalScore { get; set; }
        public decimal RelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore { get; set; }
        public bool PassesDispersionGuard { get; set; }

        // PATCH 24
        public bool PassesRelaxedDispersionGuard { get; set; }
        public bool SelectedByScarcityRelaxedDispersion { get; set; }
    }

    private sealed class WaveBSelectionSnapshot
    {
        public List RankedCandidates { get; init; } = new();
        public List SelectedMarkets { get; init; } = new();
        public Dictionary AllocationWeights { get; init; } = new();
        public Dictionary SelectedPerSymbolCounts { get; init; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        public decimal CashWeight { get; init; }

        // PATCH 22
        public bool DispersionGuardTriggered { get; init; }
        public int EffectiveMinMarkets { get; init; }
        public decimal LeaderFinalScore { get; init; }
        public decimal LeaderBasePreTradeScore { get; init; }

        // PATCH 24
        public int ViableAfterThresholdCount { get; init; }
        public int StrictDispersionPassCount { get; init; }
        public int RelaxedDispersionPassCount { get; init; }
        public bool ScarcityDispersionModeActive { get; init; }
        public int ScarcityRelaxedDispersionRescueCount { get; init; }
        public decimal EffectiveMinRelativeToLeaderFinalScore { get; init; }
        public decimal EffectiveMinRelativeToLeaderPreTradeScore { get; init; }
    }
}

 using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;

namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio;

public sealed class CioDynamicReallocationEngine
{
    private readonly decimal _minWeight;
    private readonly decimal _maxWeight;
    private readonly decimal _maxWeightPerSymbol;
    private readonly int _topK;

    // Hard block hostile deployment.
    private static readonly HashSet HardBlockedSymbols =
        new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
        {
            "ETHUSDT"
        };

    // Existing hard cap.
    private const decimal BtcHardCap = 0.35m;

    // PATCH 20 — regime-aware cash-preservation / no-trade guard
    // Goal:
    // - when edge breadth is weak, do NOT force second-tier exposure
    // - allow large residual cash instead of artificial full deployment
    // - especially defensive when only one high-conviction edge survives
    private const decimal SingleEdgeDeploymentCap = 0.20m;
    private const decimal SevereWeakBreadthSecondEdgeRatio = 0.20m;
    private const decimal ModerateWeakBreadthSecondEdgeRatio = 0.35m;
    private const decimal SevereWeakBreadthDeploymentCap = 0.30m;
    private const decimal ModerateWeakBreadthDeploymentCap = 0.45m;

    public CioDynamicReallocationEngine(
        int topK = 6,
        decimal minWeight = 0.00m,
        decimal maxWeight = 0.35m,
        decimal maxWeightPerSymbol = 0.45m)
    {
        _topK = Math.Max(1, topK);
        _minWeight = Math.Max(0m, minWeight);
        _maxWeight = Math.Max(_minWeight, Math.Min(1.0m, maxWeight));
        _maxWeightPerSymbol = Math.Max(_maxWeight, Math.Min(1.0m, maxWeightPerSymbol));
    }

    public Dictionary ComputeWeights(Dictionary scoreByMarket)
    {
        if (scoreByMarket == null || scoreByMarket.Count == 0)
            return new Dictionary();

        // Hard exclusion first.
        var filtered = scoreByMarket
            .Where(x => !IsHardBlocked(x.Key))
            .ToDictionary(x => x.Key, x => x.Value);

        if (filtered.Count == 0)
            return new Dictionary();

        var positive = filtered
            .Where(x => x.Value > 0m)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ToList();

        if (positive.Count == 0)
            return new Dictionary();

        decimal topScore = positive[0].Value;
        decimal qualityFloor = Math.Max(1m, topScore * 0.15m);

        var selected = positive
            .Where(x => x.Value >= qualityFloor)
            .Take(_topK)
            .ToList();

        if (selected.Count == 0)
            return new Dictionary();

        // Convex spread: leaders get meaningfully higher weight than tail survivors.
        var raw = selected.ToDictionary(
            x => x.Key,
            x => ScoreToConvexWeight(x.Value, topScore));

        decimal rawSum = raw.Values.Sum();
        if (rawSum <= 0m)
            return new Dictionary();

        var normalized = raw.ToDictionary(
            x => x.Key,
            x => x.Value / rawSum);

        decimal regimeAwareDeploymentCap = ComputeRegimeAwareDeploymentCap(selected, topScore);

        return EnforceConstraintsWithCashFallback(normalized, regimeAwareDeploymentCap);
    }

    private Dictionary EnforceConstraintsWithCashFallback(
        Dictionary weights,
        decimal deploymentCap)
    {
        if (weights == null || weights.Count == 0)
            return new Dictionary();

        var output = weights.ToDictionary(x => x.Key, x => x.Value);

        // Stage 1: clamp generic market bounds without re-normalizing excess back in.
        foreach (var key in output.Keys.ToList())
        {
            if (output[key] < _minWeight)
                output[key] = 0m;
            else if (output[key] > _maxWeight)
                output[key] = _maxWeight;
        }

        // Stage 2: per-symbol cap with cash fallback.
        ApplyPerSymbolCapWithoutRedistribution(output, _maxWeightPerSymbol);

        // Stage 3: explicit BTC hard cap with cash fallback.
        ApplySymbolHardCapWithoutRedistribution(output, "BTCUSDT", BtcHardCap);

        // Stage 4: PATCH 20 regime-aware deployment cap.
        // If breadth is weak, keep residual capital in cash instead of forcing lower-quality exposure.
        ApplyDeploymentCapWithoutRedistribution(output, deploymentCap);

        // Final cleanup: keep positive weights only.
        return output
            .Where(x => x.Value > 0m)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ToDictionary(x => x.Key, x => x.Value);
    }

    private static decimal ComputeRegimeAwareDeploymentCap(
        IReadOnlyList> selected,
        decimal topScore)
    {
        if (selected == null || selected.Count == 0 || topScore <= 0m)
            return 0m;

        // One surviving real edge = defensive no-trade regime.
        if (selected.Count == 1)
            return SingleEdgeDeploymentCap;

        decimal secondScore = selected
            .Skip(1)
            .Select(x => x.Value)
            .DefaultIfEmpty(0m)
            .Max();

        decimal secondEdgeRatio = topScore <= 0m
            ? 0m
            : secondScore / topScore;

        if (secondEdgeRatio <= SevereWeakBreadthSecondEdgeRatio)
            return SevereWeakBreadthDeploymentCap;

        if (secondEdgeRatio <= ModerateWeakBreadthSecondEdgeRatio)
            return ModerateWeakBreadthDeploymentCap;

        return 1.0m;
    }

    private static void ApplyDeploymentCapWithoutRedistribution(
        Dictionary weights,
        decimal deploymentCap)
    {
        if (weights.Count == 0)
            return;

        deploymentCap = Math.Max(0m, Math.Min(1.0m, deploymentCap));

        decimal total = weights.Values.Sum();
        if (total <= 0m || total <= deploymentCap)
            return;

        decimal scale = deploymentCap / total;
        foreach (var key in weights.Keys.ToList())
            weights[key] *= scale;
    }

    private static decimal ScoreToConvexWeight(decimal score, decimal topScore)
    {
        if (score <= 0m || topScore <= 0m)
            return 0m;

        decimal ratio = score / topScore;
        ratio = Math.Max(0m, Math.Min(1m, ratio));

        return ratio * ratio;
    }

    private static bool IsHardBlocked(MarketKey market)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(market.Symbol))
            return false;

        return HardBlockedSymbols.Contains(market.Symbol);
    }

    private static void ApplyPerSymbolCapWithoutRedistribution(
        Dictionary weights,
        decimal symbolCap)
    {
        if (weights.Count == 0)
            return;

        var bySymbol = weights
            .GroupBy(x => x.Key.Symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        foreach (var group in bySymbol)
        {
            decimal total = group.Sum(x => x.Value);
            if (total <= symbolCap)
                continue;

            foreach (var item in group)
            {
                decimal share = total <= 0m ? 0m : item.Value / total;
                weights[item.Key] = symbolCap * share;
            }
        }
    }

    private static void ApplySymbolHardCapWithoutRedistribution(
        Dictionary weights,
        string symbol,
        decimal hardCap)
    {
        var symbolItems = weights
            .Where(x => x.Key.Symbol.Equals(symbol, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .ToList();

        if (symbolItems.Count == 0)
            return;

        decimal currentTotal = symbolItems.Sum(x => x.Value);
        if (currentTotal <= hardCap)
            return;

        foreach (var item in symbolItems)
        {
            decimal share = currentTotal <= 0m ? 0m : item.Value / currentTotal;
            weights[item.Key] = hardCap * share;
        }
    }
}
