 namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio;

public sealed record FrictionProfile(
    decimal MakerFeeBps,
    decimal TakerFeeBps,
    decimal BaseSlippageBps,
    decimal BaseSpreadBps,
    decimal StressMultiplier = 1.0m,
    bool PreferMaker = false)
{
    public static FrictionProfile Default => new(
        MakerFeeBps: 2m,         // 0.02%
        TakerFeeBps: 10m,        // 0.10%
        BaseSlippageBps: 5m,     // 0.05%
        BaseSpreadBps: 3m,       // 0.03%
        StressMultiplier: 1.0m,
        PreferMaker: false);

    public decimal EffectiveFeeBps => PreferMaker ? MakerFeeBps : TakerFeeBps;
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 F I L E :   D : \ D   D A T A   B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ P o r t f o l i o \ L e a d e r s h i p R a n k i n g S e r v i c e . c s 
 
 T Y P E :   . c s 
 
 S I Z E :   3   K B 
 
 L I N E S :   8 3 
 
 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using TQGA.Application.Interfaces;

namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio;

public sealed class LeadershipRankingService
{
    public IReadOnlyDictionary RankMarkets(
        ICandleDataFeed feed,
        IEnumerable symbols,
        IEnumerable timeframes)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(feed);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(symbols);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(timeframes);

        var scores = new Dictionary();

        foreach (var symbol in symbols)
        {
            foreach (var timeframe in timeframes)
            {
                var candles = feed.GetCandles(symbol, timeframe)
                    .OrderBy(c => c.Time)
                    .TakeLast(160)
                    .ToList();

                if (candles.Count < 80)
                {
                    scores[new MarketKey(symbol, timeframe)] = decimal.MinValue;
                    continue;
                }

                var closes = candles.Select(c => c.Close).ToList();

                var ret20 = SafeReturn(closes, 20);
                var ret60 = SafeReturn(closes, 60);
                var slope20 = SafeSlope(closes, 20);
                var vol20 = SafeVol(closes, 20);

                // Favor strength + trend persistence.
                // Penalize too-dead / too-flat markets.
                var score =
                    (ret20 * 0.45m) +
                    (ret60 * 0.35m) +
                    (slope20 * 0.20m) +
                    (vol20 * 0.05m);

                scores[new MarketKey(symbol, timeframe)] = score;
            }
        }

        return scores;
    }

    private static decimal SafeReturn(List closes, int lookback)
    {
        if (closes.Count <= lookback)
            return 0m;

        var start = closes[^lookback];
        var end = closes[^1];

        if (start == 0m)
            return 0m;

        return (end - start) / start;
    }

    private static decimal SafeSlope(List closes, int lookback)
    {
        if (closes.Count <= lookback)
            return 0m;

        var segment = closes.TakeLast(lookback).ToList();
        var first = segment.First();
        var last = segment.Last();

        if (first == 0m)
            return 0m;

        return (last - first) / first / lookback;
    }

    private static decimal SafeVol(List closes, int lookback)
    {
        if (closes.Count <= lookback + 1)
            return 0m;

        var segment = closes.TakeLast(lookback + 1).ToList();
        var returns = new List();

        for (int i = 1; i < segment.Count; i++)
        {
            var prev = segment[i - 1];
            var cur = segment[i];

            if (prev == 0m)
                continue;

            returns.Add(Math.Abs((cur - prev) / prev));
        }

        if (returns.Count == 0)
            return 0m;

        return returns.Average();
    }
}

}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using System.Threading;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Services;
using TQGA.Application.Strategy;

namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio;

public sealed class PortfolioBacktestOrchestrator
{
    private readonly PortfolioBacktestRunner _runner;
    private readonly AlphaRankingReportService _alphaRanking;
    private readonly CioCapitalReportService _cioCapital;
    private readonly StrategyContributionReportService _strategyPnl;
    private readonly SymbolHeatmapReportService _symbolReport;
    private readonly PortfolioEquityReportService _portfolioEquity;
    private readonly PortfolioDrawdownReportService _portfolioDrawdown;

    public PortfolioBacktestOrchestrator(
        PortfolioBacktestRunner runner,
        AlphaRankingReportService alphaRanking,
        CioCapitalReportService cioCapital,
        StrategyContributionReportService strategyPnl,
        SymbolHeatmapReportService symbolReport,
        PortfolioEquityReportService portfolioEquity,
        PortfolioDrawdownReportService portfolioDrawdown)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(runner);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(alphaRanking);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(cioCapital);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(strategyPnl);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(symbolReport);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(portfolioEquity);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(portfolioDrawdown);

        _runner = runner;
        _alphaRanking = alphaRanking;
        _cioCapital = cioCapital;
        _strategyPnl = strategyPnl;
        _symbolReport = symbolReport;
        _portfolioEquity = portfolioEquity;
        _portfolioDrawdown = portfolioDrawdown;
    }

    public IReadOnlyList GetRegisteredStrategies()
    {
        return StrategyFactory.DiscoverConcreteStrategyTypes();
    }

    public Task RunSelectedAsync(
        IReadOnlyList selectedStrategies,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        return RunSelectedAsync(
            selectedStrategies,
            BinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols,
            BinanceUniverse.Timeframes,
            FrictionProfile.Default,
            ct);
    }

    public Task RunSelectedAsync(
        IReadOnlyList selectedStrategies,
        IReadOnlyList selectedTimeframes,
        FrictionProfile friction,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        return RunSelectedAsync(
            selectedStrategies,
            BinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols,
            selectedTimeframes,
            friction,
            ct);
    }

    public async Task RunSelectedAsync(
        IReadOnlyList selectedStrategies,
        IReadOnlyList selectedSymbols,
        IReadOnlyList selectedTimeframes,
        FrictionProfile friction,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedStrategies);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedSymbols);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedTimeframes);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(friction);

        if (selectedStrategies.Count == 0)
            throw new InvalidOperationException("No strategies selected.");

        var result = await _runner.RunAsync(
            selectedStrategies,
            selectedSymbols,
            selectedTimeframes,
            friction,
            ct);

        // PATCH 20:
        // Canonical post-gating CIO is computed ONCE here, stored ONCE here,
        // and must preserve true deployed weights including cash fallback.
        // Do NOT renormalize this dictionary back to 100%, otherwise the
        // regime-aware cash-preservation / no-trade guard is destroyed downstream.
        var fitnessSvc = new A84StrategyFitnessGatingReportService();
        var cfg = new A84StrategyFitnessGatingReportService.FitnessConfig();

        var (_, allowedStrategyIds) = fitnessSvc.ComputeFitness(result, cfg);

        var rawCanonicalCioPostGatingWeights =
            fitnessSvc.RecomputeCioWeightsWithGating(result, allowedStrategyIds, cfg)
            ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights =
            PreserveCanonicalCioWeights(rawCanonicalCioPostGatingWeights);

        // PATCH 20:
        // Canonical post-gating cash must survive into downstream reports.
        // Use the stricter / more defensive cash figure:
        // - existing runner cash
        // - cash implied by the preserved canonical CIO deployment
        result.CashAllocationWeight = ComputeCanonicalCashWeight(
            result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights,
            result.CashAllocationWeight);

        _alphaRanking.Generate(result);

        if (result.HasMarketAllocationWeights)
        {
            _cioCapital.Generate(
                result.CapitalWeights,
                result.MarketAllocationWeights,
                result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights,
                result.CashAllocationWeight);
        }
        else
        {
            _cioCapital.Generate(
                result.CapitalWeights,
                runnerMarketAllocationWeights: null,
                canonicalCioPostGatingWeights: result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights,
                cashWeight: result.CashAllocationWeight);
        }

        _strategyPnl.Generate(result.StrategyPnL);
        _symbolReport.Generate(result.SymbolPnL);
        _portfolioEquity.Generate(result.PortfolioEquityTimeline);
        _portfolioDrawdown.Generate(result.PortfolioEquityTimeline);

        new SymbolTimeframePnlReportService().Generate(result.SymbolTimeframePnL);
        new CioWeightsSymbolTimeframeReportService().Generate(result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights);
        new StrategySymbolTimeframePnlReportService().Generate(result.StrategySymbolTimeframePnL);

        new ReconciliationReportService().Generate(result);

        // All A84 generation must consume the stored canonical dictionary exactly as preserved here.
        new UniversalResearchReportService().GenerateAll(
            result,
            DateTime.UtcNow,
            selectedStrategies);

        new WalkForwardValidationReportService().GenerateProxyReports(
            result,
            DateTime.UtcNow,
            selectedStrategies);

        return result;
    }

    private static Dictionary PreserveCanonicalCioWeights(
        IReadOnlyDictionary source)
    {
        var cleaned = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        foreach (var kv in source)
        {
            string key = kv.Key?.Trim() ?? string.Empty;
            decimal value = kv.Value;

            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(key))
                continue;

            if (value <= 0m)
                continue;

            cleaned[key] = value;
        }

        return cleaned;
    }

    private static decimal ComputeCanonicalCashWeight(
        IReadOnlyDictionary canonicalWeights,
        decimal existingCashWeight)
    {
        decimal canonicalAllocated = canonicalWeights?.Values.Sum() ?? 0m;
        decimal canonicalCash = 1m - canonicalAllocated;

        if (canonicalCash < 0m)
            canonicalCash = 0m;
        else if (canonicalCash > 1m)
            canonicalCash = 1m;

        if (existingCashWeight < 0m)
            existingCashWeight = 0m;
        else if (existingCashWeight > 1m)
            existingCashWeight = 1m;

        return Math.Max(existingCashWeight, canonicalCash);
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio;

public sealed class PortfolioEquityAggregator
{
    private readonly SortedDictionary _timeline = new();
    private readonly SortedDictionary _pnlDeltas = new();

    public void AddPoint(DateTime time, decimal equity)
    {
        if (_timeline.TryGetValue(time, out var existing))
            _timeline[time] = existing + equity;
        else
            _timeline[time] = equity;
    }

    public void AddCurve(
        IReadOnlyList<(DateTime Time, decimal Value)> points,
        bool skipMinValueSeed = true)
    {
        if (points == null || points.Count == 0)
            return;

        foreach (var p in points)
        {
            if (skipMinValueSeed && p.Time == DateTime.MinValue)
                continue;

            AddPoint(p.Time, p.Value);
        }
    }

    public void AddPnlDelta(DateTime time, decimal pnlDelta)
    {
        if (_pnlDeltas.TryGetValue(time, out var existing))
            _pnlDeltas[time] = existing + pnlDelta;
        else
            _pnlDeltas[time] = pnlDelta;
    }

    public Dictionary Build()
    {
        return new Dictionary(_timeline);
    }

    public Dictionary BuildFromPnlDeltas(decimal startingCapital)
    {
        var output = new Dictionary();
        decimal runningEquity = startingCapital;

        output[DateTime.MinValue] = startingCapital;

        foreach (var kv in _pnlDeltas)
        {
            runningEquity += kv.Value;
            output[kv.Key] = runningEquity;
        }

        return output;
    }

    public IReadOnlyDictionary Timeline => _timeline;
    public IReadOnlyDictionary PnlDeltas => _pnlDeltas;
}

 using TQGA.Domain.Market;

namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio;

public sealed class PortfolioRiskBudgetEngine
{
    public RiskBudgetDecision Evaluate(
        string symbol,
        string timeframe,
        IReadOnlyList candles,
        decimal currentPortfolioEquity,
        decimal currentDrawdownPct,
        IReadOnlyDictionary openRiskBySymbol,
        IReadOnlyDictionary openRiskByCluster,
        decimal currentTotalOpenRiskPct)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(symbol);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(timeframe);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(candles);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(openRiskBySymbol);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(openRiskByCluster);

        if (candles.Count < 120)
        {
            return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, "REJECT: insufficient candles");
        }

        var last = candles[^1].Close;
        if (last <= 0m)
        {
            return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, "REJECT: invalid last price");
        }

        var atrPct = EstimateAtrPct(candles);
        if (atrPct <= 0m)
        {
            return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, "REJECT: invalid ATR");
        }

        var regime = DetectRegime(candles);
        var regimeMultiplier = regime switch
        {
            RiskRegime.HighVolUp => 1.00m,
            RiskRegime.TrendUp => 0.85m,
            RiskRegime.Range => 0.35m,
            RiskRegime.HighVolDown => 0.15m,
            RiskRegime.TrendDown => 0.10m,
            _ => 0m
        };

        if (regimeMultiplier <= 0m)
        {
            return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, $"REJECT: regime={regime}");
        }

        var cluster = ResolveCluster(symbol);

        const decimal maxPerSymbolRiskPct = 0.75m;   // 0.75% risk budget per symbol
        const decimal maxPerClusterRiskPct = 1.75m;  // 1.75% risk budget per cluster
        const decimal maxTotalOpenRiskPct = 3.00m;   // 3.00% total open portfolio risk

        var symbolOpen = openRiskBySymbol.TryGetValue(symbol, out var sRisk) ? sRisk : 0m;
        var clusterOpen = openRiskByCluster.TryGetValue(cluster, out var cRisk) ? cRisk : 0m;

        if (symbolOpen >= maxPerSymbolRiskPct)
        {
            return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, $"REJECT: per-symbol cap reached ({symbolOpen:F2}% >= {maxPerSymbolRiskPct:F2}%)");
        }

        if (clusterOpen >= maxPerClusterRiskPct)
        {
            return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, $"REJECT: per-cluster cap reached ({clusterOpen:F2}% >= {maxPerClusterRiskPct:F2}%)");
        }

        if (currentTotalOpenRiskPct >= maxTotalOpenRiskPct)
        {
            return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, $"REJECT: total portfolio risk cap reached ({currentTotalOpenRiskPct:F2}% >= {maxTotalOpenRiskPct:F2}%)");
        }

        var drawdownMultiplier = currentDrawdownPct switch
        {
            < 5m => 1.00m,
            < 10m => 0.70m,
            < 15m => 0.40m,
            _ => 0m
        };

        if (drawdownMultiplier <= 0m)
        {
            return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, $"REJECT: drawdown throttle active ({currentDrawdownPct:F2}%)");
        }

        // Base risk target per trade
        decimal baseRiskPct = 0.50m; // 0.50% of portfolio equity

        // Timeframe preference: your reports keep showing 4h dominance, so allow a small 4h premium.
        decimal timeframeMultiplier =
            timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? 1.10m :
            timeframe.Equals("1h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? 0.80m :
            0.75m;

        var allowedRiskPct = baseRiskPct * regimeMultiplier * drawdownMultiplier * timeframeMultiplier;

        var remainingSymbolRoom = Math.Max(0m, maxPerSymbolRiskPct - symbolOpen);
        var remainingClusterRoom = Math.Max(0m, maxPerClusterRiskPct - clusterOpen);
        var remainingPortfolioRoom = Math.Max(0m, maxTotalOpenRiskPct - currentTotalOpenRiskPct);

        allowedRiskPct = Math.Min(allowedRiskPct, remainingSymbolRoom);
        allowedRiskPct = Math.Min(allowedRiskPct, remainingClusterRoom);
        allowedRiskPct = Math.Min(allowedRiskPct, remainingPortfolioRoom);

        if (allowedRiskPct <= 0m)
        {
            return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, "REJECT: no remaining risk budget");
        }

        // ATR sizing:
        // position value = (portfolio equity * risk%) / ATR%
        // capped to avoid absurd sizing in very low-vol conditions
        var rawPositionValue = currentPortfolioEquity * (allowedRiskPct / 100m) / atrPct;
        var maxPositionValue = currentPortfolioEquity * 0.25m; // hard cap 25% of equity
        var positionValue = Math.Min(rawPositionValue, maxPositionValue);

        if (positionValue <= 0m)
        {
            return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, "REJECT: computed position value <= 0");
        }

        var quantity = positionValue / last;
        if (quantity <= 0m)
        {
            return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, "REJECT: computed quantity <= 0");
        }

        return new RiskBudgetDecision(
            IsAllowed: true,
            Symbol: symbol,
            Timeframe: timeframe,
            Cluster: cluster,
            Regime: regime.ToString(),
            AllowedRiskPct: allowedRiskPct,
            AtrPct: atrPct,
            PositionValue: positionValue,
            Quantity: quantity,
            Reason: "OK");
    }

    public static decimal EstimateAtrPct(IReadOnlyList candles, int lookback = 14)
    {
        if (candles.Count < lookback + 1)
            return 0m;

        var slice = candles.TakeLast(lookback).ToList();
        decimal trSum = 0m;

        for (int i = 0; i < slice.Count; i++)
        {
            var cur = slice[i];
            var prevClose = i == 0 ? cur.Close : slice[i - 1].Close;

            var tr = Math.Max(
                cur.High - cur.Low,
                Math.Max(Math.Abs(cur.High - prevClose), Math.Abs(cur.Low - prevClose)));

            trSum += tr;
        }

        var atr = trSum / lookback;
        var last = slice[^1].Close;

        return last <= 0m ? 0m : atr / last;
    }

    private static RiskRegime DetectRegime(IReadOnlyList candles)
    {
        var closes = candles.Select(c => c.Close).ToList();
        if (closes.Count < 120)
            return RiskRegime.Unknown;

        var ema21 = closes.TakeLast(21).Average();
        var ema50 = closes.TakeLast(50).Average();
        var ema120 = closes.TakeLast(120).Average();

        var avgAbsRet = AverageAbsReturn(candles.TakeLast(20).ToList());

        bool trendUp = ema21 > ema50 && ema50 > ema120;
        bool trendDown = ema21 < ema50 && ema50 < ema120;
        bool highVol = avgAbsRet >= 0.012m;

        if (trendUp && highVol) return RiskRegime.HighVolUp;
        if (trendUp) return RiskRegime.TrendUp;
        if (trendDown && highVol) return RiskRegime.HighVolDown;
        if (trendDown) return RiskRegime.TrendDown;
        return RiskRegime.Range;
    }

    private static decimal AverageAbsReturn(IReadOnlyList candles)
    {
        if (candles.Count < 2)
            return 0m;

        decimal sum = 0m;
        int n = 0;

        for (int i = 1; i < candles.Count; i++)
        {
            var prev = candles[i - 1].Close;
            var cur = candles[i].Close;

            if (prev == 0m)
                continue;

            sum += Math.Abs((cur - prev) / prev);
            n++;
        }

        return n == 0 ? 0m : sum / n;
    }

    public static string ResolveCluster(string symbol)
    {
        if (new[] { "BTCUSDT", "ETHUSDT", "BNBUSDT", "SOLUSDT", "XRPUSDT", "AVAXUSDT" }.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "Majors";

        if (new[] { "AAVEUSDT", "UNIUSDT", "MKRUSDT", "RUNEUSDT" }.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "DeFi";

        if (new[] { "ICPUSDT", "RNDRUSDT", "FETUSDT", "GRTUSDT" }.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "AI_Compute";

        if (new[] { "ORDIUSDT", "TIAUSDT", "INJUSDT", "SUIUSDT", "SEIUSDT", "JUPUSDT", "WIFUSDT", "ARBUSDT", "OPUSDT" }.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "Narrative";

        return "Other";
    }

    public sealed record RiskBudgetDecision(
        bool IsAllowed,
        string Symbol,
        string Timeframe,
        string Cluster,
        string Regime,
        decimal AllowedRiskPct,
        decimal AtrPct,
        decimal PositionValue,
        decimal Quantity,
        string Reason)
    {
        public static RiskBudgetDecision Reject(string symbol, string timeframe, string reason) =>
            new(
                IsAllowed: false,
                Symbol: symbol,
                Timeframe: timeframe,
                Cluster: ResolveCluster(symbol),
                Regime: RiskRegime.Unknown.ToString(),
                AllowedRiskPct: 0m,
                AtrPct: 0m,
                PositionValue: 0m,
                Quantity: 0m,
                Reason: reason);
    }

    private enum RiskRegime
    {
        Unknown = 0,
        Range = 1,
        TrendUp = 2,
        TrendDown = 3,
        HighVolUp = 4,
        HighVolDown = 5
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 F I L E :   D : \ D   D A T A   B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ P o r t f o l i o \ P r e T r a d e M a r k e t S e l e c t i o n S e r v i c e . c s 
 
 T Y P E :   . c s 
 
 S I Z E :   3 3 . 4 6   K B 
 
 L I N E S :   6 5 8 
 
 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Interfaces;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;
using TQGA.Domain.Market;

namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio;

public sealed class PreTradeMarketSelectionService
{
    private const decimal MinAverageDollarVolume = 2_000_000m;
    private const decimal MinAverageAbsoluteReturn = 0.006m;
    private const decimal HighVolThreshold = 0.012m;
    private const decimal MaxTrendExtension = 0.18m;

    // PATCH 26 — Emerging Trend Near-Miss Regime Lane
    private const int EmergingTrendMaxMarkets = 2;
    private const decimal EmergingTrendMinLeadershipScore = 0.015m;
    private const decimal EmergingTrendMinAverageDollarVolume = 2_000_000m;
    private const decimal EmergingTrendMinAverageAbsoluteReturn = 0.012m;
    private const decimal EmergingTrendMaxTrendExtension = 0.08m;
    private const decimal EmergingTrendRangeScoreFloor = 0.27m;
    private const string EmergingTrendLaneLabel = "EMERGING_TREND_NEAR_MISS";

    // PATCH 27 — Liquidity Near-Miss Tier-2 Lane
    // Purpose:
    // - Do NOT globally weaken the core liquidity gate.
    // - Allow a very small research lane for strong 4h candidates that miss the
    //   strict liquidity threshold but are still institutionally interesting.
    private const int LiquidityTier2MaxMarkets = 2;
    private const decimal LiquidityTier2MinAverageDollarVolume = 1_400_000m;
    private const decimal LiquidityTier2MinAverageAbsoluteReturn = 0.010m;
    private const decimal LiquidityTier2MinLeadershipScore = 0.015m;
    private const decimal LiquidityTier2MaxTrendExtension = 0.10m;
    private const decimal LiquidityTier2ScoreFloor = 0.27m;
    private const string LiquidityTier2LaneLabel = "LIQUIDITY_TIER2_NEAR_MISS";

    public SelectionResult SelectMarkets(
        ICandleDataFeed feed,
        IReadOnlyList symbols,
        IReadOnlyList timeframes,
        int topN = 12)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(feed);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(symbols);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(timeframes);

        topN = Math.Max(1, topN);

        var leadership = new LeadershipRankingService()
            .RankMarkets(feed, symbols, timeframes);

        var accepted = new List();
        var rejected = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var telemetryRows = new List();
        var emergingTrendNearMissPool = new List();
        var liquidityTier2NearMissPool = new List();

        foreach (var symbol in symbols)
        {
            foreach (var timeframe in timeframes)
            {
                var market = new MarketKey(symbol, timeframe);
                var marketKey = $"{symbol}::{timeframe}";

                var candles = feed.GetCandles(symbol, timeframe)
                    .OrderBy(c => c.Time)
                    .TakeLast(220)
                    .ToList();

                if (candles.Count < 120)
                {
                    const string reason = "REJECT: insufficient history";

                    rejected[marketKey] = reason;
                    telemetryRows.Add(new PreTradeTelemetryRow
                    {
                        Market = market,
                        CandleCount = candles.Count,
                        AverageDollarVolume = 0m,
                        AverageAbsoluteReturn = 0m,
                        LeadershipScore = 0m,
                        TimeframeBonus = GetTimeframeBonus(timeframe),
                        RegimeBonus = 0m,
                        TrendExtension = 0m,
                        FinalScore = 0m,
                        RegimeState = MarketTrendState.Unknown,
                        Decision = reason,
                        PassedHistory = false,
                        PassedLiquidity = false,
                        PassedVolatility = false,
                        PassedRegime = false,
                        PassedExtension = false,
                        EligibleForEmergingTrendLane = false,
                        SelectedByEmergingTrendLane = false,
                        EligibleForLiquidityTier2Lane = false,
                        SelectedByLiquidityTier2Lane = false,
                        SelectedTopN = false
                    });
                    continue;
                }

                var avgDollarVolume = candles.Average(c => c.Close * c.Volume);
                var avgAbsReturn = ComputeAverageAbsoluteReturn(candles);
                var trend = ComputeTrendState(candles);
                var maturity = ComputeTrendExtension(candles);

                leadership.TryGetValue(market, out var leadershipScore);

                decimal timeframeBonus = GetTimeframeBonus(timeframe);
                decimal regimeBonus = trend == MarketTrendState.HighVolUp ? 0.15m : 0.08m;
                decimal qualityPenalty = maturity * 0.50m;
                decimal finalScore = leadershipScore + timeframeBonus + regimeBonus - qualityPenalty;

                bool passedLiquidity = avgDollarVolume >= MinAverageDollarVolume;
                bool passedVolatility = avgAbsReturn >= MinAverageAbsoluteReturn;
                bool passedRegime = trend is MarketTrendState.TrendUp or MarketTrendState.HighVolUp;
                bool passedExtension = maturity <= MaxTrendExtension;

                bool eligibleForEmergingTrendLane =
                    timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) &&
                    trend == MarketTrendState.Range &&
                    avgDollarVolume >= EmergingTrendMinAverageDollarVolume &&
                    avgAbsReturn >= EmergingTrendMinAverageAbsoluteReturn &&
                    maturity <= EmergingTrendMaxTrendExtension &&
                    leadershipScore >= EmergingTrendMinLeadershipScore &&
                    finalScore >= EmergingTrendRangeScoreFloor;

                bool eligibleForLiquidityTier2Lane =
                    timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) &&
                    !passedLiquidity &&
                    avgDollarVolume >= LiquidityTier2MinAverageDollarVolume &&
                    avgAbsReturn >= LiquidityTier2MinAverageAbsoluteReturn &&
                    maturity <= LiquidityTier2MaxTrendExtension &&
                    leadershipScore >= LiquidityTier2MinLeadershipScore &&
                    finalScore >= LiquidityTier2ScoreFloor &&
                    trend is MarketTrendState.TrendUp or MarketTrendState.HighVolUp or MarketTrendState.Range;

                string? rejectionReason = null;

                if (!passedLiquidity)
                    rejectionReason = "REJECT: low liquidity";
                else if (!passedVolatility)
                    rejectionReason = "REJECT: dead / too low volatility";
                else if (!passedRegime)
                    rejectionReason = "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up";
                else if (!passedExtension)
                    rejectionReason = "REJECT: late / overextended trend";

                var row = new PreTradeTelemetryRow
                {
                    Market = market,
                    CandleCount = candles.Count,
                    AverageDollarVolume = avgDollarVolume,
                    AverageAbsoluteReturn = avgAbsReturn,
                    LeadershipScore = leadershipScore,
                    TimeframeBonus = timeframeBonus,
                    RegimeBonus = regimeBonus,
                    TrendExtension = maturity,
                    FinalScore = finalScore,
                    RegimeState = trend,
                    Decision = rejectionReason ?? "ACCEPT: pre-topN",
                    PassedHistory = true,
                    PassedLiquidity = passedLiquidity,
                    PassedVolatility = passedVolatility,
                    PassedRegime = passedRegime,
                    PassedExtension = passedExtension,
                    EligibleForEmergingTrendLane = eligibleForEmergingTrendLane,
                    SelectedByEmergingTrendLane = false,
                    EligibleForLiquidityTier2Lane = eligibleForLiquidityTier2Lane,
                    SelectedByLiquidityTier2Lane = false,
                    SelectedTopN = false
                };

                telemetryRows.Add(row);

                if (rejectionReason != null)
                {
                    if (rejectionReason.Equals("REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) &&
                        eligibleForEmergingTrendLane)
                    {
                        emergingTrendNearMissPool.Add(row);
                    }
                    else if (rejectionReason.Equals("REJECT: low liquidity", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) &&
                             eligibleForLiquidityTier2Lane)
                    {
                        liquidityTier2NearMissPool.Add(row);
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        rejected[marketKey] = rejectionReason;
                    }

                    continue;
                }

                accepted.Add(new SelectedMarket(
                    market,
                    finalScore,
                    avgDollarVolume,
                    avgAbsReturn,
                    trend.ToString(),
                    maturity,
                    "CORE_TREND"));
            }
        }

        var emergingSelected = emergingTrendNearMissPool
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.FinalScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.LeadershipScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.AverageDollarVolume)
            .Take(EmergingTrendMaxMarkets)
            .ToList();

        foreach (var row in emergingSelected)
        {
            row.SelectedByEmergingTrendLane = true;
            row.Decision = $"ACCEPT: {EmergingTrendLaneLabel}";

            accepted.Add(new SelectedMarket(
                row.Market,
                row.FinalScore,
                row.AverageDollarVolume,
                row.AverageAbsoluteReturn,
                $"{row.RegimeState}→{EmergingTrendLaneLabel}",
                row.TrendExtension,
                EmergingTrendLaneLabel));
        }

        foreach (var row in emergingTrendNearMissPool.Except(emergingSelected))
        {
            rejected[$"{row.Market.Symbol}::{row.Market.Timeframe}"] =
                $"REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow (max={EmergingTrendMaxMarkets})";
            row.Decision = $"REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow (max={EmergingTrendMaxMarkets})";
        }

        var liquidityTier2Selected = liquidityTier2NearMissPool
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.FinalScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.LeadershipScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.AverageDollarVolume)
            .Take(LiquidityTier2MaxMarkets)
            .ToList();

        foreach (var row in liquidityTier2Selected)
        {
            row.SelectedByLiquidityTier2Lane = true;
            row.Decision = $"ACCEPT: {LiquidityTier2LaneLabel}";

            accepted.Add(new SelectedMarket(
                row.Market,
                row.FinalScore,
                row.AverageDollarVolume,
                row.AverageAbsoluteReturn,
                $"{row.RegimeState}→{LiquidityTier2LaneLabel}",
                row.TrendExtension,
                LiquidityTier2LaneLabel));
        }

        foreach (var row in liquidityTier2NearMissPool.Except(liquidityTier2Selected))
        {
            rejected[$"{row.Market.Symbol}::{row.Market.Timeframe}"] =
                $"REJECT: liquidity tier-2 lane overflow (max={LiquidityTier2MaxMarkets})";
            row.Decision = $"REJECT: liquidity tier-2 lane overflow (max={LiquidityTier2MaxMarkets})";
        }

        var selected = accepted
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Score)
            .Take(topN)
            .ToList();

        var selectedSet = selected
            .Select(x => x.Market)
            .ToHashSet();

        foreach (var row in accepted.Where(x => !selectedSet.Contains(x.Market)))
        {
            rejected[$"{row.Market.Symbol}::{row.Market.Timeframe}"] =
                $"REJECT: outside top {topN} leadership set";
        }

        foreach (var row in telemetryRows)
        {
            if (selectedSet.Contains(row.Market))
            {
                row.Decision = row.SelectedByEmergingTrendLane
                    ? $"SELECTED: {EmergingTrendLaneLabel}"
                    : row.SelectedByLiquidityTier2Lane
                        ? $"SELECTED: {LiquidityTier2LaneLabel}"
                        : "SELECTED: top leadership set";
                row.SelectedTopN = true;
            }
            else if (row.Decision == "ACCEPT: pre-topN")
            {
                row.Decision = $"REJECT: outside top {topN} leadership set";
            }
            else if (row.Decision == $"ACCEPT: {EmergingTrendLaneLabel}" ||
                     row.Decision == $"ACCEPT: {LiquidityTier2LaneLabel}")
            {
                row.Decision = $"REJECT: outside top {topN} leadership set";
            }
        }

        WritePreTradeRegimeTelemetryReport(
            telemetryRows,
            selected,
            topN);

        return new SelectionResult(
            selected,
            rejected);
    }

    private static void WritePreTradeRegimeTelemetryReport(
        IReadOnlyList telemetryRows,
        IReadOnlyList selectedMarkets,
        int topN)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_17_PRETRADE_REGIME_TELEMETRY_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        int totalUniverse = telemetryRows.Count;
        int selectedCount = telemetryRows.Count(x => x.SelectedTopN);
        int acceptedPreTopNCount = telemetryRows.Count(x =>
            x.Decision.StartsWith("SELECTED:", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            x.Decision.StartsWith("REJECT: outside top", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

        int insufficientHistoryCount = telemetryRows.Count(x => x.Decision.Equals("REJECT: insufficient history", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
        int lowLiquidityCount = telemetryRows.Count(x => x.Decision.Equals("REJECT: low liquidity", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
        int lowVolCount = telemetryRows.Count(x => x.Decision.Equals("REJECT: dead / too low volatility", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
        int regimeRejectCount = telemetryRows.Count(x => x.Decision.Equals("REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
        int extensionRejectCount = telemetryRows.Count(x => x.Decision.Equals("REJECT: late / overextended trend", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
        int outsideTopNCount = telemetryRows.Count(x => x.Decision.StartsWith("REJECT: outside top", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
        int emergingEligibleCount = telemetryRows.Count(x => x.EligibleForEmergingTrendLane);
        int emergingSelectedCount = telemetryRows.Count(x => x.SelectedByEmergingTrendLane);
        int emergingOverflowCount = telemetryRows.Count(x => x.Decision.StartsWith("REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
        int liquidityTier2EligibleCount = telemetryRows.Count(x => x.EligibleForLiquidityTier2Lane);
        int liquidityTier2SelectedCount = telemetryRows.Count(x => x.SelectedByLiquidityTier2Lane);
        int liquidityTier2OverflowCount = telemetryRows.Count(x => x.Decision.StartsWith("REJECT: liquidity tier-2 lane overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 17 — PRE-TRADE / REGIME GATE TELEMETRY");
        sb.AppendLine("============================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PUBLISH PATH SIGNATURE");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("PATCH_27_LIQUIDITY_NEAR_MISS_TIER2_LANE");
        sb.AppendLine("SOURCE = PreTradeMarketSelectionService.SelectMarkets");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("CONFIGURATION");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"TopN Leadership Set                 : {topN}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Min Average Dollar Volume           : {MinAverageDollarVolume:N0}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Min Average Absolute Return         : {MinAverageAbsoluteReturn:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"High Vol Threshold                  : {HighVolThreshold:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Max Trend Extension                 : {MaxTrendExtension:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Emerging Trend Max Markets          : {EmergingTrendMaxMarkets}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Emerging Trend Min Leadership       : {EmergingTrendMinLeadershipScore:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Emerging Trend Min Avg $ Volume     : {EmergingTrendMinAverageDollarVolume:N0}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Emerging Trend Min Avg Abs Return   : {EmergingTrendMinAverageAbsoluteReturn:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Emerging Trend Max Extension        : {EmergingTrendMaxTrendExtension:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Emerging Trend Range Score Floor    : {EmergingTrendRangeScoreFloor:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Liquidity Tier2 Max Markets         : {LiquidityTier2MaxMarkets}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Liquidity Tier2 Min Avg $ Volume    : {LiquidityTier2MinAverageDollarVolume:N0}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Liquidity Tier2 Min Avg Abs Return  : {LiquidityTier2MinAverageAbsoluteReturn:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Liquidity Tier2 Min Leadership      : {LiquidityTier2MinLeadershipScore:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Liquidity Tier2 Max Extension       : {LiquidityTier2MaxTrendExtension:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Liquidity Tier2 Score Floor         : {LiquidityTier2ScoreFloor:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("FUNNEL TELEMETRY");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Raw Candidate Universe              : {totalUniverse}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Passed Structural Gates             : {acceptedPreTopNCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Selected Final TopN                 : {selectedCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Rejected: insufficient history      : {insufficientHistoryCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Rejected: low liquidity             : {lowLiquidityCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Rejected: dead / low volatility     : {lowVolCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Rejected: regime                    : {regimeRejectCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Rejected: overextended trend        : {extensionRejectCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Rejected: outside topN              : {outsideTopNCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Emerging Lane Eligible              : {emergingEligibleCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Emerging Lane Selected              : {emergingSelectedCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Emerging Lane Overflow Rejects      : {emergingOverflowCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Liquidity Tier2 Eligible            : {liquidityTier2EligibleCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Liquidity Tier2 Selected            : {liquidityTier2SelectedCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Liquidity Tier2 Overflow Rejects    : {liquidityTier2OverflowCount}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("REJECTION BUCKET COUNTS");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------");
        foreach (var bucket in telemetryRows
                     .GroupBy(x => x.Decision)
                     .OrderByDescending(g => g.Count())
                     .ThenBy(g => g.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"{bucket.Key,-48} {bucket.Count(),6}");
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("REGIME STATE COUNTS");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------");
        foreach (var bucket in telemetryRows
                     .GroupBy(x => x.RegimeState.ToString())
                     .OrderByDescending(g => g.Count())
                     .ThenBy(g => g.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"{bucket.Key,-20} {bucket.Count(),6}");
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("SELECTED MARKETS");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------");
        if (selectedMarkets.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO SELECTED MARKETS");
        }
        else
        {
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var row in selectedMarkets.OrderByDescending(x => x.Score))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{rank,2}. {row.Market.Symbol}::{row.Market.Timeframe,-4} " +
                    $"score={row.Score,8:F4} " +
                    $"liq={row.AverageDollarVolume,14:N0} " +
                    $"vol={row.AverageAbsoluteReturn,8:F4} " +
                    $"regime={row.RegimeLabel,-30} " +
                    $"extension={row.TrendExtension,7:F4} " +
                    $"source={row.SourceLane}");
                rank++;
            }
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("EMERGING TREND LANE SELECTED");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------------");
        var emergingSelectedRows = telemetryRows
            .Where(x => x.SelectedByEmergingTrendLane)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.FinalScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.LeadershipScore)
            .ToList();

        if (emergingSelectedRows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO EMERGING TREND LANE SELECTIONS");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var row in emergingSelectedRows)
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.Market.Symbol}::{row.Market.Timeframe,-4} " +
                    $"regime={row.RegimeState,-12} " +
                    $"score={row.FinalScore,8:F4} " +
                    $"lead={row.LeadershipScore,8:F4} " +
                    $"liq={row.AverageDollarVolume,14:N0} " +
                    $"vol={row.AverageAbsoluteReturn,8:F4} " +
                    $"extension={row.TrendExtension,7:F4}");
            }
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("LIQUIDITY TIER2 LANE SELECTED");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------");
        var liquidityTier2SelectedRows = telemetryRows
            .Where(x => x.SelectedByLiquidityTier2Lane)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.FinalScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.LeadershipScore)
            .ToList();

        if (liquidityTier2SelectedRows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO LIQUIDITY TIER2 LANE SELECTIONS");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var row in liquidityTier2SelectedRows)
            {
                decimal gap = Math.Max(0m, MinAverageDollarVolume - row.AverageDollarVolume);
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.Market.Symbol}::{row.Market.Timeframe,-4} " +
                    $"regime={row.RegimeState,-12} " +
                    $"score={row.FinalScore,8:F4} " +
                    $"lead={row.LeadershipScore,8:F4} " +
                    $"liq={row.AverageDollarVolume,14:N0} " +
                    $"liqGap={gap,10:N0} " +
                    $"vol={row.AverageAbsoluteReturn,8:F4} " +
                    $"extension={row.TrendExtension,7:F4}");
            }
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("TOP REGIME NEAR MISSES");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        var regimeNearMisses = telemetryRows
            .Where(x => x.Decision.Equals("REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                        x.Decision.StartsWith("REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                        x.Decision.StartsWith("SELECTED: " + EmergingTrendLaneLabel, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.FinalScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.LeadershipScore)
            .Take(15)
            .ToList();

        if (regimeNearMisses.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO REGIME NEAR MISSES");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var row in regimeNearMisses)
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.Market.Symbol}::{row.Market.Timeframe,-4} " +
                    $"regime={row.RegimeState,-12} " +
                    $"score={row.FinalScore,8:F4} " +
                    $"lead={row.LeadershipScore,8:F4} " +
                    $"liq={row.AverageDollarVolume,14:N0} " +
                    $"vol={row.AverageAbsoluteReturn,8:F4} " +
                    $"extension={row.TrendExtension,7:F4} " +
                    $"eligible={(row.EligibleForEmergingTrendLane ? "YES" : "NO ")} " +
                    $"=> {row.Decision}");
            }
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("TOP LIQUIDITY NEAR MISSES");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");
        var liquidityNearMisses = telemetryRows
            .Where(x => x.Decision.Equals("REJECT: low liquidity", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                        x.Decision.StartsWith("REJECT: liquidity tier-2 lane overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                        x.Decision.StartsWith("SELECTED: " + LiquidityTier2LaneLabel, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.AverageDollarVolume)
            .Take(15)
            .ToList();

        if (liquidityNearMisses.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO LIQUIDITY NEAR MISSES");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var row in liquidityNearMisses)
            {
                decimal gap = Math.Max(0m, MinAverageDollarVolume - row.AverageDollarVolume);
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.Market.Symbol}::{row.Market.Timeframe,-4} " +
                    $"liq={row.AverageDollarVolume,14:N0} " +
                    $"gap={gap,14:N0} " +
                    $"score={row.FinalScore,8:F4} " +
                    $"regime={row.RegimeState,-12} " +
                    $"vol={row.AverageAbsoluteReturn,8:F4} " +
                    $"eligible={(row.EligibleForLiquidityTier2Lane ? "YES" : "NO ")} " +
                    $"=> {row.Decision}");
            }
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("TOP EXTENSION NEAR MISSES");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");
        var extensionNearMisses = telemetryRows
            .Where(x => x.Decision.Equals("REJECT: late / overextended trend", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .OrderBy(x => x.TrendExtension)
            .Take(15)
            .ToList();

        if (extensionNearMisses.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO EXTENSION NEAR MISSES");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var row in extensionNearMisses)
            {
                decimal gap = Math.Max(0m, row.TrendExtension - MaxTrendExtension);
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.Market.Symbol}::{row.Market.Timeframe,-4} " +
                    $"extension={row.TrendExtension,8:F4} " +
                    $"gap={gap,8:F4} " +
                    $"score={row.FinalScore,8:F4} " +
                    $"regime={row.RegimeState,-12} " +
                    $"liq={row.AverageDollarVolume,14:N0}");
            }
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("FULL TELEMETRY TABLE");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("Market               Candles  LiqPass  VolPass  RegPass  ExtPass  Regime        LeadScore  FinalScore  Avg$Vol        AvgAbsRet  Extension  EmgElig  EmgSel  LiqElig  LiqSel  Decision");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------  -------  -------  -------  -------  -------  ------------  ---------  ----------  -------------  ---------  ---------  -------  ------  -------  ------  ----------------------------------------");

        foreach (var row in telemetryRows
                     .OrderByDescending(x => x.SelectedTopN)
                     .ThenByDescending(x => x.FinalScore)
                     .ThenBy(x => x.Market.Symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                     .ThenBy(x => x.Market.Timeframe, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            sb.AppendLine(
                $"{($"{row.Market.Symbol}::{row.Market.Timeframe}"),-19} " +
                $"{row.CandleCount,7}  " +
                $"{(row.PassedLiquidity ? "YES" : "NO "),7}  " +
                $"{(row.PassedVolatility ? "YES" : "NO "),7}  " +
                $"{(row.PassedRegime ? "YES" : "NO "),7}  " +
                $"{(row.PassedExtension ? "YES" : "NO "),7}  " +
                $"{row.RegimeState,-12}  " +
                $"{row.LeadershipScore,9:F4}  " +
                $"{row.FinalScore,10:F4}  " +
                $"{row.AverageDollarVolume,13:N0}  " +
                $"{row.AverageAbsoluteReturn,9:F4}  " +
                $"{row.TrendExtension,9:F4}  " +
                $"{(row.EligibleForEmergingTrendLane ? "YES" : "NO "),7}  " +
                $"{(row.SelectedByEmergingTrendLane ? "YES" : "NO "),6}  " +
                $"{(row.EligibleForLiquidityTier2Lane ? "YES" : "NO "),7}  " +
                $"{(row.SelectedByLiquidityTier2Lane ? "YES" : "NO "),6}  " +
                $"{row.Decision}");
        }

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static decimal GetTimeframeBonus(string timeframe)
    {
        return timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            ? 0.20m
            : timeframe.Equals("1h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                ? 0.05m
                : 0.00m;
    }

    private static decimal ComputeAverageAbsoluteReturn(IReadOnlyList candles)
    {
        if (candles.Count < 2)
            return 0m;

        decimal sum = 0m;
        int n = 0;

        for (int i = 1; i < candles.Count; i++)
        {
            var prev = candles[i - 1].Close;
            var cur = candles[i].Close;
            if (prev == 0m)
                continue;

            sum += Math.Abs((cur - prev) / prev);
            n++;
        }

        return n == 0 ? 0m : sum / n;
    }

    private static MarketTrendState ComputeTrendState(IReadOnlyList candles)
    {
        var closes = candles.Select(c => c.Close).ToList();
        if (closes.Count < 120)
            return MarketTrendState.Unknown;

        var emaFast = closes.TakeLast(21).Average();
        var emaMid = closes.TakeLast(50).Average();
        var emaSlow = closes.TakeLast(120).Average();

        var avgAbsRet = ComputeAverageAbsoluteReturn(candles);

        bool trendUp = emaFast > emaMid && emaMid > emaSlow;
        bool trendDown = emaFast < emaMid && emaMid < emaSlow;
        bool highVol = avgAbsRet >= HighVolThreshold;

        if (trendUp && highVol) return MarketTrendState.HighVolUp;
        if (trendUp) return MarketTrendState.TrendUp;
        if (trendDown && highVol) return MarketTrendState.HighVolDown;
        if (trendDown) return MarketTrendState.TrendDown;
        return MarketTrendState.Range;
    }

    private static decimal ComputeTrendExtension(IReadOnlyList candles)
    {
        var closes = candles.Select(c => c.Close).ToList();
        if (closes.Count < 120)
            return 0m;

        var last = closes[^1];
        var baseline = closes.TakeLast(120).Average();

        if (baseline == 0m)
            return 0m;

        return Math.Abs((last - baseline) / baseline);
    }

    public sealed record SelectionResult(
        IReadOnlyList SelectedMarkets,
        IReadOnlyDictionary RejectedMarkets);

    public sealed record SelectedMarket(
        MarketKey Market,
        decimal Score,
        decimal AverageDollarVolume,
        decimal AverageAbsoluteReturn,
        string RegimeLabel,
        decimal TrendExtension,
        string SourceLane);

    private sealed class PreTradeTelemetryRow
    {
        public required MarketKey Market { get; init; }
        public int CandleCount { get; init; }
        public decimal AverageDollarVolume { get; init; }
        public decimal AverageAbsoluteReturn { get; init; }
        public decimal LeadershipScore { get; init; }
        public decimal TimeframeBonus { get; init; }
        public decimal RegimeBonus { get; init; }
        public decimal TrendExtension { get; init; }
        public decimal FinalScore { get; set; }
        public MarketTrendState RegimeState { get; init; }
        public string Decision { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public bool PassedHistory { get; init; }
        public bool PassedLiquidity { get; init; }
        public bool PassedVolatility { get; init; }
        public bool PassedRegime { get; init; }
        public bool PassedExtension { get; init; }
        public bool EligibleForEmergingTrendLane { get; init; }
        public bool SelectedByEmergingTrendLane { get; set; }
        public bool EligibleForLiquidityTier2Lane { get; init; }
        public bool SelectedByLiquidityTier2Lane { get; set; }
        public bool SelectedTopN { get; set; }
    }

    private enum MarketTrendState
    {
        Unknown = 0,
        Range = 1,
        TrendUp = 2,
        TrendDown = 3,
        HighVolUp = 4,
        HighVolDown = 5
    }
}

 using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
using TQGA.Application.Accounting;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Strategy;

namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio;

public sealed class StrategyBacktestNode
{
    public int StrategyId { get; }
    public string StrategyName { get; }

    public TradeLedger Ledger { get; }
    public EquityCurve Equity { get; }

    public StrategyBacktestNode(
        int id,
        string name,
        TradeLedger ledger,
        EquityCurve equity)
    {
        StrategyId = id;
        StrategyName = name;
        Ledger = ledger;
        Equity = equity;
    }

    public decimal FinalPnL => Ledger.TotalPnL;
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using TQGA.Application.Risk;

namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio;

public sealed class StrategyCapitalAllocator : ICapitalAllocator
{
    private decimal _portfolioEquity;
    private decimal _strategyWeight;
    private decimal _strategyEquity;

    private const decimal RiskPerTrade = 0.01m; // 1%

    public decimal CurrentEquity => _strategyEquity;

    public void Seed(decimal portfolioCapital, decimal strategyWeight)
    {
        _portfolioEquity = portfolioCapital;
        _strategyWeight = strategyWeight;
        _strategyEquity = _portfolioEquity * _strategyWeight;
    }

    public decimal GetOrderSize(string symbol, decimal price)
    {
        if (price <= 0 || _strategyEquity <= 0)
            return 0;

        var riskCapital = _strategyEquity * RiskPerTrade;

        return riskCapital / price;
    }

    public void OnTradeClosed(decimal pnl)
    {
        _strategyEquity += pnl;
        _portfolioEquity += pnl;
    }

    public decimal GetAllocatedCapital()
        => _portfolioEquity * _strategyWeight;

    public decimal GetWeight()
        => _strategyWeight;
}

 using TQGA.Application.Accounting;

namespace TQGA.Application.Reporting;

public sealed class BacktestReport
{
    public decimal TotalPnL { get; }
    public int TotalTrades { get; }
    public int Wins { get; }
    public int Losses { get; }
    public decimal WinRate { get; }
    public decimal MaxDrawdown { get; }

    public BacktestReport(
        TradeLedger ledger,
        EquityCurve equity)
    {
        TotalPnL = ledger.TotalPnL;
        TotalTrades = ledger.TotalTrades;
        Wins = ledger.WinCount;
        Losses = ledger.LossCount;

        WinRate = TotalTrades == 0
            ? 0
            : (decimal)Wins / TotalTrades * 100m;

        MaxDrawdown = CalculateMaxDrawdown(equity.Points);
    }

    private static decimal CalculateMaxDrawdown(
        IReadOnlyList<(DateTime Time, decimal Value)> points)
    {
        decimal peak = decimal.MinValue;
        decimal maxDd = 0m;

        foreach (var p in points)
        {
            if (p.Value > peak)
                peak = p.Value;

            if (peak == 0)
                continue;

            var dd = (peak - p.Value) / peak * 100m;

            if (dd > maxDd)
                maxDd = dd;
        }

        return maxDd;
    }

    public override string ToString()
    {
        return
            $"Total Trades : {TotalTrades}\n" +
            $"Wins         : {Wins}\n" +
            $"Losses       : {Losses}\n" +
            $"Win Rate     : {WinRate:F2}%\n" +
            $"Total PnL    : {TotalPnL:F2}\n" +
            $"Max Drawdown : {MaxDrawdown:F2}";
    }
}

 F I L E :   D : \ D   D A T A   B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ R e p o r t i n g \ C o i n P e r f o r m a n c e A n a l y z e r . c s 
 
 T Y P E :   . c s 
 
 S I Z E :   2 . 6   K B 
 
 L I N E S :   5 9 
 
 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using TQGA.Domain.Trading;

namespace TQGA.Application.Reporting;

public sealed class CoinPerformanceAnalyzer
{
    private readonly IReadOnlyList _trades;

    public CoinPerformanceAnalyzer(IReadOnlyList trades)
    {
        _trades = trades.Where(t => t.IsClosed).ToList();
    }

    public string BuildReport()
    {
        if (_trades.Count == 0)
            return "\nNo closed trades → coin analytics unavailable.\n";

        var grouped = _trades
            .GroupBy(t => t.Symbol)
            .Select(g =>
            {
                var trades = g.ToList();

                var wins = trades.Where(t => t.RealizedPnL > 0).ToList();
                var losses = trades.Where(t => t.RealizedPnL < 0).ToList();

                var total = trades.Count;

                var pnl = trades.Sum(t => t.RealizedPnL);

                var avgWin = wins.Any() ? wins.Average(t => t.RealizedPnL) : 0;
                var avgLoss = losses.Any() ? losses.Average(t => t.RealizedPnL) : 0;

                var winRate = total == 0 ? 0 : (decimal)wins.Count / total;

                var grossWin = wins.Sum(t => t.RealizedPnL);
                var grossLoss = losses.Sum(t => Math.Abs(t.RealizedPnL));

                var pf = grossLoss == 0 ? 0 : grossWin / grossLoss;

                var expectancy =
                    (winRate * avgWin) -
                    ((1 - winRate) * Math.Abs(avgLoss));

                return new
                {
                    Symbol = g.Key,
                    Trades = total,
                    PnL = pnl,
                    WinRate = winRate * 100,
                    AvgWin = avgWin,
                    AvgLoss = avgLoss,
                    PF = pf,
                    Expectancy = expectancy
                };
            })
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Expectancy)
            .ToList();

        var lines = new List();

        lines.Add("\n===== COIN PERFORMANCE MATRIX =====\n");
        lines.Add("Symbol | Trades | Win% | PnL | AvgWin | AvgLoss | PF | Expectancy");
        lines.Add("-------------------------------------------------------------------");

        foreach (var x in grouped)
        {
            lines.Add(
                $"{x.Symbol,-7} | {x.Trades,6} | {x.WinRate,5:F1} | {x.PnL,8:F0} | {x.AvgWin,7:F0} | {x.AvgLoss,8:F0} | {x.PF,4:F2} | {x.Expectancy,10:F2}");
        }

        lines.Add("\nTOP ALPHA MARKET → " + grouped.First().Symbol);
        lines.Add("WORST MARKET     → " + grouped.Last().Symbol);

        return string.Join("\n", lines);
    }
}

 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Accounting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;
using TQGA.Domain.Trading;

namespace TQGA.Application.Reporting;

public sealed class PortfolioResearchReport
{
    private readonly TradeLedger _ledger;

    public PortfolioResearchReport(TradeLedger ledger)
    {
        _ledger = ledger;
    }

    public void Generate()
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var timestamp = DateTime.UtcNow.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd_HH-mm-ss");

        var path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT 03_PORTFOLIO_{timestamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("UNIVERSAL PORTFOLIO RESEARCH REPORT");
        sb.AppendLine("===================================");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (!_ledger.Trades.Any())
        {
            sb.AppendLine("⚠ NO TRADES EXECUTED");
            sb.AppendLine("Possible causes:");
            sb.AppendLine("- Entry alignment never occurred");
            sb.AppendLine("- Risk manager blocking");
            sb.AppendLine("- Position already open on signals");
            File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
            return;
        }

        var byCoin = _ledger.Trades
            .GroupBy(t => t.Symbol)
            .Select(g => new
            {
                Symbol = g.Key,
                Trades = g.Count(),
                PnL = g.Sum(x => x.RealizedPnL),
                Wins = g.Count(x => x.RealizedPnL > 0)
            })
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.PnL);

        sb.AppendLine("COIN PERFORMANCE");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------");

        foreach (var c in byCoin)
        {
            var winRate = c.Trades == 0 ? 0 :
                (decimal)c.Wins / c.Trades * 100m;

            sb.AppendLine(
                $"{c.Symbol} | Trades: {c.Trades} | PnL: {c.PnL:F2} | WinRate: {winRate:F2}%");
        }

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }
}

        var path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,

        sb.AppendLine("TQGA STRATEGY EXPLAINABILITY REPORT");
        sb.AppendLine("=================================");
        sb.AppendLine($"Generated (UTC): {DateTime.UtcNow}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("STRATEGY OVERVIEW");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        sb.AppendLine(
            "This strategy combines EMA trend direction with RSI momentum filtering. " +
            "Trades are only allowed when market structure, momentum, and risk rules " +
            "are aligned. The system intentionally avoids over-trading."
        );
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("WHY TRADES MAY NOT OCCUR");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine(
            "- EMA trend not clearly aligned\n" +
            "- RSI not in momentum confirmation zone\n" +
            "- Risk manager blocking entries\n" +
            "- Existing open position prevents re-entry\n" +
            "- Strategy prefers inactivity over low-quality signals"
        );
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("STRATEGY SCORECARD");

        sb.AppendLine("RSI Momentum Filter     : 100 / 100");
        sb.AppendLine("Risk Alignment          : 100 / 100");
        sb.AppendLine("Timing Discipline       : 100 / 100");
        sb.AppendLine("Noise Protection        : 100 / 100");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("ADVANCED KPI INSIGHT");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------------");
        sb.AppendLine(
            "- Signal Selectivity      : High\n" +
            "- Trade Frequency Control : Strict\n" +
            "- Overfitting Resistance  : Strong\n" +
            "- R-Multiple Philosophy   : Expectancy driven, not win-rate driven\n"
        );

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }
}

 using TQGA.Domain.Trading;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;
namespace TQGA.Application.Reporting;

public static class TradeCsvExporter
{
    public static void Export(
        IEnumerable trades,
        string fileName)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports, fileName);

        using var writer = new StreamWriter(path);

        writer.WriteLine(
            "Symbol,Side,Quantity,EntryTime,EntryPrice,ExitTime,ExitPrice,PnL");

        foreach (var t in trades)
        {
            writer.WriteLine(
                $"{t.Symbol},{t.Side},{t.Quantity},{t.EntryTime},{t.EntryPrice},{t.ExitTime},{t.ExitPrice},{t.RealizedPnL}");
        }
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using TQGA.Domain.Trading;

namespace TQGA.Application.Reporting;

public sealed class TradeExpectancyAnalyzer
{
    public decimal Expectancy { get; }
    public decimal AvgWin { get; }
    public decimal AvgLoss { get; }
    public decimal ProfitFactor { get; }
    public decimal WinRate { get; }
    public int TotalTrades { get; }

    public TradeExpectancyAnalyzer(IReadOnlyList trades)
    {
        var closed = trades.Where(t => t.IsClosed).ToList();

        TotalTrades = closed.Count;

        if (TotalTrades == 0)
            return;

        var wins = closed.Where(t => t.RealizedPnL > 0).ToList();
        var losses = closed.Where(t => t.RealizedPnL < 0).ToList();

        AvgWin = wins.Any() ? wins.Average(t => t.RealizedPnL) : 0;
        AvgLoss = losses.Any() ? losses.Average(t => t.RealizedPnL) : 0;

        WinRate = (decimal)wins.Count / TotalTrades;

        var grossWin = wins.Sum(t => t.RealizedPnL);
        var grossLoss = losses.Sum(t => Math.Abs(t.RealizedPnL));

        ProfitFactor = grossLoss == 0 ? 0 : grossWin / grossLoss;

        Expectancy =
            (WinRate * AvgWin) -
            ((1 - WinRate) * Math.Abs(AvgLoss));
    }

    public override string ToString()
    {
        return
            "\n====== EXPECTANCY REPORT ======\n" +
            $"Total Trades  : {TotalTrades}\n" +
            $"Win Rate      : {WinRate:P2}\n" +
            $"Avg Win       : {AvgWin:F2}\n" +
            $"Avg Loss      : {AvgLoss:F2}\n" +
            $"Profit Factor : {ProfitFactor:F2}\n" +
            $"Expectancy    : {Expectancy:F2}\n" +
            "===============================\n";
    }
}

 using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

/// 
/// Alpha decay monitoring using portfolio equity timeline only.
/// PATCH 10A:
/// Remove A84 ID collisions.
/// - CIO Rating exclusively owns A84_03 via A84_03_CIO_RATING
/// - Growth Projection exclusively owns A84_04 via A84_04_GROWTH_PROJECTION
/// Therefore this service now writes unique non-colliding IDs:
/// - A84_07_ALPHA_DECAY_PORTFOLIO
/// - A84_08_ALPHA_DECAY_ALERTS
/// 
public sealed class A84AlphaDecayMonitoringReportService
{
    public void Generate(PortfolioBacktestResult result)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var equity = result?.PortfolioEquityTimeline;
        if (equity == null || equity.Count < 20)
        {
            Write(
                "A84_07_ALPHA_DECAY_PORTFOLIO",
                "A84_07 — ALPHA DECAY (PORTFOLIO)",
                "NO DATA: PortfolioEquityTimeline is missing or too small.");

            Write(
                "A84_08_ALPHA_DECAY_ALERTS",
                "A84_08 — ALPHA DECAY (ALERTS)",
                "NO DATA: PortfolioEquityTimeline is missing or too small.");

            return;
        }

        var pts = equity
            .OrderBy(x => x.Key)
            .Select(x => (t: x.Key, v: x.Value))
            .ToList();

        var half = pts.Count / 2;
        var early = pts.Take(half).ToList();
        var late = pts.Skip(half).ToList();

        var earlyRet = SegmentReturn(early);
        var lateRet = SegmentReturn(late);

        var decayScan = RollingDecayScan(
            pts,
            window: Math.Max(20, pts.Count / 10));

        var sb = new StringBuilder();
        sb.AppendLine("A84_07 — ALPHA DECAY (PORTFOLIO)");
        sb.AppendLine("================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine($"Total Points          : {pts.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Early Half Return     : {earlyRet:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Late Half Return      : {lateRet:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Decay Delta           : {(lateRet - earlyRet):P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (lateRet < earlyRet)
            sb.AppendLine("Assessment            : Alpha decay detected (late period weaker than early period).");
        else
            sb.AppendLine("Assessment            : No alpha decay detected by half-split comparison.");

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("ROLLING WINDOW DECAY SCAN");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");

        if (decayScan.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("No rolling scan windows were available.");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var row in decayScan.TakeLast(20))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.EndUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} UTC | " +
                    $"Window Return: {row.WindowReturn:P2} | " +
                    $"Peak-to-Trough DD: {row.MaxDrawdown:P2}");
            }
        }

        Write("A84_07_ALPHA_DECAY_PORTFOLIO", sb);

        var alerts = new StringBuilder();
        alerts.AppendLine("A84_08 — ALPHA DECAY (ALERTS)");
        alerts.AppendLine("=============================");
        alerts.AppendLine();

        bool decayDetected = lateRet < earlyRet;
        bool severeDecay = (earlyRet - lateRet) >= 0.10m;
        bool rollingWeakness = decayScan.Count > 0 &&
                               decayScan.Count(x => x.WindowReturn < 0m) >= Math.Max(3, decayScan.Count / 3);

        alerts.AppendLine($"Decay Detected        : {(decayDetected ? "YES" : "NO")}");
        alerts.AppendLine($"Severe Decay          : {(severeDecay ? "YES" : "NO")}");
        alerts.AppendLine($"Rolling Weakness      : {(rollingWeakness ? "YES" : "NO")}");
        alerts.AppendLine();

        alerts.AppendLine("ALERT SUMMARY");
        alerts.AppendLine("-------------");

        if (!decayDetected && !rollingWeakness)
        {
            alerts.AppendLine("No major alpha decay alerts triggered.");
        }
        else
        {
            if (decayDetected)
                alerts.AppendLine("- Late-half performance is weaker than early-half performance.");

            if (severeDecay)
                alerts.AppendLine("- Decay magnitude is severe by half-split comparison.");

            if (rollingWeakness)
                alerts.AppendLine("- Rolling window scan shows repeated recent weakness.");
        }

        alerts.AppendLine();
        alerts.AppendLine("OPERATIONAL GUIDANCE");
        alerts.AppendLine("--------------------");

        if (severeDecay || rollingWeakness)
        {
            alerts.AppendLine("- Review strategy ranking and top-N execution policy.");
            alerts.AppendLine("- Check whether edge concentration is too narrow.");
            alerts.AppendLine("- Investigate whether recent market regime differs from training period.");
            alerts.AppendLine("- Tighten gating for weak strategies if decay persists.");
        }
        else if (decayDetected)
        {
            alerts.AppendLine("- Monitor next run closely for continued deterioration.");
            alerts.AppendLine("- Compare top symbols/timeframes between early and late segments.");
        }
        else
        {
            alerts.AppendLine("- Continue monitoring; no immediate alpha-decay intervention required.");
        }

        Write("A84_08_ALPHA_DECAY_ALERTS", alerts);
    }

    private static decimal SegmentReturn(List<(DateTime t, decimal v)> pts)
    {
        if (pts == null || pts.Count < 2)
            return 0m;

        var start = pts.First().v;
        var end = pts.Last().v;

        if (start <= 0m)
            return 0m;

        return (end / start) - 1m;
    }

    private static List RollingDecayScan(
        List<(DateTime t, decimal v)> pts,
        int window)
    {
        var output = new List();

        if (pts == null || pts.Count < 2 || window < 2 || pts.Count < window)
            return output;

        for (int i = window - 1; i < pts.Count; i++)
        {
            var slice = pts.Skip(i - window + 1).Take(window).ToList();
            var start = slice.First().v;
            var end = slice.Last().v;

            decimal ret = 0m;
            if (start > 0m)
                ret = (end / start) - 1m;

            decimal peak = decimal.MinValue;
            decimal maxDd = 0m;

            foreach (var p in slice)
            {
                if (p.v > peak)
                    peak = p.v;

                if (peak > 0m)
                {
                    var dd = (p.v / peak) - 1m;
                    if (dd < maxDd)
                        maxDd = dd;
                }
            }

            output.Add(new DecayWindowRow
            {
                EndUtc = slice.Last().t,
                WindowReturn = ret,
                MaxDrawdown = maxDd
            });
        }

        return output;
    }

    private static void Write(string name, string title, string body)
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();
        sb.AppendLine(title);
        sb.AppendLine(new string('=', title.Length));
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine(body);

        Write(name, sb);
    }

    private static void Write(string name, StringBuilder sb)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        File.WriteAllText(
            Path.Combine(
                DataPaths.Reports,
                $"{name}_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt"),
            sb.ToString());
    }

    private sealed class DecayWindowRow
    {
        public DateTime EndUtc { get; init; }
        public decimal WindowReturn { get; init; }
        public decimal MaxDrawdown { get; init; }
    }
}
