 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

/// 
/// Produces a compact (ChatGPT-paste-friendly) summary of the key system outputs.
/// Target size: ~3–4 KB, with 5–10 lines per major section.
/// 
public sealed class A84ChatGptUploadReportService
{
    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyList selectedStrategies,
        Dictionary? fitness,
        HashSet? allowedStrategyIds,
        Dictionary? cioWeightsPostGating)
    {
        if (result == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(result));
        if (selectedStrategies == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(selectedStrategies));

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        fitness ??= new Dictionary();
        allowedStrategyIds ??= new HashSet();
        cioWeightsPostGating ??= new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        var sb = new StringBuilder(capacity: 5000);

        var ts = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        var outFile = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"A84_06_CHATGPT_UPLOAD_{runUtc:yyyyMMdd}_{ts}.txt".Replace($"{runUtc:yyyyMMdd}_{runUtc:yyyyMMdd}", runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd")));

        // ---------- Header ----------
        sb.AppendLine("A84_06 — CHATGPT UPLOAD (COMPACT)");
        sb.AppendLine("================================");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC) : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        // ---------- Architecture state ----------
        sb.AppendLine("TQGA — ARCHITECTURE STATE (Institutional Mode)");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("• Market grid: Top20 symbols × 3 TF (1h, 4h, 1d) => 60 markets.");
        sb.AppendLine("• Backtest: Strategy × Market grid; captures StrategyPnL, SymbolPnL, Symbol×TF PnL, Strategy×Symbol×TF PnL.");
        sb.AppendLine("• CIO: ranks markets by PnL score (per Symbol×TF) then allocates with caps (per-market + per-symbol).");
        sb.AppendLine("• Fitness gating: kills dead strategies (0 trades / low PnL / fitness<=0) before CIO recompute.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        // ---------- Run scope ----------
        sb.AppendLine("RUN SCOPE");
        sb.AppendLine("---------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Strategies Selected : {selectedStrategies.Count}");
        for (int i = 0; i < Math.Min(10, selectedStrategies.Count); i++)
            sb.AppendLine($"  S{i + 1:00}  {selectedStrategies[i].Name}");
        if (selectedStrategies.Count > 10) sb.AppendLine("  ...");
        sb.AppendLine();

        // ---------- Portfolio snapshot ----------
        sb.AppendLine("PORTFOLIO SNAPSHOT");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------");
        var startEq = 100000m;
        var endEq = TryGetEndEquity(result, startEq);
        var retPct = startEq <= 0 ? 0m : ((endEq - startEq) / startEq) * 100m;

        sb.AppendLine($"Start Equity : {startEq:0.00}");
        sb.AppendLine($"End Equity   : {endEq:0.00}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Total Return : {retPct:0.00}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"Equity Points: {result.PortfolioEquityTimeline?.Count ?? 0}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        // ---------- Top strategies ----------
        sb.AppendLine("TOP STRATEGIES (PnL)");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------------");
        foreach (var x in (result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary())
                     .OrderByDescending(k => k.Value)
                     .Take(6))
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"S{x.Key:00}  PnL {x.Value:0.00}");
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        // ---------- Fitness / gating ----------
        sb.AppendLine("FITNESS GATING (summary)");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------");
        if (fitness.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("No fitness snapshot available.");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var row in fitness.Values
                         .OrderByDescending(r => r.FitnessScore)
                         .Take(6))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{row.StrategyCode} | PnL {row.PnL:0.00} | Trades {row.Trades} | Fit {row.FitnessScore:0.000} | Allowed {row.Allowed} | {row.GateReason}");
            }

            sb.AppendLine($"Allowed Strategies: {(allowedStrategyIds.Count == 0 ? "NONE" : string.Join(",", allowedStrategyIds.OrderBy(x => x).Select(x => $"S{x:00}")))}");
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        // ---------- Top markets ----------
        sb.AppendLine("TOP MARKETS (Symbol×TF PnL)");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------");
        foreach (var kv in (result.SymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                     .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
                     .Take(10))
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key}  PnL {kv.Value:0.00}");
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        // ---------- CIO allocation post-gating ----------
        sb.AppendLine("CIO ALLOCATION (POST-GATING, Top 10)");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------------");
        if (cioWeightsPostGating.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("No CIO post-gating weights available.");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var kv in cioWeightsPostGating
                         .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
                         .Take(10))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key}  W {(kv.Value * 100m):0.00}%");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        // ---------- Walk-forward + realism checklist ----------
        sb.AppendLine("REALISM / SURVIVAL CHECKLIST (minimum)");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("• Walk-forward: split history into sequential windows; tune on train, validate on next window only.");
        sb.AppendLine("• Friction: add fees + slippage + spread; stress with 2× and 4× friction multipliers.");
        sb.AppendLine("• Regime robustness: require stable performance across multiple regime buckets (trend/range/volatile).");
        sb.AppendLine("• Risk limits: max exposure per symbol, max drawdown stop, and kill-switch for degraded fitness.");
        sb.AppendLine("• No-leakage: indicators must use only past candles; avoid using final equity to pick parameters.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        // ---------- What to upload ----------
        sb.AppendLine("WHAT TO UPLOAD TO CHATGPT");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("1) This file (A84_06_CHATGPT_UPLOAD)");
        sb.AppendLine("2) A84_00 Executive Summary");
        sb.AppendLine("3) A84_05 Strategy Fitness + CIO Gating");
        sb.AppendLine("4) REPORT_11 Symbol×TF PnL and REPORT_12 CIO weights");
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(outFile, sb.ToString(), Encoding.UTF8);
    }

    private static decimal TryGetEndEquity(PortfolioBacktestResult result, decimal fallback)
    {
        if (result.PortfolioEquityTimeline == null || result.PortfolioEquityTimeline.Count == 0)
            return fallback;

        // SortedDictionary => last value is end equity
        return result.PortfolioEquityTimeline.Last().Value;
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class A84ExecutiveSummaryReportService
{
    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyList selectedStrategies,
        Dictionary cioWeightsFinal,
        int recentMinutesWindow = 10)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedStrategies);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(cioWeightsFinal);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var outFile = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"A84_00_EXECUTIVE_SUMMARY_{runUtc:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        // PATCH 14C:
        // Use ONLY real equity timestamps for Start/End time.
        // Never allow DateTime.MinValue to be published.
        var eq = result.PortfolioEquityTimeline ?? new Dictionary();

        var ordered = eq
            .OrderBy(x => x.Key)
            .ToList();

        var realPoints = ordered
            .Where(x => x.Key != DateTime.MinValue)
            .ToList();

        DateTime? startTimeUtc = null;
        DateTime? endTimeUtc = null;
        decimal startEquity = 0m;
        decimal endEquity = 0m;

        if (realPoints.Count > 0)
        {
            startTimeUtc = realPoints.First().Key;
            endTimeUtc = realPoints.Last().Key;
            startEquity = realPoints.First().Value;
            endEquity = realPoints.Last().Value;
        }
        else if (ordered.Count > 0)
        {
            // Only seed/no-real-time case:
            // keep equity values, but publish no fake time.
            startTimeUtc = null;
            endTimeUtc = null;
            startEquity = ordered.First().Value;
            endEquity = ordered.Last().Value;
        }

        var totalReturnPct = startEquity <= 0m
            ? 0m
            : ((endEquity / startEquity) - 1m) * 100m;

        var strategyLines = selectedStrategies
            .Select((t, idx) => $"  S{idx + 1:00}  {t.Name}")
            .ToList();

        var topStrategies = result.StrategyPnL
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .Take(30)
            .Select(x =>
                $"S{x.Key:00}  {PadRightSafe(StrategyNameFromSelection(selectedStrategies, x.Key), 28)}  PnL  {x.Value,14:0.00}")
            .ToList();

        var topMarkets = result.SymbolTimeframePnL
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .Take(30)
            .Select(x =>
                $"{PadRightSafe(x.Key, 22)}  PnL  {x.Value,14:0.00}")
            .ToList();

        var recentFiles = new List();
        try
        {
            if (Directory.Exists(DataPaths.Reports))
            {
                var cutoff = runUtc.AddMinutes(-recentMinutesWindow);

                recentFiles = Directory
                    .GetFiles(DataPaths.Reports)
                    .Select(f => new FileInfo(f))
                    .Where(fi => fi.LastWriteTimeUtc >= cutoff && fi.LastWriteTimeUtc <= runUtc.AddMinutes(1))
                    .OrderByDescending(fi => fi.LastWriteTimeUtc)
                    .Take(50)
                    .Select(fi => $"{fi.LastWriteTimeUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}  {fi.Name}")
                    .ToList();
            }
        }
        catch
        {
            // Best-effort only.
        }

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("A84_00 — EXECUTIVE SUMMARY");
        sb.AppendLine("==========================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PUBLISH PATH SIGNATURE");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("PATCH_14C_A84_00_REAL_FIRST_TIMESTAMP_ONLY");
        sb.AppendLine("WRITER = A84ExecutiveSummaryReportService.GenerateAndWrite");
        sb.AppendLine("RULE   = DateTime.MinValue is never published");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC): {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Strategies Selected: {selectedStrategies.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Equity Points      : {eq.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Start Time (UTC)   : {FormatUtc(startTimeUtc)}");
        sb.AppendLine($"End Time (UTC)     : {FormatUtc(endTimeUtc)}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Start Equity       : {startEquity:0.00}");
        sb.AppendLine($"End Equity         : {endEquity:0.00}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Total Return       : {totalReturnPct:0.00}%");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("POST-GATING CIO SUMMARY");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------");
        if (cioWeightsFinal.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: Canonical CIO weights are empty.");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"Markets Allocated : {cioWeightsFinal.Count}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Top Weight        : {cioWeightsFinal.Values.Max():P2}");
            sb.AppendLine();

            foreach (var kv in cioWeightsFinal
                         .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
                         .Take(10))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{PadRightSafe(kv.Key, 24)}  {kv.Value,10:P2}");
            }
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("STRATEGIES SELECTED");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------");
        if (strategyLines.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NONE");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var line in strategyLines)
                sb.AppendLine(line);
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("TOP STRATEGIES BY PNL");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------");
        if (topStrategies.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var line in topStrategies)
                sb.AppendLine(line);
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("TOP MARKETS BY SYMBOL::TF PNL");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------");
        if (topMarkets.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var line in topMarkets)
                sb.AppendLine(line);
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("RECENT GENERATED FILES");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        if (recentFiles.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO RECENT FILES FOUND IN WINDOW");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var line in recentFiles)
                sb.AppendLine(line);
        }

        File.WriteAllText(outFile, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static string StrategyNameFromSelection(
        IReadOnlyList selectedStrategies,
        int strategyId)
    {
        var idx = strategyId - 1;

        if (idx < 0 || idx >= selectedStrategies.Count)
            return $"Strategy_{strategyId:00}";

        return selectedStrategies[idx].Name;
    }

    private static string PadRightSafe(string value, int totalWidth)
    {
        value ??= string.Empty;

        if (value.Length == totalWidth)
            return value;

        if (value.Length < totalWidth)
            return value.PadRight(totalWidth);

        if (totalWidth <= 3)
            return value[..totalWidth];

        return value[..(totalWidth - 3)] + "...";
    }

    private static string FormatUtc(DateTime? value)
    {
        if (!value.HasValue)
            return "N/A";

        return value.Value.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
    }
}

 S I Z E :   8 . 1 6   K B

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

/// 
/// A84 special reports orchestrator:
/// - A84_01 / A84_02 family coordination
/// - PATCH 15 compile fix:
///   A84_RegimeResearchService.Generate now expects
///   (PortfolioBacktestResult result, Dictionary canonicalCioPostGatingWeights)
///   so this service must pass the full result, not SymbolTimeframePnL.
/// 
public sealed class A84MarketRegimeDetectionReportService
{
    private readonly A84_RegimeResearchService _regime = new();

    public void Generate(PortfolioBacktestResult result)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        if (result == null)
        {
            WriteReportText(
                "A84_01_MARKET_REGIME",
                "A84_01 — MARKET REGIME",
                "NO DATA: PortfolioBacktestResult is null.");

            WriteReportText(
                "A84_02_REGIME_TRANSITIONS",
                "A84_02 — REGIME TRANSITIONS (PORTFOLIO)",
                "NO DATA: PortfolioBacktestResult is null.");

            WriteReportText(
                "A84_02B_REGIME_STATS",
                "A84_02B — REGIME STATS (PORTFOLIO)",
                "NO DATA: PortfolioBacktestResult is null.");

            return;
        }

        // PATCH 15 compile-safe bridge:
        // Prefer the stored canonical post-gating CIO dictionary.
        // If it is empty, fall back to aligned raw CIO weights only for regime-report compatibility.
        var canonicalCio = BuildCanonicalCioForRegime(result);

        // A84_01 / A84_03 / A84_04 family
        _regime.Generate(result, canonicalCio);

        // A84_02 / A84_02B family
        GeneratePortfolioRegimeTransitions(result.PortfolioEquityTimeline);
    }

    private static Dictionary BuildCanonicalCioForRegime(PortfolioBacktestResult result)
    {
        if (result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights != null &&
            result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights.Count > 0)
        {
            return new Dictionary(
                result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights,
                StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        }

        var cioRaw = result.CioSymbolTimeframeWeights ?? new Dictionary();
        var aligned = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        foreach (var kv in cioRaw)
        {
            var key = kv.Key ?? string.Empty;
            var value = kv.Value;

            if (value <= 0m)
                continue;

            if (key.StartsWith("CIO::", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                key = key.Substring("CIO::".Length);

            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(key))
                continue;

            aligned[key] = value;
        }

        var sum = aligned.Values.Sum();
        if (sum > 0m)
        {
            var keys = aligned.Keys.ToList();
            foreach (var k in keys)
                aligned[k] = aligned[k] / sum;
        }

        return aligned;
    }

    private void GeneratePortfolioRegimeTransitions(IReadOnlyDictionary equityTimeline)
    {
        if (equityTimeline == null || equityTimeline.Count < 30)
        {
            WriteReportText(
                "A84_02_REGIME_TRANSITIONS",
                "A84_02 — REGIME TRANSITIONS (PORTFOLIO)",
                "NO DATA: PortfolioEquityTimeline missing or too small.");

            WriteReportText(
                "A84_02B_REGIME_STATS",
                "A84_02B — REGIME STATS (PORTFOLIO)",
                "NO DATA: PortfolioEquityTimeline missing or too small.");

            return;
        }

        var ordered = equityTimeline
            .Where(x => x.Key != DateTime.MinValue)
            .OrderBy(x => x.Key)
            .ToList();

        if (ordered.Count < 30)
        {
            WriteReportText(
                "A84_02_REGIME_TRANSITIONS",
                "A84_02 — REGIME TRANSITIONS (PORTFOLIO)",
                "NO DATA: Real PortfolioEquityTimeline points are too small after removing seed marker.");

            WriteReportText(
                "A84_02B_REGIME_STATS",
                "A84_02B — REGIME STATS (PORTFOLIO)",
                "NO DATA: Real PortfolioEquityTimeline points are too small after removing seed marker.");

            return;
        }

        var transitionsSb = new StringBuilder();
        transitionsSb.AppendLine("A84_02 — REGIME TRANSITIONS (PORTFOLIO)");
        transitionsSb.AppendLine("=======================================");
        transitionsSb.AppendLine();

        var stats = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        string? prevState = null;
        int transitionCount = 0;

        // Simple rolling regime detector using 20-point lookback.
        for (int i = 20; i < ordered.Count; i++)
        {
            var window = ordered.Skip(i - 20).Take(20).ToList();
            var state = DetectPortfolioState(window);

            if (!stats.ContainsKey(state))
                stats[state] = 0;
            stats[state]++;

            if (prevState != null && !string.Equals(prevState, state, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                transitionCount++;
                transitionsSb.AppendLine(
                    $"{ordered[i].Key:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} | {prevState} -> {state}");
            }

            prevState = state;
        }

        if (transitionCount == 0)
            transitionsSb.AppendLine("NO TRANSITIONS DETECTED UNDER CURRENT RULES.");

        WriteRaw("A84_02_REGIME_TRANSITIONS", transitionsSb.ToString());

        var statsSb = new StringBuilder();
        statsSb.AppendLine("A84_02B — REGIME STATS (PORTFOLIO)");
        statsSb.AppendLine("==================================");
        statsSb.AppendLine();
        statsSb.AppendLine($"Real Equity Points : {ordered.Count}");
        statsSb.AppendLine($"Transition Count   : {transitionCount}");
        statsSb.AppendLine();

        statsSb.AppendLine("STATE COUNTS");
        statsSb.AppendLine("------------");

        foreach (var kv in stats.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
            statsSb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-16} {kv.Value,8}");

        WriteRaw("A84_02B_REGIME_STATS", statsSb.ToString());
    }

    private static string DetectPortfolioState(List> window)
    {
        if (window == null || window.Count < 2)
            return "INSUFFICIENT";

        var start = window.First().Value;
        var end = window.Last().Value;

        if (start <= 0m)
            return "INSUFFICIENT";

        var ret = ((end / start) - 1m) * 100m;

        // crude drawdown proxy inside the window
        decimal peak = decimal.MinValue;
        decimal maxDd = 0m;
        foreach (var p in window)
        {
            if (p.Value > peak)
                peak = p.Value;

            if (peak > 0m)
            {
                var dd = ((p.Value / peak) - 1m) * 100m;
                if (dd < maxDd)
                    maxDd = dd;
            }
        }

        if (ret >= 3m && maxDd > -2m) return "TREND_UP";
        if (ret <= -3m && maxDd <= -4m) return "DRAWDOWN";
        if (Math.Abs(ret) < 1m) return "RANGE";
        if (ret > 0m) return "RECOVERY";
        return "WEAKNESS";
    }

    private static void WriteReportText(string prefix, string title, string body)
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();
        sb.AppendLine(title);
        sb.AppendLine(new string('=', title.Length));
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine(body);

        WriteRaw(prefix, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static void WriteRaw(string prefix, string content)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"{prefix}_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        File.WriteAllText(path, content);
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 F I L E :   D : \ D   D A T A   B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ S e r v i c e s \ A 8 4 S t r a t e g y F i t n e s s G a t i n g R e p o r t S e r v i c e . c s 
 
 T Y P E :   . c s 
 
 S I Z E :   1 4 . 6 7   K B 
 
 L I N E S :   3 2 1 
 
 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;
using TQGA.Application.Portfolio;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class A84StrategyFitnessGatingReportService
{
    public sealed class FitnessConfig
    {
        public int MinTrades { get; init; } = 30;
        public decimal MinPnL { get; init; } = 0m;
        public int MaxStrategiesAllowed { get; init; } = 50;
        public int TopKMarkets { get; init; } = 20;
        public decimal MaxWeightPerMarket { get; init; } = 0.10m;
        public decimal MaxWeightPerSymbol { get; init; } = 0.25m;

        // PATCH 23 — regime-aware scarcity override
        // Goal:
        // when Wave B + cash preservation already forced the system into defensive scarcity,
        // do NOT auto-reject the strongest positive strategy only because trade count is below the normal threshold.
        public decimal ScarcityModeMinCashWeight { get; init; } = 0.75m;
        public int ScarcityModeMaxSelectedMarkets { get; init; } = 1;
        public int ScarcityOverrideMinTrades { get; init; } = 12;
        public decimal ScarcityOverrideMinPnL { get; init; } = 50m;
        public int ScarcityOverrideMaxStrategies { get; init; } = 1;
    }

    public sealed class FitnessRow
    {
        public int StrategyId { get; init; }
        public string StrategyCode { get; init; } = "";
        public decimal PnL { get; init; }
        public int Trades { get; init; }
        public int Exits { get; init; }
        public decimal FitnessScore { get; init; }
        public bool Allowed { get; init; }
        public string GateReason { get; init; } = "";

        // PATCH 23
        public bool ScarcityOverrideApplied { get; init; }
    }

    public (Dictionary fitness, HashSet allowedIds) ComputeFitness(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        FitnessConfig cfg)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(cfg);

        var fitness = new Dictionary();
        var allowed = new HashSet();

        bool scarcityModeActive = IsScarcityDefensiveMode(result, cfg);
        int scarcityWinnerId = GetScarcityWinnerStrategyId(result);

        int scarcityOverrideAppliedCount = 0;

        foreach (var kv in result.StrategyPnL.OrderBy(k => k.Key))
        {
            var sid = kv.Key;
            var pnl = kv.Value;

            result.StrategyDiagnostics.TryGetValue(sid, out var diag);
            var trades = diag?.ExecutedEntries ?? 0;
            var exits = diag?.ExecutedExits ?? 0;

            const decimal startEquity = 100_000m;
            var retPct = startEquity <= 0m ? 0m : (pnl / startEquity) * 100m;

            decimal scoreCore = 0m;
            if (retPct > 0m && trades > 0)
            {
                var logTerm = (decimal)Math.Log(1.0 + (double)(retPct / 100m));
                var sqrtTrades = (decimal)Math.Sqrt(trades);
                scoreCore = logTerm * sqrtTrades;
            }

            bool allowedFlag = true;
            string reason = "OK";
            bool scarcityOverrideApplied = false;

            if (trades < cfg.MinTrades)
            {
                allowedFlag = false;
                reason = $"GATED: trades<{cfg.MinTrades}";
            }
            else if (pnl <= cfg.MinPnL)
            {
                allowedFlag = false;
                reason = $"GATED: pnl<= {cfg.MinPnL:0.##}";
            }
            else if (scoreCore <= 0m)
            {
                allowedFlag = false;
                reason = "GATED: fitness<=0";
            }

            // PATCH 23:
            // scarcity override may rescue exactly one top positive winner
            // when:
            // - defensive scarcity mode is active
            // - normal gate failure is ONLY low trades
            // - strategy is the top positive PnL winner
            // - trades clear a lower scarcity threshold
            // - pnl is materially positive
            if (!allowedFlag &&
                scarcityModeActive &&
                scarcityOverrideAppliedCount < cfg.ScarcityOverrideMaxStrategies &&
                sid == scarcityWinnerId &&
                trades >= cfg.ScarcityOverrideMinTrades &&
                pnl > cfg.ScarcityOverrideMinPnL &&
                scoreCore > 0m &&
                reason.StartsWith("GATED: trades<", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                allowedFlag = true;
                scarcityOverrideApplied = true;
                scarcityOverrideAppliedCount++;

                reason =
                    $"SCARCITY_OVERRIDE: defensive mode active, top positive winner rescued despite trades<{cfg.MinTrades}";
            }

            var row = new FitnessRow
            {
                StrategyId = sid,
                StrategyCode = $"S{sid:00}",
                PnL = pnl,
                Trades = trades,
                Exits = exits,
                FitnessScore = scoreCore,
                Allowed = allowedFlag,
                GateReason = reason,
                ScarcityOverrideApplied = scarcityOverrideApplied
            };

            fitness[sid] = row;

            if (allowedFlag)
                allowed.Add(sid);
        }

        if (allowed.Count > cfg.MaxStrategiesAllowed)
        {
            allowed = allowed
                .OrderByDescending(id => fitness[id].FitnessScore)
                .Take(cfg.MaxStrategiesAllowed)
                .ToHashSet();
        }

        foreach (var id in fitness.Keys.ToList())
        {
            var r = fitness[id];

            if (!allowed.Contains(id) && r.Allowed)
            {
                fitness[id] = new FitnessRow
                {
                    StrategyId = r.StrategyId,
                    StrategyCode = r.StrategyCode,
                    PnL = r.PnL,
                    Trades = r.Trades,
                    Exits = r.Exits,
                    FitnessScore = r.FitnessScore,
                    Allowed = false,
                    GateReason = "GATED: max strategies clamp",
                    ScarcityOverrideApplied = false
                };
            }
        }

        return (fitness, allowed);
    }

    public Dictionary RecomputeCioWeightsWithGating(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        HashSet allowedStrategyIds,
        FitnessConfig cfg)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(allowedStrategyIds);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(cfg);

        var scoreByMarket = new Dictionary();

        foreach (var kv in result.StrategySymbolTimeframePnL)
        {
            if (!TryParseStrategySymbolTfKey(kv.Key, out var sid, out var symbol, out var tf))
                continue;

            if (!allowedStrategyIds.Contains(sid))
                continue;

            var mk = new MarketKey(symbol, tf);

            if (!scoreByMarket.ContainsKey(mk))
                scoreByMarket[mk] = 0m;

            scoreByMarket[mk] += kv.Value;
        }

        var cio = new CioDynamicReallocationEngine(
            topK: cfg.TopKMarkets,
            minWeight: 0.00m,
            maxWeight: cfg.MaxWeightPerMarket,
            maxWeightPerSymbol: cfg.MaxWeightPerSymbol);

        var weights = cio.ComputeWeights(scoreByMarket);

        return weights.ToDictionary(
            x => $"CIO::{x.Key.Symbol}::{x.Key.Timeframe}",
            x => x.Value,
            StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    }

    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        FitnessConfig? cfg = null)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);

        cfg ??= new FitnessConfig();

        var (fitness, allowed) = ComputeFitness(result, cfg);

        // PATCH 13C:
        // A84_05 MUST publish only the exact stored canonical dictionary.
        // This method is forbidden from using:
        // - RecomputeCioWeightsWithGating(...)
        // - MaxWeightPerMarket display logic
        // - local cleaning / local normalization / local capping
        var canonicalCio = result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights
            ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        bool scarcityModeActive = IsScarcityDefensiveMode(result, cfg);
        int scarcityWinnerId = GetScarcityWinnerStrategyId(result);

        var outFile = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"A84_05_STRATEGY_FITNESS_{runUtc:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("A84_05 — STRATEGY FITNESS + CIO GATING");
        sb.AppendLine("======================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC) : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("PUBLISH PATH SIGNATURE");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("PATCH_13C_A84_05_CANONICAL_ONLY");
        sb.AppendLine("PATCH_23_SCARCITY_STRATEGY_GATE");
        sb.AppendLine("SOURCE = exact result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights");
        sb.AppendLine("RECOMPUTE = DISABLED");
        sb.AppendLine("LOCAL_CAP = DISABLED");
        sb.AppendLine("LOCAL_RESCALING = DISABLED");
        sb.AppendLine("LOCAL_CLEANING = DISABLED");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("FITNESS CONFIG (GATING INPUTS ONLY)");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"MinTrades                : {cfg.MinTrades}");
        sb.AppendLine($"MinPnL                   : {cfg.MinPnL:0.##}");
        sb.AppendLine($"TopKMarkets              : {cfg.TopKMarkets}");
        sb.AppendLine($"MaxWeightPerMarket       : {cfg.MaxWeightPerMarket:P2}  (NOT USED FOR A84_05 PUBLISH)");
        sb.AppendLine($"MaxWeightPerSymbol       : {cfg.MaxWeightPerSymbol:P2}  (NOT USED FOR A84_05 PUBLISH)");
        sb.AppendLine($"ScarcityModeMinCash      : {cfg.ScarcityModeMinCashWeight:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"ScarcityModeMaxMarkets   : {cfg.ScarcityModeMaxSelectedMarkets}");
        sb.AppendLine($"ScarcityOverrideMinTrades: {cfg.ScarcityOverrideMinTrades}");
        sb.AppendLine($"ScarcityOverrideMinPnL   : {cfg.ScarcityOverrideMinPnL:0.##}");
        sb.AppendLine($"ScarcityOverrideMaxStrat : {cfg.ScarcityOverrideMaxStrategies}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SCARCITY DEFENSIVE MODE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Active                   : {(scarcityModeActive ? "YES" : "NO")}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Runner Selected Markets  : {result.SelectedMarkets?.Count ?? 0}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Runner Cash Weight       : {result.CashAllocationWeight:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top Positive Winner      : {(scarcityWinnerId <= 0 ? "NONE" : $"S{scarcityWinnerId:00}")}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("STRATEGY FITNESS TABLE");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("Code | PnL         | Trades | Exits | Fitness   | Allowed | Override | GateReason");
        sb.AppendLine("-----+-------------+--------+-------+-----------+---------+----------+-----------------------------------------------");

        foreach (var row in fitness.Values.OrderByDescending(r => r.FitnessScore))
        {
            sb.AppendLine(
                $"{row.StrategyCode,-4} | {row.PnL,11:0.00} | {row.Trades,6} | {row.Exits,5} | {row.FitnessScore,9:0.0000} | {(row.Allowed ? "YES" : "NO "),-7} | {(row.ScarcityOverrideApplied ? "YES" : "NO "),-8} | {row.GateReason}");
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine($"Allowed strategies : {allowed.Count} / {fitness.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Allowed list       : {(allowed.Count == 0 ? "NONE" : string.Join(", ", allowed.OrderBy(x => x).Select(x => $"S{x:00}")))}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("CANONICAL CIO SNAPSHOT");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Canonical Count    : {canonicalCio.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Canonical Sum      : {canonicalCio.Values.Sum():P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Canonical Max      : {(canonicalCio.Count == 0 ? 0m : canonicalCio.Values.Max()):P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("CIO WEIGHTS (POST-GATING) TOP 20");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------------");
        if (canonicalCio.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: Stored canonical CIO weights are empty.");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var w in canonicalCio
                         .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
                         .Take(20))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{w.Key,-22} W {w.Value:P2}");
            }
        }

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);
        File.WriteAllText(outFile, sb.ToString(), Encoding.UTF8);
    }

    private static bool TryParseStrategySymbolTfKey(
        string key,
        out int strategyId,
        out string symbol,
        out string timeframe)
    {
        strategyId = 0;
        symbol = "";
        timeframe = "";

        var parts = key.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        if (parts.Length != 3)
            return false;

        var s = parts[0].Trim();
        if (!s.StartsWith("S", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return false;

        if (!int.TryParse(s.Substring(1), out strategyId))
            return false;

        symbol = parts[1].Trim();
        timeframe = parts[2].Trim();

        return !(string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(symbol) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(timeframe));
    }

    private static bool IsScarcityDefensiveMode(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        FitnessConfig cfg)
    {
        int selectedMarkets = result.SelectedMarkets?.Count ?? 0;
        decimal cashWeight = result.CashAllocationWeight;

        return selectedMarkets <= cfg.ScarcityModeMaxSelectedMarkets &&
               cashWeight >= cfg.ScarcityModeMinCashWeight;
    }

    private static int GetScarcityWinnerStrategyId(PortfolioBacktestResult result)
    {
        if (result.StrategyPnL == null || result.StrategyPnL.Count == 0)
            return 0;

        return result.StrategyPnL
            .Where(x => x.Value > 0m)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Key)
            .Select(x => x.Key)
            .FirstOrDefault();
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

/// 
/// A84_05 — STRATEGY FITNESS (Institutional heuristic)
/// Uses ONLY existing PortfolioBacktestResult fields:
/// - StrategyPnL (Dictionary)
/// - StrategyDiagnostics (Dictionary)
///
/// No dependency on non-existent fields like StrategyTrades.
/// 
public sealed class A84StrategyFitnessReportService
{
    public void Generate(PortfolioBacktestResult result)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        if (result is null)
        {
            WriteReportText(
                "A84_05_STRATEGY_FITNESS",
                "A84_05 — STRATEGY FITNESS",
                "NO DATA: PortfolioBacktestResult is null.");
            return;
        }

        var pnlByStrategy = result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary();
        var diagByStrategy = result.StrategyDiagnostics ?? new Dictionary();

        if (pnlByStrategy.Count == 0 && diagByStrategy.Count == 0)
        {
            WriteReportText(
                "A84_05_STRATEGY_FITNESS",
                "A84_05 — STRATEGY FITNESS",
                "NO DATA: StrategyPnL and StrategyDiagnostics are empty.");
            return;
        }

        // Normalize PnL magnitude so it doesn't dominate everything.
        var maxAbsPnL = pnlByStrategy.Count == 0
            ? 1m
            : pnlByStrategy.Values.Select(v => Math.Abs(v)).DefaultIfEmpty(1m).Max();

        if (maxAbsPnL <= 0) maxAbsPnL = 1m;

        // Union of strategy IDs from both dicts
        var ids = pnlByStrategy.Keys
            .Concat(diagByStrategy.Keys)
            .Distinct()
            .OrderBy(x => x)
            .ToList();

        var rows = new List(ids.Count);

        foreach (var id in ids)
        {
            pnlByStrategy.TryGetValue(id, out var pnl);
            diagByStrategy.TryGetValue(id, out var d);

            var ticks = d?.TicksProcessed ?? 0;

            var entryAttempts = d?.EntryAttempts ?? 0;
            var executedEntries = d?.ExecutedEntries ?? 0;
            var executedExits = d?.ExecutedExits ?? 0;

            var signalLong = d?.SignalLong ?? 0;
            var signalExit = d?.SignalExit ?? 0;

            // Trades proxy: executed entries
            var trades = executedEntries;

            // Execution quality proxies
            decimal execRate = SafeDiv(executedEntries, entryAttempts);                 // 0..1
            decimal completionRate = SafeDiv(executedExits, Math.Max(1, executedEntries)); // 0..1
            decimal churnPenalty = entryAttempts <= 0 ? 0m : SafeDiv(entryAttempts - executedEntries, entryAttempts); // 0..1
            decimal discipline = SafeDiv(signalExit, Math.Max(1, signalLong));          // 0..1-ish

            // PnL scoring
            decimal pnlScore = Clamp01(Math.Abs(pnl) / maxAbsPnL);
            decimal directionScore = pnl >= 0 ? 1.0m : 0.0m;
            decimal activityScore = Clamp01(trades / 5000m); // tune later

            // Institutional fitness (bounded, deterministic)
            decimal fitness =
                (pnlScore * 0.45m) +
                (directionScore * 0.15m) +
                (activityScore * 0.20m) +
                (execRate * 0.10m) +
                (completionRate * 0.10m) -
                (churnPenalty * 0.10m);

            // Hard kill-switch: dead strategy => zero fitness
            if (trades <= 0)
                fitness = 0m;

            rows.Add(new Row(
                Id: id,
                PnL: pnl,
                Ticks: ticks,
                Trades: trades,
                EntryAttempts: entryAttempts,
                ExecutedEntries: executedEntries,
                ExecutedExits: executedExits,
                ExecRate: execRate,
                CompletionRate: completionRate,
                Discipline: discipline,
                ChurnPenalty: churnPenalty,
                Fitness: fitness
            ));
        }

        var ranked = rows
            .OrderByDescending(r => r.Fitness)
            .ThenByDescending(r => r.PnL)
            .ToList();

        var sb = new StringBuilder();
        sb.AppendLine("A84_05 — STRATEGY FITNESS");
        sb.AppendLine("=========================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("Fitness is a bounded institutional score (0..1) using StrategyPnL + StrategyDiagnostics.");
        sb.AppendLine("Dead strategies (0 trades) are forced to Fitness 0.");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine($"MaxAbsPnL normalization : {maxAbsPnL:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("Rank | Strat | Fitness | PnL           | Trades | ExecRate | ExitCov | Churn  | Discipline");
        sb.AppendLine("-----+-------+---------+---------------+--------+----------+---------+--------+-----------");

        int rank = 1;
        foreach (var r in ranked)
        {
            var strat = $"S{r.Id:00}";
            sb.AppendLine(
                $"{rank,4} | {strat,-5} | {r.Fitness,7:F3} | {r.PnL,13:F2} | {r.Trades,6} | {r.ExecRate,8:P2} | {r.CompletionRate,7:P2} | {r.ChurnPenalty,6:P2} | {r.Discipline,9:P2}");
            rank++;
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("CIO Action Hint:");
        sb.AppendLine("- Only allocate capital to strategies with Fitness >= 0.25 and Trades > 0.");
        sb.AppendLine("- If Fitness=0, the strategy is inactive (signals not firing or execution path blocked).");

        WriteReportFile("A84_05_STRATEGY_FITNESS", sb.ToString());
    }

    private static decimal SafeDiv(int a, int b) => b <= 0 ? 0m : (decimal)a / b;

    private static decimal Clamp01(decimal x)
    {
        if (x < 0m) return 0m;
        if (x > 1m) return 1m;
        return x;
    }

    private static void WriteReportText(string name, string title, string body)
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();
        sb.AppendLine(title);
        sb.AppendLine(new string('=', Math.Max(10, title.Length)));
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine(body);

        WriteReportFile(name, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static void WriteReportFile(string name, string content)
    {
        var ts = DateTime.UtcNow.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        File.WriteAllText(
            Path.Combine(DataPaths.Reports, $"{name}_{ts}.txt"),
            content,
            Encoding.UTF8);
    }

    private sealed record Row(
        int Id,
        decimal PnL,
        long Ticks,
        int Trades,
        int EntryAttempts,
        int ExecutedEntries,
        int ExecutedExits,
        decimal ExecRate,
        decimal CompletionRate,
        decimal Discipline,
        decimal ChurnPenalty,
        decimal Fitness);
}

 F I L E :   D : \ D   D A T A   B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ S e r v i c e s \ A 8 4 _ R e g i m e R e s e a r c h S e r v i c e . c s 
 
 T Y P E :   . c s 
 
 S I Z E :   1 3 . 5 8   K B 
 
 L I N E S :   2 9 1 
 
 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class A84_RegimeResearchService
{
    public void Generate(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        Dictionary canonicalCioPostGatingWeights)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(canonicalCioPostGatingWeights);

        GenerateMarketRegime(result.SymbolTimeframePnL);
        GenerateMarketRanking(result.SymbolTimeframePnL);
        GenerateCioSkill(result, canonicalCioPostGatingWeights);
        GenerateGrowthScenarioMode(result, canonicalCioPostGatingWeights);
    }

    private void GenerateMarketRegime(Dictionary pnl)
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("A84_01 — MARKET REGIME MAP");
        sb.AppendLine("===========================");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (pnl == null || pnl.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: SymbolTimeframePnL is empty.");
            Write("A84_01_MARKET_REGIME", sb);
            return;
        }

        foreach (var kv in pnl.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).Take(30))
        {
            var regime = DetectRegime(kv.Value);
            sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-20} {kv.Value,12:F2}   {regime}");
        }

        Write("A84_01_MARKET_REGIME", sb);
    }

    private void GenerateMarketRanking(Dictionary pnl)
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("A84_02 — MARKET EDGE RANKING");
        sb.AppendLine("============================");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (pnl == null || pnl.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: SymbolTimeframePnL is empty.");
            Write("A84_02_MARKET_RANKING", sb);
            return;
        }

        int rank = 1;

        foreach (var kv in pnl.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"{rank,3} | {kv.Key,-20} | {kv.Value,12:F2}");
            rank++;
        }

        Write("A84_02_MARKET_RANKING", sb);
    }

    private void GenerateCioSkill(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        Dictionary canonicalCioPostGatingWeights)
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("A84_03 — CIO ALLOCATION SKILL");
        sb.AppendLine("==============================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("SOURCE: Exact stored post-gating CIO deployment with cash preservation intact.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (canonicalCioPostGatingWeights.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: Stored canonical CIO dictionary is empty.");
            sb.AppendLine($"Cash Held         : {Math.Max(0m, Math.Min(1m, result.CashAllocationWeight)):P2}");
            Write("A84_03_CIO_RATING", sb);
            return;
        }

        var concentration = canonicalCioPostGatingWeights.Values.Max();
        var diversification = canonicalCioPostGatingWeights.Count;
        var cashHeld = Math.Max(0m, Math.Min(1m, result.CashAllocationWeight));

        sb.AppendLine($"Markets Allocated : {diversification}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Max Weight        : {concentration:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Cash Held         : {cashHeld:P2}");

        string rating =
            concentration < 0.10m ? "Institutional"
          : concentration < 0.20m ? "Professional"
          : concentration < 0.35m ? "Selective"
          : "Concentrated";

        sb.AppendLine($"CIO Rating        : {rating}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (cashHeld >= 0.50m)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("PATCH 20 SIGNAL");
            sb.AppendLine("---------------");
            sb.AppendLine("Regime-aware no-trade guard is active. Large residual cash is being preserved instead of forcing second-tier exposure.");
            sb.AppendLine();
        }

        sb.AppendLine("CANONICAL POST-GATING CIO WEIGHTS");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------------");

        foreach (var kv in canonicalCioPostGatingWeights.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).Take(10))
            sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-24} {kv.Value,10:P2}");

        Write("A84_03_CIO_RATING", sb);
    }

    private void GenerateGrowthScenarioMode(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        Dictionary canonicalCioPostGatingWeights)
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("A84_04 — SYSTEM GROWTH SCENARIO MODE");
        sb.AppendLine("====================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PUBLISH PATH SIGNATURE");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("PATCH_15_A84_04_SCENARIO_MODE");
        sb.AppendLine("RULE = fixed monthly ROI projection removed");
        sb.AppendLine("RULE = scenario output must warn on negative return, single-market concentration, alpha decay");
        sb.AppendLine();

        var equity = result.PortfolioEquityTimeline ?? new Dictionary();
        var ordered = equity.OrderBy(x => x.Key).ToList();
        var realPoints = ordered.Where(x => x.Key != DateTime.MinValue).ToList();

        decimal startEquity = 0m;
        decimal endEquity = 0m;
        decimal totalReturnPct = 0m;

        if (realPoints.Count > 0)
        {
            startEquity = realPoints.First().Value;
            endEquity = realPoints.Last().Value;
            totalReturnPct = startEquity <= 0m
                ? 0m
                : ((endEquity / startEquity) - 1m) * 100m;
        }

        var allocationCount = canonicalCioPostGatingWeights.Count;
        var topWeight = allocationCount == 0 ? 0m : canonicalCioPostGatingWeights.Values.Max();
        var cashHeld = Math.Max(0m, Math.Min(1m, result.CashAllocationWeight));

        decimal earlyHalfReturn = 0m;
        decimal lateHalfReturn = 0m;
        bool alphaDecayDetected = false;

        if (realPoints.Count >= 4)
        {
            var half = realPoints.Count / 2;
            var early = realPoints.Take(half).ToList();
            var late = realPoints.Skip(half).ToList();

            earlyHalfReturn = SegmentReturnPct(early);
            lateHalfReturn = SegmentReturnPct(late);
            alphaDecayDetected = lateHalfReturn < earlyHalfReturn;
        }

        bool negativeReturn = totalReturnPct < 0m;
        bool singleMarketConcentration = allocationCount <= 1;
        bool extremeConcentration = topWeight >= 0.80m;

        sb.AppendLine("CURRENT RUN REALITY");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Start Equity              : {startEquity:0.00}");
        sb.AppendLine($"End Equity                : {endEquity:0.00}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Total Return              : {totalReturnPct:0.00}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"Post-Gating Markets       : {allocationCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top CIO Weight            : {topWeight:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Post-Gating Cash Held     : {cashHeld:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Early Half Return         : {earlyHalfReturn:0.00}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"Late Half Return          : {lateHalfReturn:0.00}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"Alpha Decay Detected      : {(alphaDecayDetected ? "YES" : "NO")}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("REALISM WARNINGS");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------");
        if (!negativeReturn && !singleMarketConcentration && !extremeConcentration && !alphaDecayDetected)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO MAJOR WARNING: Current run does not trip the Patch 15 realism flags.");
        }
        else
        {
            if (negativeReturn)
                sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Current run total return is negative. Fixed optimistic growth projection is forbidden.");

            if (singleMarketConcentration)
                sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Post-gating allocation breadth is one market. Portfolio is a single-edge survivor.");

            if (!singleMarketConcentration && extremeConcentration)
                sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Top CIO weight is extreme. Diversification is materially weak.");

            if (alphaDecayDetected)
                sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Alpha decay detected. Late-half performance is weaker than early-half performance.");
        }

        if (cashHeld >= 0.50m)
            sb.AppendLine("INFO: Patch 20 defensive posture is active. Capital is being held in cash because edge breadth is too weak for broader deployment.");

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("SCENARIO MODE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------");
        sb.AppendLine("This section is scenario planning only. It is NOT a fixed forward projection.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        decimal currentCapital = endEquity > 0m ? endEquity : 100000m;

        var scenarios = BuildScenarios(
            negativeReturn,
            singleMarketConcentration || extremeConcentration,
            alphaDecayDetected);

        sb.AppendLine("Scenario        Monthly Assumption   12-Month Capital   Interpretation");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------  -------------------  -----------------  ------------------------------");

        foreach (var s in scenarios)
        {
            decimal projected = Project12Months(currentCapital, s.MonthlyRate);
            sb.AppendLine(
                $"{PadRightSafe(s.Name, 14)}  {s.MonthlyRate,18:P2}  {projected,17:0.00}  {s.Interpretation}");
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("OPERATOR GUIDANCE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        if (negativeReturn || alphaDecayDetected || singleMarketConcentration || extremeConcentration)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("1) Treat this run as unstable for institutional projection purposes.");
            sb.AppendLine("2) Prioritize Wave B signal ranking and top-N execution before trusting growth narratives.");
            sb.AppendLine("3) Require better breadth across strategies and SYMBOL::TF edges before restoring optimistic scenario assumptions.");
            sb.AppendLine("4) Use A84_05, A84_07, and A84_08 as the primary reality checks before any growth claim.");

            if (cashHeld >= 0.50m)
                sb.AppendLine("5) High cash is currently a defensive feature, not automatically a defect, when regime breadth is weak.");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Current run does not trigger the Patch 15 realism alarms, but scenarios remain illustrative only.");
        }

        Write("A84_04_GROWTH_PROJECTION", sb);
    }

    private static List BuildScenarios(
        bool negativeReturn,
        bool concentrated,
        bool alphaDecayDetected)
    {
        // PATCH 15 deterministic scenario rules:
        // - Stress scenario stays defensive when live run is weak.
        // - Base scenario is suppressed to flat when realism flags are active.
        // - Recovery scenario remains modest under stress; no aggressive fixed-growth path.
        if (negativeReturn || concentrated || alphaDecayDetected)
        {
            return new List
            {
                new("Stress",  -0.02m, "Weak run persists / further degradation"),
                new("Base",     0.00m, "Capital preservation, no growth assumption"),
                new("Recovery", 0.01m, "Partial stabilization after execution improvements")
            };
        }

        return new List
        {
            new("Stress",   -0.01m, "Temporary setback / mild degradation"),
            new("Base",      0.01m, "Measured continuation under controlled conditions"),
            new("Upside",    0.02m, "Improved breadth and stable non-decaying edge")
        };
    }

    private static decimal Project12Months(decimal capital, decimal monthlyRate)
    {
        decimal output = capital;

        for (int i = 0; i < 12; i++)
            output *= (1m + monthlyRate);

        return output;
    }

    private static decimal SegmentReturnPct(List> segment)
    {
        if (segment.Count < 2)
            return 0m;

        decimal start = segment.First().Value;
        decimal end = segment.Last().Value;

        if (start <= 0m)
            return 0m;

        return ((end / start) - 1m) * 100m;
    }

    private static string DetectRegime(decimal pnl)
    {
        if (pnl > 40000m) return "STRONG TREND";
        if (pnl > 10000m) return "TREND";
        if (pnl > 0m) return "WEAK TREND";
        if (pnl > -5000m) return "RANGE";

        return "HOSTILE";
    }

    private static void Write(string name, StringBuilder sb)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        File.WriteAllText(
            Path.Combine(
                DataPaths.Reports,
                $"{name}_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt"),
            sb.ToString());
    }

    private static string PadRightSafe(string value, int totalWidth)
    {
        value ??= string.Empty;

        if (value.Length == totalWidth)
            return value;

        if (value.Length < totalWidth)
            return value.PadRight(totalWidth);

        if (totalWidth <= 3)
            return value[..totalWidth];

        return value[..(totalWidth - 3)] + "...";
    }

    private sealed record GrowthScenario(
        string Name,
        decimal MonthlyRate,
        string Interpretation);
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class AlphaRankingReportService
{
    // Institutional fix:
    // - Do NOT resolve a DI-scoped TradeDecisionDiagnostics here.
    // - Always read diagnostics snapshots from PortfolioBacktestResult (per-strategy).
    public void Generate(PortfolioBacktestResult? result)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 05 — ALPHA DIAGNOSTICS (PER STRATEGY)");
        sb.AppendLine("===========================================");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (result == null)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: result is null.");
            Write(sb);
            return;
        }

        var strategyPnL = result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary();
        var strategyDiagnostics = result.StrategyDiagnostics ?? new Dictionary();

        bool hasPnL = strategyPnL.Count > 0;
        bool hasDiag = strategyDiagnostics.Count > 0;

        if (!hasPnL && !hasDiag)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: StrategyPnL and StrategyDiagnostics are empty.");
            sb.AppendLine("NOTE: Ensure PortfolioBacktestRunner populates StrategyDiagnostics snapshots per strategy.");
            Write(sb);
            return;
        }

        var ids = new HashSet();

        if (hasPnL)
        {
            foreach (int id in strategyPnL.Keys)
                ids.Add(id);
        }

        if (hasDiag)
        {
            foreach (int id in strategyDiagnostics.Keys)
                ids.Add(id);
        }

        sb.AppendLine("ID  | PnL        | Ticks     | Long    | Short   | Exit    | EntryAtt | EntryOK  | ExitOK");
        sb.AppendLine("----+------------+-----------+---------+---------+---------+----------+----------+--------");

        foreach (int id in ids.OrderBy(i => i))
        {
            strategyPnL.TryGetValue(id, out decimal pnl);

            TradeDecisionDiagnosticsSnapshot? snapshot = null;
            bool hasSnapshot = false;

            if (hasDiag)
                hasSnapshot = strategyDiagnostics.TryGetValue(id, out snapshot);

            int ticksProcessed = hasSnapshot && snapshot != null ? snapshot.TicksProcessed : 0;
            int signalLong = hasSnapshot && snapshot != null ? snapshot.SignalLong : 0;
            int signalShort = hasSnapshot && snapshot != null ? snapshot.SignalShort : 0;
            int signalExit = hasSnapshot && snapshot != null ? snapshot.SignalExit : 0;
            int entryAttempts = hasSnapshot && snapshot != null ? snapshot.EntryAttempts : 0;
            int executedEntries = hasSnapshot && snapshot != null ? snapshot.ExecutedEntries : 0;
            int executedExits = hasSnapshot && snapshot != null ? snapshot.ExecutedExits : 0;

            sb.AppendLine(string.Format(
                "{0,2:00}  | {1,10:F2} | {2,9} | {3,7} | {4,7} | {5,7} | {6,8} | {7,8} | {8,6}",
                id,
                pnl,
                ticksProcessed,
                signalLong,
                signalShort,
                signalExit,
                entryAttempts,
                executedEntries,
                executedExits));
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("NOTES");
        sb.AppendLine("-----");
        sb.AppendLine("- This report is generated from PortfolioBacktestResult snapshots (institutional-safe).");
        sb.AppendLine("- If counts are zero, verify TradingEngine increments diagnostics and Runner stores snapshots.");

        Write(sb);
    }

    private static void Write(StringBuilder sb)
    {
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_05_ALPHA_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 F I L E :   D : \ D   D A T A   B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ S e r v i c e s \ C i o C a p i t a l R e p o r t S e r v i c e . c s 
 
 T Y P E :   . c s 
 
 S I Z E :   1 2 . 0 9   K B 
 
 L I N E S :   2 7 0 
 
 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class CioCapitalReportService
{
    public void Generate(Dictionary weights)
    {
        Generate(
            strategyWeights: weights,
            runnerMarketAllocationWeights: null,
            canonicalCioPostGatingWeights: null,
            cashWeight: 0m);
    }

    public void Generate(
        Dictionary strategyWeights,
        IReadOnlyDictionary? marketAllocationWeights,
        decimal cashWeight)
    {
        Generate(
            strategyWeights,
            runnerMarketAllocationWeights: marketAllocationWeights,
            canonicalCioPostGatingWeights: null,
            cashWeight: cashWeight);
    }

    public void Generate(
        Dictionary strategyWeights,
        IReadOnlyDictionary? runnerMarketAllocationWeights,
        IReadOnlyDictionary? canonicalCioPostGatingWeights,
        decimal cashWeight)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(strategyWeights);

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 06 — CAPITAL ALLOCATION");
        sb.AppendLine("================================");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION A — STRATEGY TRUST WEIGHTS");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------------------");

        foreach (var w in strategyWeights.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
            sb.AppendLine($"Strategy {w.Key:00} -> {(w.Value * 100m):F2}%");

        sb.AppendLine();

        AppendRunnerCandidateMixSection(
            sb,
            runnerMarketAllocationWeights,
            cashWeight);

        AppendCanonicalDeployableSection(
            sb,
            canonicalCioPostGatingWeights,
            cashWeight);

        File.WriteAllText(
            Path.Combine(
                DataPaths.Reports,
                $"REPORT_06_CAPITAL_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt"),
            sb.ToString());
    }

    private static void AppendRunnerCandidateMixSection(
        StringBuilder sb,
        IReadOnlyDictionary? runnerMarketAllocationWeights,
        decimal cashWeight)
    {
        sb.AppendLine("SECTION B — RUNNER CANDIDATE MIX (PRE-DEPLOYMENT)");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("SEMANTICS: These weights describe relative mix inside the candidate sleeve.");
        sb.AppendLine("SEMANTICS: They are NOT gross deployed portfolio weights.");
        sb.AppendLine("SEMANTICS: Preserved cash is shown only as a reference to downstream deployment posture.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (runnerMarketAllocationWeights is null || runnerMarketAllocationWeights.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: Runner candidate mix is empty.");
            sb.AppendLine($"Reference Preserved Cash (gross) -> {(cashWeight * 100m):F2}%");
            sb.AppendLine();
            return;
        }

        foreach (var kv in runnerMarketAllocationWeights.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
            sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key} -> {(kv.Value * 100m):F2}%");

        sb.AppendLine($"Reference Preserved Cash (gross) -> {(cashWeight * 100m):F2}%");
        sb.AppendLine();

        AppendCandidateMixMetrics(
            sb,
            sectionTitle: "SECTION C — RUNNER CANDIDATE MIX METRICS",
            underline: "-----------------------------------------",
            candidateMixWeights: runnerMarketAllocationWeights,
            referenceCashWeight: cashWeight);
    }

    private static void AppendCanonicalDeployableSection(
        StringBuilder sb,
        IReadOnlyDictionary? canonicalCioPostGatingWeights,
        decimal cashWeight)
    {
        sb.AppendLine("SECTION D — CANONICAL DEPLOYABLE CIO ALLOCATION (GROSS CAPITAL)");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------------------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("SEMANTICS: This section is the true post-gating deployable capital snapshot.");
        sb.AppendLine("SEMANTICS: Cash here is gross preserved capital, paired directly with canonical CIO weights.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (canonicalCioPostGatingWeights is null)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: Canonical post-gating CIO allocation is null.");
            sb.AppendLine($"CASH -> {(cashWeight * 100m):F2}%");
            sb.AppendLine();
            return;
        }

        if (canonicalCioPostGatingWeights.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: Canonical post-gating CIO weights are empty.");
            sb.AppendLine($"CASH -> {(cashWeight * 100m):F2}%");
            sb.AppendLine();

            AppendDeployableAllocationMetrics(
                sb,
                sectionTitle: "SECTION E — CANONICAL DEPLOYABLE ALLOCATION METRICS",
                underline: "----------------------------------------------------",
                deployableWeights: canonicalCioPostGatingWeights,
                cashWeight: cashWeight);

            return;
        }

        foreach (var kv in canonicalCioPostGatingWeights.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
            sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key} -> {(kv.Value * 100m):F2}%");

        sb.AppendLine($"CASH -> {(cashWeight * 100m):F2}%");
        sb.AppendLine();

        AppendDeployableAllocationMetrics(
            sb,
            sectionTitle: "SECTION E — CANONICAL DEPLOYABLE ALLOCATION METRICS",
            underline: "----------------------------------------------------",
            deployableWeights: canonicalCioPostGatingWeights,
            cashWeight: cashWeight);
    }

    private static void AppendCandidateMixMetrics(
        StringBuilder sb,
        string sectionTitle,
        string underline,
        IReadOnlyDictionary candidateMixWeights,
        decimal referenceCashWeight)
    {
        sb.AppendLine(sectionTitle);
        sb.AppendLine(underline);

        int marketCount = candidateMixWeights.Count;
        decimal mixSum = candidateMixWeights.Values.Sum();
        decimal maxWeight = candidateMixWeights.Values.DefaultIfEmpty(0m).Max();
        decimal minWeight = candidateMixWeights.Values.DefaultIfEmpty(0m).Min();
        decimal hhi = candidateMixWeights.Values.Sum(x => x * x);

        sb.AppendLine($"Candidate Markets: {marketCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Candidate Mix Sum: {(mixSum * 100m):F2}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"Reference Preserved Cash (gross): {(referenceCashWeight * 100m):F2}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"Max Candidate Sleeve Weight: {(maxWeight * 100m):F2}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"Min Candidate Sleeve Weight: {(minWeight * 100m):F2}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"HHI Candidate Mix: {hhi:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("INTERPRETATION");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------");
        sb.AppendLine("Candidate mix weights are internal sleeve proportions only.");
        sb.AppendLine("Do NOT add candidate mix sum and preserved cash together.");
        sb.AppendLine("Gross deployment truth is reported only in Section D / Section E.");
        sb.AppendLine();
    }

    private static void AppendDeployableAllocationMetrics(
        StringBuilder sb,
        string sectionTitle,
        string underline,
        IReadOnlyDictionary deployableWeights,
        decimal cashWeight)
    {
        sb.AppendLine(sectionTitle);
        sb.AppendLine(underline);

        int marketCount = deployableWeights.Count;
        decimal totalAllocated = deployableWeights.Values.Sum();
        decimal maxWeight = deployableWeights.Values.DefaultIfEmpty(0m).Max();
        decimal minWeight = deployableWeights.Values.DefaultIfEmpty(0m).Min();
        decimal hhi = deployableWeights.Values.Sum(x => x * x);
        decimal grossTotal = totalAllocated + cashWeight;

        sb.AppendLine($"Deployable Markets: {marketCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Gross Deployable Allocation: {(totalAllocated * 100m):F2}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"Gross Preserved Cash: {(cashWeight * 100m):F2}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"Gross Total (Deployable + Cash): {(grossTotal * 100m):F2}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"Max Gross Market Weight: {(maxWeight * 100m):F2}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"Min Gross Market Weight: {(minWeight * 100m):F2}%");
        sb.AppendLine($"HHI Deployable Allocation: {hhi:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("REALISM / RISK FLAGS");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------------");

        bool wroteWarning = false;

        if (marketCount == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("WARNING: No deployable markets survived into canonical CIO allocation.");
            wroteWarning = true;
        }

        if (marketCount == 1)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Single-market deployable allocation. Institutional diversification is absent.");
            wroteWarning = true;
        }
        else if (marketCount <= 3)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Very low deployable breadth.");
            wroteWarning = true;
        }
        else if (marketCount < 5)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Low deployable breadth.");
            wroteWarning = true;
        }

        if (maxWeight >= 0.90m)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Extreme gross concentration. One market dominates almost all deployable capital.");
            wroteWarning = true;
        }
        else if (maxWeight >= 0.80m)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Severe gross concentration. Max market weight exceeds 80%.");
            wroteWarning = true;
        }
        else if (maxWeight >= 0.60m)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("WARNING: High gross concentration. Max market weight exceeds 60%.");
            wroteWarning = true;
        }
        else if (maxWeight > 0.25m)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Elevated gross concentration. Max market weight exceeds 25%.");
            wroteWarning = true;
        }

        if (hhi >= 0.80m)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("WARNING: HHI indicates extreme deployable concentration.");
            wroteWarning = true;
        }
        else if (hhi >= 0.50m)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("WARNING: HHI indicates high deployable concentration.");
            wroteWarning = true;
        }

        if (cashWeight > 0.25m)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("WARNING: High preserved cash.");
            wroteWarning = true;
        }

        if (Math.Abs(grossTotal - 1m) > 0.0001m)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Gross deployable allocation plus cash does not reconcile to 100.00%.");
            wroteWarning = true;
        }

        if (!wroteWarning)
            sb.AppendLine("OK: No major deployable capital warning under current thresholds.");

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("OPERATOR INTERPRETATION");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------");

        if (marketCount == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Capital realism is weak because no markets survived into gross deployable CIO allocation.");
        }
        else if (marketCount == 1 || maxWeight >= 0.80m)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Capital realism is weak for institutional use. The system is effectively operating as a single-edge deployer.");
        }
        else if (marketCount <= 3 || maxWeight >= 0.60m)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Capital realism is moderate-to-weak. Deployable breadth is limited and concentration risk is material.");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Capital realism is acceptable under current simple deployable concentration thresholds.");
        }

        if (cashWeight > 0.25m)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("High cash may be correct under Patch 20 / Patch 21 defensive posture when regime quality and breadth are weak.");
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class CioWeightsSymbolTimeframeReportService
{
    public void Generate(Dictionary canonicalCioWeights)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 12 — CIO WEIGHTS (CANONICAL)");
        sb.AppendLine("====================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("Key format: CIO::SYMBOL::TF  (example: CIO::ATOMUSDT::1h)");
        sb.AppendLine();

        if (canonicalCioWeights == null || canonicalCioWeights.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: Canonical CIO weights empty.");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("TOP 50 (by weight)");
            sb.AppendLine("------------------");
            foreach (var kv in canonicalCioWeights.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).Take(50))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-28} {kv.Value,10:F6}");

            sb.AppendLine();
            sb.AppendLine("FULL LIST (sorted by weight desc)");
            sb.AppendLine("---------------------------------");
            foreach (var kv in canonicalCioWeights.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-28} {kv.Value,10:F6}");
        }

        var path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_12_CIO_WEIGHTS_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }
}
