 F I L E :   D : \ D   D A T A   B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . I n f r a s t r u c t u r e \ S t r a t e g i e s \ R e g i m e G a t e d A l t c o i n L e a d e r s h i p P u l l b a c k S i g n a l . c s 
 
 T Y P E :   . c s 
 
 S I Z E :   5 . 1 9   K B 
 
 L I N E S :   1 4 2 
 
 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using TQGA.Application.Strategy;
using TQGA.Domain.Indicators;
using TQGA.Domain.Trading;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.Strategies;

public sealed class RegimeGatedAltcoinLeadershipPullbackSignal : ISignal
{
    private readonly Ema _ema21 = new(21);
    private readonly Ema _ema50 = new(50);
    private readonly Ema _ema200 = new(200);
    private readonly Rsi _rsi14 = new(14);

    private readonly Queue _recentCloses = new();

    private const int MaxRecent = 80;

    private decimal _lastPrice;
    private decimal _previousPrice;
    private bool _isPrimedForLongReentry;

    public TradeSignal Evaluate(StrategyContext context)
    {
        decimal price = context.Price;

        _previousPrice = _lastPrice;
        _lastPrice = price;

        _ema21.Add(price);
        _ema50.Add(price);
        _ema200.Add(price);
        _rsi14.Update(price);

        PushPrice(price);

        if (_recentCloses.Count < 60)
            return TradeSignal.None;

        if (!_ema21.IsReady || !_ema50.IsReady || !_ema200.IsReady || !_rsi14.IsReady)
            return TradeSignal.None;

        decimal ema21 = _ema21.Value;
        decimal ema50 = _ema50.Value;
        decimal ema200 = _ema200.Value;
        decimal rsi = _rsi14.Value;

        bool trendAligned =
            price > ema200 &&
            ema21 > ema50 &&
            ema50 > ema200;

        bool slopeStrong =
            ema21 > AverageRecent(10) &&
            ema50 > AverageRecent(20);

        decimal extensionPctFromEma21 = PercentDistance(price, ema21);
        decimal extensionPctFromEma50 = PercentDistance(price, ema50);

        bool tooExtended =
            extensionPctFromEma21 > 8.50m ||
            extensionPctFromEma50 > 18.00m;

        if (context.HasOpenPosition)
        {
            if (ShouldExitLong(price, ema21, ema50, rsi))
            {
                _isPrimedForLongReentry = false;
                return TradeSignal.Exit;
            }

            return TradeSignal.None;
        }

        if (!trendAligned || !slopeStrong || tooExtended)
        {
            _isPrimedForLongReentry = false;
            return TradeSignal.None;
        }

        bool controlledPullback =
            price >= ema50 * 0.985m &&
            price <= ema21 * 1.015m;

        bool pullbackDepthAcceptable =
            extensionPctFromEma21 <= 3.75m &&
            price >= ema50 * 0.9925m;

        bool momentumStillHealthy =
            rsi >= 48m && rsi <= 68m;

        bool pullbackStructureHealthy =
            MinRecent(6) >= ema50 * 0.985m &&
            CountClosesBelow(ema50, 6) <= 2;

        if (controlledPullback && pullbackDepthAcceptable && momentumStillHealthy && pullbackStructureHealthy)
        {
            _isPrimedForLongReentry = true;
            return TradeSignal.None;
        }

        bool bullishResumption =
            _isPrimedForLongReentry &&
            _previousPrice > 0m &&
            price > _previousPrice &&
            price > ema21 &&
            price > AverageRecent(3) &&
            PercentDistance(price, _previousPrice) >= 0.20m;

        bool notLateChase =
            PercentDistance(price, ema21) <= 2.25m;

        bool localStrengthRecovered =
            price >= HighestRecent(5) * 0.995m;

        if (bullishResumption && notLateChase && localStrengthRecovered)
        {
            _isPrimedForLongReentry = false;
            return TradeSignal.Long;
        }

        return TradeSignal.None;
    }

    private bool ShouldExitLong(decimal price, decimal ema21, decimal ema50, decimal rsi)
    {
        bool lostFastTrend = price < ema21 * 0.9925m;
        bool lostMediumTrend = price < ema50 * 0.9975m;
        bool momentumFailure = rsi < 43m;
        bool sharpReversal = _previousPrice > 0m && PercentDistance(_previousPrice, price) >= 3.00m;

        return lostMediumTrend || (lostFastTrend && momentumFailure) || sharpReversal;
    }

    private void PushPrice(decimal price)
    {
        _recentCloses.Enqueue(price);

        while (_recentCloses.Count > MaxRecent)
            _recentCloses.Dequeue();
    }

    private decimal AverageRecent(int n)
    {
        if (_recentCloses.Count == 0)
            return 0m;

        return _recentCloses.TakeLast(System.Math.Max(1, n)).Average();
    }

    private decimal HighestRecent(int n)
    {
        if (_recentCloses.Count == 0)
            return 0m;

        return _recentCloses.TakeLast(System.Math.Max(1, n)).Max();
    }

    private decimal MinRecent(int n)
    {
        if (_recentCloses.Count == 0)
            return 0m;

        return _recentCloses.TakeLast(System.Math.Max(1, n)).Min();
    }

    private int CountClosesBelow(decimal level, int n)
    {
        if (_recentCloses.Count == 0)
            return 0;

        return _recentCloses
            .TakeLast(System.Math.Max(1, n))
            .Count(x => x < level);
    }

    private static decimal PercentDistance(decimal a, decimal b)
    {
        if (b == 0m)
            return 0m;

        return System.Math.Abs((a - b) / b) * 100m;
    }
}

 F I L E :   D : \ D   D A T A   B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . I n f r a s t r u c t u r e \ S t r a t e g i e s \ R s i R e v e r s i o n S i g n a l . c s

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using TQGA.Application.Strategy;
using TQGA.Domain.Indicators;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.Strategies;

public sealed class RsiReversionSignal : ISignal
{
    private readonly Rsi _rsi = new(14);

    public TradeSignal Evaluate(StrategyContext context)
    {
        _rsi.Update(context.Price);

        if (!_rsi.IsReady)
            return TradeSignal.None;

        // ENTRY → pullback in uptrend
        if (!context.HasOpenPosition && _rsi.Value <= 45m)
            return TradeSignal.Long;

        // EXIT → momentum exhaustion
        if (context.HasOpenPosition && _rsi.Value >= 60m)
            return TradeSignal.Exit;

        return TradeSignal.None;
    }
}

 using TQGA.Application.Strategy;
using TQGA.Domain.Indicators;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.Strategies;

public sealed class RsiSwingSignal : ISignal
{
    private readonly Ema _fast = new(50);
    private readonly Ema _slow = new(200);
    private readonly Rsi _rsi = new(14);

    public TradeSignal Evaluate(StrategyContext context)
    {
        _fast.Add(context.Price);
        _slow.Add(context.Price);
        _rsi.Update(context.Price);

        if (!_fast.IsReady || !_slow.IsReady || !_rsi.IsReady)
            return TradeSignal.None;

        bool bullishTrend = _fast.Value > _slow.Value;

        if (!context.HasOpenPosition && bullishTrend && _rsi.Value >= 38m && _rsi.Value <= 48m)
            return TradeSignal.Long;

        if (context.HasOpenPosition)
        {
            bool trendBroken = !bullishTrend;
            bool reboundComplete = _rsi.Value >= 60m;

            if (trendBroken || reboundComplete)
                return TradeSignal.Exit;
        }

        return TradeSignal.None;
    }
}

 namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.Strategies;

public sealed class SignalFireStats
{
    public int TotalCandles { get; private set; }

    public int EmaLong { get; private set; }
    public int EmaShort { get; private set; }

    public int RsiLong { get; private set; }
    public int RsiExit { get; private set; }

    public int FullLongAlignment { get; private set; }
    public int FullShortAlignment { get; private set; }

    public void NextCandle() => TotalCandles++;

    public void CountEmaLong() => EmaLong++;
    public void CountEmaShort() => EmaShort++;

    public void CountRsiLong() => RsiLong++;
    public void CountRsiExit() => RsiExit++;

    public void CountFullLong() => FullLongAlignment++;
    public void CountFullShort() => FullShortAlignment++;

    public void Print()
    {
        Console.WriteLine("\n========== SIGNAL DIAGNOSTICS ==========");
        Console.WriteLine($"Candles processed        : {TotalCandles}");
        Console.WriteLine($"EMA Long fires           : {EmaLong}");
        Console.WriteLine($"EMA Short fires          : {EmaShort}");
        Console.WriteLine($"RSI Long fires           : {RsiLong}");
        Console.WriteLine($"RSI Exit fires           : {RsiExit}");
        Console.WriteLine($"FULL LONG ALIGNMENTS     : {FullLongAlignment}");
        Console.WriteLine($"FULL SHORT ALIGNMENTS    : {FullShortAlignment}");
        Console.WriteLine("========================================\n");
    }
}

 using TQGA.Application.Strategy;
using TQGA.Domain.Indicators;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.Strategies;

/// 
/// Trend-pullback signal:
/// - only looks for long entries when the fast EMA is above the slow EMA
/// - uses RSI pullback for better entry location
/// - exits when momentum becomes stretched or trend weakens
/// This is intentionally aligned with the current TQGA trend-heavy edge profile.
/// 
public sealed class TrendPullbackSignal : ISignal
{
    private readonly Ema _fast = new(50);
    private readonly Ema _slow = new(200);
    private readonly Rsi _rsi = new(14);

    public TradeSignal Evaluate(StrategyContext context)
    {
        _fast.Add(context.Price);
        _slow.Add(context.Price);
        _rsi.Update(context.Price);

        if (!_fast.IsReady || !_slow.IsReady || !_rsi.IsReady)
            return TradeSignal.None;

        var bullishTrend = _fast.Value > _slow.Value;

        if (!context.HasOpenPosition && bullishTrend && _rsi.Value <= 48m)
            return TradeSignal.Long;

        if (context.HasOpenPosition && (!bullishTrend || _rsi.Value >= 62m))
            return TradeSignal.Exit;

        return TradeSignal.None;
    }
}

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.Time;

public sealed class SimulatedClock : IClock
{
    public DateTime UtcNow { get; private set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;

    public void Advance(TimeSpan delta)
    {
        UtcNow = UtcNow.Add(delta);
    }
}

 using TQGA.Application.Trading;
using TQGA.Domain.Trading;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.Trading;

public sealed class BacktestOrderExecutor : IOrderExecutor
{
    private decimal _lastPrice;
    private decimal _lastFillPrice;

    public void UpdateMarketPrice(decimal price)
    {
        _lastPrice = price;
    }

    public Task PlaceMarketOrderAsync(
        string symbol,
        TradeSide side,
        decimal quantity,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        _lastFillPrice = _lastPrice;
        return Task.CompletedTask;
    }

    public Task ClosePositionAsync(string symbol, CancellationToken ct)
    {
        _lastFillPrice = _lastPrice;
        return Task.CompletedTask;
    }

    public decimal GetFillPrice() => _lastFillPrice;
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using TQGA.Application.Trading;
using TQGA.Domain.Trading;

namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.Trading;

public sealed class InMemoryPositionRepository : IPositionRepository
{
    private Position? _position;

    public bool HasOpenPosition()
        => _position != null;

    public decimal CurrentSize()
        => _position?.Quantity ?? 0m;

    public void Open(TradeSide side, decimal quantity, decimal price)
    {
        if (_position != null)
            return;

        var signedQty = side == TradeSide.Buy
            ? quantity
            : -quantity;

        _position = new Position(
            symbol: "DEFAULT",
            quantity: signedQty,
            entryPrice: price
        );
    }

    public void Close(decimal price)
    {
        if (_position == null)
            return;

        _position = null;
    }
}

        _btnCatNone = new Button { Text = "Cat None", Left = 990, Top = 285, Width = 100 };

    protected override void OnLoad(EventArgs e)
    {
        base.OnLoad(e);
        _structure.Generate();
        LoadStrategyList();
        LoadTimeframeList();
        LoadCoinCategories();
        RefreshCoinNames();
        MessageBox.Show("TQGA READY", "BOOT");
    }

    private void LoadStrategyList()
    {
        if (_strategyList == null)
            return;

        _strategyList.Items.Clear();

        using var scope = _sp.CreateScope();
        var orchestrator = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService();

        foreach (Type t in orchestrator.GetRegisteredStrategies())
            _strategyList.Items.Add(new StrategyListItem(t), true);
    }

    private void LoadTimeframeList()
    {
        if (_timeframeList == null)
            return;

        _timeframeList.Items.Clear();

        foreach (string tf in AppBinanceUniverse.Timeframes)
            _timeframeList.Items.Add(tf, true);
    }

    private void LoadCoinCategories()
    {
        if (_coinCategoryList == null)
            return;

        _coinCategoryList.Items.Clear();

        foreach (string key in CoinCategories.Keys)
            _coinCategoryList.Items.Add(key, true);
    }

    private void RefreshCoinNames()
    {
        if (_coinNameList == null || _coinCategoryList == null)
            return;

        List selectedCategories = _coinCategoryList.CheckedItems
            .OfType()
            .ToList();

        List selectedSymbols = selectedCategories.Count == 0
            ? AppBinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols.ToList()
            : selectedCategories
                .Where(CoinCategories.ContainsKey)
                .SelectMany(x => CoinCategories[x])
                .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                .Where(x => AppBinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols.Contains(x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                .OrderBy(x => x)
                .ToList();

        _coinNameList.Items.Clear();

        foreach (string s in selectedSymbols)
            _coinNameList.Items.Add(s, true);
    }

    private static void SetAllChecked(CheckedListBox? list, bool isChecked)
    {
        if (list == null)
            return;

        for (int i = 0; i < list.Items.Count; i++)
            list.SetItemChecked(i, isChecked);
    }

    private async Task RunResearch()
    {
        using var scope = _sp.CreateScope();
        var orchestrator = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService();

        IReadOnlyList selectedStrategies = GetSelectedStrategyTypes(orchestrator);
        IReadOnlyList selectedTimeframes = GetSelectedTimeframes();
        IReadOnlyList selectedSymbols = GetSelectedSymbols();
        FrictionProfile friction = FrictionProfile.Default;

        await RunSafe(() => orchestrator.RunSelectedAsync(
            selectedStrategies,
            selectedSymbols,
            selectedTimeframes,
            friction,
            CancellationToken.None));
    }

    private async Task PublishPortalAsync()
    {
        Toggle(false);

        try
        {
            var result = await Task.Run(() => _portalPublish.PublishLatestReports());

            MessageBox.Show(
                $"Portal generated successfully.\n\n" +
                $"Reports: {result.ReportCount}\n" +
                $"Report Source: {result.ReportDirectory}\n" +
                $"Site: {result.SiteDirectory}\n" +
                $"Local Web URL: {result.LocalWebUrl}",
                "PUBLISHED",
                MessageBoxButtons.OK,
                MessageBoxIcon.Information);
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            MessageBox.Show(
                $"Publish failed.\n\n{ex.Message}",
                "PUBLISHED ERROR",
                MessageBoxButtons.OK,
                MessageBoxIcon.Error);
        }
        finally
        {
            Toggle(true);
        }
    }

    private async Task BuildReportAll31WithMessageAsync()
    {
        Toggle(false);

        try
        {
            string report31Path = await BuildReportAll31Async(copyToClipboard: true);
            string report31HtmlPath = Path.ChangeExtension(report31Path, ".html");

            MessageBox.Show(
                $"REPORT ALL 31 generated successfully.\n\n" +
                $"TXT File: {report31Path}\n" +
                $"HTML File: {report31HtmlPath}\n\n" +
                $"The formatted audit report has also been copied to clipboard.",
                "REPORT ALL 31",
                MessageBoxButtons.OK,
                MessageBoxIcon.Information);
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            MessageBox.Show(
                $"REPORT ALL 31 generation failed.\n\n{ex.Message}",
                "REPORT ALL 31 ERROR",
                MessageBoxButtons.OK,
                MessageBoxIcon.Error);
        }
        finally
        {
            Toggle(true);
        }
    }

    private async Task GitPublishedAsync()
    {
        Toggle(false);

        try
        {
            string report31Path = await BuildReportAll31Async(copyToClipboard: false);
            string formattedText = await File.ReadAllTextAsync(report31Path);

            string repoRootPath = ResolveGitRepoPath();

            var publishResult = await Task.Run(() =>
                _gitHubPagesPublish.PublishReportAll31(
                    report31Path,
                    formattedText,
                    repoRootPath));

            MessageBox.Show(
                $"GIT publish completed successfully.\n\n" +
                $"Local Repo: {publishResult.RepoRootPath}\n" +
                $"Latest Raw Text: {publishResult.PublishedLatestTextPath}\n" +
                $"Website Page File: {publishResult.PublishedIndexHtmlPath}\n" +
                $"Archive File (Local Only): {publishResult.PublishedArchiveReportPath}\n" +
                $"Reports Index File: {publishResult.PublishedReportsIndexPath}\n\n" +
                $"Public Site: {publishResult.PublicUrl}\n" +
                $"Public Latest TXT: {publishResult.PublicLatestTextUrl}\n" +
                $"Public Reports Index: {publishResult.PublicReportsIndexUrl}",
                "GIT PUBLISHED",
                MessageBoxButtons.OK,
                MessageBoxIcon.Information);
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            MessageBox.Show(
                $"GIT publish failed.\n\n{ex.Message}",
                "GIT PUBLISHED ERROR",
                MessageBoxButtons.OK,
                MessageBoxIcon.Error);
        }
        finally
        {
            Toggle(true);
        }
    }

    private string ResolveTqgaSolutionRoot()
    {
        string? current = AppContext.BaseDirectory;

        while (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(current))
        {
            string slnPath = Path.Combine(current, "TQGA.sln");
            if (File.Exists(slnPath))
                return current;

            DirectoryInfo? parent = Directory.GetParent(current);
            if (parent == null)
                break;

            current = parent.FullName;
        }

        current = Directory.GetCurrentDirectory();

        while (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(current))
        {
            string slnPath = Path.Combine(current, "TQGA.sln");
            if (File.Exists(slnPath))
                return current;

            DirectoryInfo? parent = Directory.GetParent(current);
            if (parent == null)
                break;

            current = parent.FullName;
        }

        throw new InvalidOperationException(
            "Could not locate TQGA.sln from the running application path. " +
            "Please run the WinForms app from within the TQGA solution structure.");
    }

    private string ResolveGitRepoPath()
    {
        if (Directory.Exists(FixedGitHubPagesRepoPath))
        {
            _gitHubPagesPublish.SaveRepoPath(FixedGitHubPagesRepoPath);
            return FixedGitHubPagesRepoPath;
        }

        string? saved = _gitHubPagesPublish.TryLoadSavedRepoPath();
        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(saved) && Directory.Exists(saved))
            return saved;

        throw new DirectoryNotFoundException(
            $"GitHub Pages local repository folder was not found.\nExpected:\n{FixedGitHubPagesRepoPath}");
    }

    private async Task BuildReportAll31Async(bool copyToClipboard)
    {
        string combinedPath = await Task.Run(() => _fullReport.SaveCombinedToFile());

        string rawText = await File.ReadAllTextAsync(combinedPath);
        string formattedText = FormatAuditReportAll31(rawText);

        string directory = Path.GetDirectoryName(combinedPath) ?? AppContext.BaseDirectory;
        string report31Path = Path.Combine(
            directory,
            $"REPORT_ALL_31_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        await File.WriteAllTextAsync(report31Path, formattedText);

        string report31HtmlPath = Path.ChangeExtension(report31Path, ".html");
        string htmlWrapped = WrapTextAsHtml(formattedText);
        await File.WriteAllTextAsync(report31HtmlPath, htmlWrapped);

        if (copyToClipboard)
            Clipboard.SetText(formattedText);

        return report31Path;
    }

    private static string FormatAuditReportAll31(string input)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(input))
            return string.Empty;

        string normalized = input
            .Replace("\r\n", "\n")
            .Replace("\r", "\n");

        string[] lines = normalized.Split('\n');

        var output = new List(lines.Length + 200);
        bool previousBlank = false;
        int blankCount = 0;

        output.Add("TQGA REPORT ALL 31");
        output.Add("============================================================");
        output.Add($"Generated (UTC): {DateTime.UtcNow:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        output.Add("Formatting: Wrapped / normalized / audit-friendly separation");
        output.Add(string.Empty);

        foreach (string rawLine in lines)
        {
            string line = rawLine?.TrimEnd() ?? string.Empty;
            string upper = line.Trim().ToUpperInvariant();

            bool isMajorHeader =
                upper.StartsWith("REPORT ") ||
                upper.StartsWith("A84") ||
                upper.StartsWith("WF ") ||
                upper.StartsWith("WF_") ||
                upper.StartsWith("WALK FORWARD") ||
                upper.StartsWith("FULL REPORT") ||
                upper.StartsWith("TQGA ");

            if (isMajorHeader && output.Count > 0 && output[^1] != string.Empty)
                output.Add(string.Empty);

            if (isMajorHeader)
            {
                output.Add("------------------------------------------------------------");
                output.Add(line);
                output.Add("------------------------------------------------------------");
                previousBlank = false;
                blankCount = 0;
                continue;
            }

            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(line))
            {
                if (!previousBlank || blankCount < 2)
                {
                    output.Add(string.Empty);
                    blankCount++;
                }

                previousBlank = true;
                continue;
            }

            previousBlank = false;
            blankCount = 0;

            output.Add(WrapLine(line, 140));
        }

        return string.Join(Environment.NewLine, output);
    }

    private static string WrapTextAsHtml(string text)
    {
        string encoded = HtmlEncode(text);

        return
$@"


  
  Test Page






{encoded}






";
    }

    private static string HtmlEncode(string text)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(text))
            return string.Empty;

        return text
            .Replace("&", "&")
            .Replace("<", "<")
            .Replace(">", ">");
    }

    private static string WrapLine(string text, int maxWidth)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(text) || text.Length <= maxWidth)
            return text;

        string[] parts = text.Split(' ', StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);
        var lines = new List();
        var current = new System.Text.StringBuilder();

        foreach (string part in parts)
        {
            if (current.Length == 0)
            {
                current.Append(part);
                continue;
            }

            if (current.Length + 1 + part.Length <= maxWidth)
            {
                current.Append(' ');
                current.Append(part);
                continue;
            }

            lines.Add(current.ToString());
            current.Clear();
            current.Append(part);
        }

        if (current.Length > 0)
            lines.Add(current.ToString());

        return string.Join(Environment.NewLine, lines);
    }

    private IReadOnlyList GetSelectedStrategyTypes(PortfolioBacktestOrchestrator orchestrator)
    {
        if (_strategyList == null || _strategyList.Items.Count == 0)
            return orchestrator.GetRegisteredStrategies();

        List checkedItems = _strategyList.CheckedItems
            .OfType()
            .Select(x => x.Type)
            .ToList();

        return checkedItems.Count == 0
            ? orchestrator.GetRegisteredStrategies()
            : checkedItems;
    }

    private IReadOnlyList GetSelectedTimeframes()
    {
        if (_timeframeList == null || _timeframeList.Items.Count == 0)
            return AppBinanceUniverse.Timeframes;

        List checkedItems = _timeframeList.CheckedItems
            .OfType()
            .ToList();

        return checkedItems.Count == 0
            ? AppBinanceUniverse.Timeframes
            : checkedItems;
    }

    private IReadOnlyList GetSelectedSymbols()
    {
        if (_coinNameList == null || _coinNameList.Items.Count == 0)
            return AppBinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols;

        List checkedItems = _coinNameList.CheckedItems
            .OfType()
            .ToList();

        return checkedItems.Count == 0
            ? AppBinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols
            : checkedItems;
    }

    private async Task RunSafe(Func action)
    {
        Toggle(false);

        try
        {
            await Task.Run(action);
            MessageBox.Show("DONE");
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            MessageBox.Show(ex.Message);
        }

        Toggle(true);
    }

    private void Toggle(bool enabled)
    {
        if (_btnDownload != null) _btnDownload.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnUpdate != null) _btnUpdate.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnRunResearch != null) _btnRunResearch.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnFullReportSave != null) _btnFullReportSave.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnFullReportClipboard != null) _btnFullReportClipboard.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnPublished != null) _btnPublished.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnReportAll31 != null) _btnReportAll31.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnGitPublished != null) _btnGitPublished.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnCodesFile != null) _btnCodesFile.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnGitHubPublished != null) _btnGitHubPublished.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnGitHubReportsPublished != null) _btnGitHubReportsPublished.Enabled = enabled;

        if (_strategyList != null) _strategyList.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_timeframeList != null) _timeframeList.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_coinCategoryList != null) _coinCategoryList.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_coinNameList != null) _coinNameList.Enabled = enabled;

        if (_btnSelectAll != null) _btnSelectAll.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnSelectNone != null) _btnSelectNone.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnTfAll != null) _btnTfAll.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnTfNone != null) _btnTfNone.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnCatAll != null) _btnCatAll.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnCatNone != null) _btnCatNone.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnCoinAll != null) _btnCoinAll.Enabled = enabled;
        if (_btnCoinNone != null) _btnCoinNone.Enabled = enabled;
    }

    private sealed record StrategyListItem(Type Type)
    {
        public override string ToString() => Type.Name;
    }
}

 using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Portfolio;
using TQGA.Application.Reporting;
using TQGA.Application.Services;
using TQGA.Application.Strategy;
using TQGA.Infrastructure;
using TQGA.Infrastructure.MarketData;

namespace TQGA.WinForms;

internal static class Program
{
    [STAThread]
    private static void Main()
    {
        var host = Host.CreateDefaultBuilder()
            .ConfigureServices((context, services) =>
            {
                services.AddInfrastructure();

                services.AddSingleton();

                services.AddScoped();
                services.AddScoped();
                services.AddScoped();

                services.AddScoped();
                services.AddScoped();
                services.AddScoped();
                services.AddScoped();

                // Shared helper services
                services.AddScoped();

                // Report / analytics services required by PortfolioBacktestOrchestrator
                services.AddScoped();
                services.AddScoped();
                services.AddScoped();
                services.AddScoped();
                services.AddScoped();
                services.AddScoped();

                // Other application services
                services.AddScoped();
                services.AddScoped();

                services.AddSingleton();
                services.AddSingleton();

                services.AddScoped();
            })
            .Build();

        ApplicationConfiguration.Initialize();

        using var scope = host.Services.CreateScope();
        var mainForm = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService();

        System.Windows.Forms.Application.Run(mainForm);
    }
}

CURRENT DATA / EXECUTION NOTES
------------------------------
- ICandleDataFeed still exposes GetCandles(symbol, timeframe) only.
- Trade domain model already supports Quantity.
- BacktestOrderExecutor already accepts quantity in market order placement.
- Current TradingEngine still behaves as a single-open-trade engine per strategy instance.
- Therefore the safest institutional upgrade path is to apply risk budgeting at the portfolio/backtest layer first.

CURRENT RISK BUDGET ENGINE
--------------------------
PortfolioRiskBudgetEngine now decides how much to trust each selected market opportunity.

Current dimensions:
- ATR sizing
- regime multiplier
- 4h preference bonus
- per-symbol cap
- per-cluster cap
- total portfolio risk cap
- drawdown-based throttling
- hard position value cap

Purpose:
- reduce concentration blowups
- smooth fold dispersion
- lower over-allocation to unstable markets
- improve realism before deeper TradingEngine surgery

CURRENT RESEARCH STATUS
-----------------------
The platform currently supports:
- Strategy backtesting
- Symbol PnL attribution
- Symbol x Timeframe PnL attribution
- Strategy x Symbol x Timeframe attribution

- Strategy fitness gating
- Alpha decay monitoring
- Regime classification reports
- Executive compact ChatGPT upload summary
- Pre-trade market selection
- Symbol/category constrained backtest runs
- True rule-based walk-forward rerun reporting
- Risk-budgeted opportunity scaling

KEY CURRENT INSIGHT
-------------------
Strongest edge profile remains:
- 4h
- leadership markets
- pullback inside trend
- expansion / high-vol regime

CURRENT LIMITATION
------------------
Risk budgeting currently scales trust at the portfolio/backtest layer.
Full trade-by-trade portfolio budgeting inside TradingEngine remains a later upgrade.
